Chapter 602: I Am the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor You Speak Of

Jiang Lianyi shared, “I do have a bit of a problem regarding cultivation. I’ve been stuck at a cultivation realm for quite some time, still unable to break through.”

Seventh Elder nodded. “So you’ve encountered a bottleneck. That’s common. I have pills that can help you break through it.”

“It’s not a bottleneck. It’s that someone is ahead of me, so I can’t break through.”

A look of understanding flashed across Seventh Elder’s visage. It seems the new member is cultivating a special technique.

These special cultivation techniques were ubiquitous in the Great Qian and Great Yu eras. Their main characteristic was that cultivators ahead in the cultivation technique would absorb the cultivators who cultivated it later—the winner took all. By the Great Xia era, due to the cruelty of such cultivation techniques and the availability of other methods, cultivators no longer practiced them.

“What about changing sects and cultivating anew?” Seventh Elder suggested.

“That probably won’t work. If I start over, I can’t guarantee I’ll reach my current cultivation realm again.”

“I see. If all fails, just tell me who’s ahead of you. I’ll make them cultivate anew!”

Jiang Lianyi sounded somewhat worried. “But that person is very strong.” freewebnovel.com

“Are they at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage?”

“They’re not.”

Hearing it wasn’t the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, Seventh Elder was relieved. He patted his chest and assured, “As long as it’s not the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, I can beat them easily.”

Which of the Dao-Seeking Nine isn’t renowned for combat prowess?

“This isn’t the place to talk. Let’s continue inside the city,” First Elder reminded the group. Discussing such matters at the city gate isn’t appropriate. Even using muting spells isn’t foolproof; what if a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator passes by and overhears?

The Demon Alliance’s preparations were ample. They had arranged accommodations for every faction. A major sect like the Dao-Seeking Sect was allocated an entire floor of an inn.

~~~

Inside the Demon City, it was even more bustling with multifarious cultivators. Apart from local cultivators of the Demon Region, there were seafolks from the East Sea with fish-like traits, monks with gleaming bald heads and plain robes from the Golden Buddhist Kingdom, and rogue cultivators with thick hair from the Extreme North...

Jiang Lianyi’s gaze lingered on the Buddhist Kingdom’s monks for a moment. Lu Yang suddenly remembered that the Buddhist sects were fabricated by the Five Ancient Immortals and that no Buddhist cultivators existed in ancient times. He transmitted an auditory message to Jiang Lianyi, explaining the current state of Buddhism. His own understanding was limited, so he could only provide a general overview.

Jian Lianyi was slightly surprised. “So that’s how it is. I never imagined the story we made up then would become so widespread in the cultivation world.” She had been present when the Four Ancient Immortals fabricated the story, occasionally chiming in. By that count, I could be considered a founder of Buddhism as well.

Lu Yang shrugged. “After all, so much time has passed. The stories from antiquity have become legends. It’s hard to distinguish what is true and false.”

Oh, I can’t exactly call them false. They’ve simply undergone a series of artistic embellishments and selective narrations.

By the time they arrived at the inn, Seventh Elder was still boasting. After all, it was rare to encounter a new member of the Heavenly Court Creed. This time, I’m determined to indulge in my desire to act as a commendable teacher and role model. “I’m not boasting, but my pill-concocting skills are number one in the current cultivation world. If you have any requests regarding pills, feel free to look for me.”

Fifth Elder was unwilling to let Seventh Elder steal the spotlight. “My artifact-refining skills are peerless, and it’s no exaggeration to say they’re number one in the cultivation world. Considering you’re a new member of our creed, if you lack a magical treasure, I’ll forge one for you!”

The corner of Jiang Lianyi’s lips curved into a smile. Fifth Elder’s words reminded her of an old friend. “An artifact-refining master? What a coincidence. I also know someone who claims to be the number one in the cultivation world.”

Fifth Elder raised an eyebrow. “So arrogant? When I meet him someday, I’ll show him who the true number one artifact-refiner is.

“By the way, I haven’t gotten the chance to ask, what’s your name?”

“Jiang Lianyi.”

“The name sounds familiar.” Third Elder scratched his head.

As a Confucian cultivator, Fourth Elder was erudite and knowledgeable. “It’s the same name as the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor.”

As an old-timer in the Heavenly Court Creed, Seventh Elder pretended to be knowledgeable and experienced as he praised, “That’s a pretty good name. According to the fortune theory, having the same name as the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor allows you to partake in her fortune. It will greatly aid your cultivation. Breaking through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage in the future is possible.”

Jiang Lianyi hesitated for a moment. Recalling how her Everlasting-jiejie and her Senior Brother Lu Yang had both earnestly promised that the Dao-Seeking Sect members were utterly trustworthy, she removed her hood, revealing her stunningly beautiful appearance.

“The Phoenix Ancient Ancestor!!!” First Elder’s eyes widened. He shuddered and was unable to control his voice, involuntarily crying out as he staggered three steps backward.

He had sneaked into the Phoenix Tribe to visit their ancient tombs in his youth and had seen statues of the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor. It was thanks to the First Elder’s guidance and the maps he bestowed that Gan Tian was able to navigate the ancient tombs of the various tribes with ease.

Seventh Elder turned to look at First Elder with displeasure. “Of course, I know she has the same name as the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor.”

“She is the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor! I’ve seen her statue in the Phoenix Tribe!”

Seventh Elder broke out in laughter, not buying it. “Big Bro, you’re really humorous...”

Then, his eyes rolled back, and he fell to the ground with a thud, passing out.

What did I say just now? I said that the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor should come to me for cultivation problems?

A few seconds later, Seventh Elder woke up, his face still filled with disbelief. He suspected he was dreaming and even slapped himself twice.

“Are you the Ancient Phoenix Ancestor’s reincarnation cultivating anew?” First Elder asked cautiously, not daring to breathe heavily.

Li Haoran’s existence had introduced him to the concept of reincarnation.

“I’ve not heard of any reincarnation cultivating anew. I am the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor you speak of. I have been slumbering in a secret domain until a few days ago, when Senior Brother Lu Yang awakened me. I underwent nirvana rebirth and returned to the world.”

First Elder sucked in a cold breath of air. This is the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor! A mythical figure! Where did Lu Yang dig up this big shot from?

And he even managed to hoodwink her into joining the Heavenly Court Creed.

You’re far more impressive than your shifu. Old Nine goes out every day scamming people, yet his deception skills aren’t as high as yours.

I’ll get Old Nine to take you as his shifu later.

“Wait, what did you call Lu Yang?”

Lu Yang hastily interposed himself between them to put an end to this topic. “Nothing, nothing. Senior Lianyi misspoke.”

Seventh Elder trembled as he looked at Jiang Lianyi. So what you said about meeting a bottleneck earlier was referring to a half-immortal bottleneck? “You mentioned someone is ahead of you, preventing your breakthrough. Who is that?”

“The Qilin Immortal. According to current terminologies, he’s perhaps known as the Demon Immortal.”

Seventh Elder, “...”

Did I just say that so long as it’s not the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, I can beat them easily?

Fifth Elder’s condition was hardly any better than Seventh Elder’s. I had also made quite a few bold statements earlier. “You also mentioned earlier that you know someone who claims to be the number one artifact-refiner. Who is that?”

“The Heaven Mandate Immortal.”

Fifth Elder nearly fainted on the spot.

Third Elder and Fourth Elder remained silent. Fortunately, we hadn’t spoken earlier.

“Then what is your position in the Heavenly Court?”

“One of the Heavenly Court’s Four Regents[1]—the Extreme South Nirvana Great Emperor.”

The five elders collectively sucked in a cold breath. They had intended to broaden their horizons by attending the Demon Kingdom’s founding ceremony, but they hadn’t expected their horizons to be broadened this soon.

1. ”Siyu” refers to the Four Heavenly Ministers/Four Sovereigns of the Great Jade Emperor. The Great Jade Emperor is one of the Four Heavenly Emperors. Above the Four Heavenly Ministers are the three supreme beings, known as the “Sanqing.” ☜

Chapter 603: The Purpose of Becoming Strong

The Extreme South Nirvana Great Emperor was the collective brainchild of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and the two members of her sect.

“Extreme South” was the prefix proposed by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy; “Nirvana” was the characteristic suggested by Lu Yang; Jiang Lianyi adopted the honorific title of “Great Emperor” upon considering that the ancient Dijiang dared to call himself the “Demon Monarch” and that her title couldn’t be weaker than his.

Before setting out, the five elders had intended to see the legendary ancient Dijiang in person. This was a living ancient half-immortal, a bona fide prominent figure. The kingdom-founding ceremony was still a few days away, and they were merely picking up Lu Yang on the way to let him broaden his horizons in the Demon City.

How did the situation reverse in the blink of an eye?

And why did the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor join the Heavenly Court, even becoming one of the Four Regents? Could it be that the Heavenly Court wasn’t fabricated and that it truly existed in ancient times? Our Heavenly Court Creed is genuinely an ancient organization?

Even though the five elders had roamed the world and witnessed many immortal traces, encountering a half-immortal powerhouse was a first for them, especially at such close range.

Jiang Lianyi raised her hand, gesturing to the five elders not to be so nervous. “The Heavenly Court Creed still requires the support of you seniors to continue its existence.”

“We dare not accept such praise; you flatter us.” Before learning her identity, they could play at being seniors. But now that they learned Jiang Lianyi’s identity, who would dare act like a senior before such a mighty personage?

Inside the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was so amused by this scene that she rolled on the ground. “Yes yes yes! Exactly this kind of reaction! It was precisely for this that Lianyi, Little Ling, and I hid our identities to go to auctions and similar places back then!”

Lu Yang, “...”

While Jiang Lianyi spoke with the five elders, the kind-hearted Lu Yang had repeatedly tried to introduce her identity, but the Everlasting Immortal Fairy thwarted all his attempts.

So this was the reason.

Senior Lianyi is truly worthy of being your unofficial disciple. Despite losing this part of her memory, she can still elicit such reactions from the elders. Is it innate talent or muscle memory?

With a “heave-ho,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy sprang up from the ground in a carp flip. She brushed the dirt off her and earnestly instructed the second-in-command, guiding his cultivation. “Saw that? This is the purpose of becoming strong.”

Listening to the immortal’s teachings, Lu Yang turned pensive. It seems my mental state is still lacking. Even now, I can be easily swayed by an immortal’s bewitching words, believing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy can say something profoundly philosophical.

Having finally encountered a puissant figure from ancient times, Third Elder had a question. He had been studying hard recently to enhance his refinement, lest he make a fool of himself outside. “I’ve been reading lately, and the books say the Heaven Mandate Immortal had a fondness for married women, impregnating countless women. Is this true?”

Jiang Lianyi, “...”

How did such a rumor spread? Aren’t they afraid of encountering danger during their tribulations?

Putting aside other things, how could the offspring of immortals be so easily conceived? If it were that easy, I would have been pregnant with my husband’s child a long time ago.

Jiang Lianyi shook her head gently, denying this claim. “The Heaven Mandate Immortal did not have a fondness for married women.“

Third Elder presented another question. ”I also heard that the Nine Netherworlds had already existed in ancient times, governing life, death, and reincarnation, determining the lifespans of all living beings?” This was the latest doctrine promoted after the Nine-Netherworlds Creed joined hands with the Heavenly Court Creed.

“It’s false. There was no concept of the Nine Netherworlds or reincarnation in ancient times. A person’s death was like a lamp extinguishing—there wouldn’t be a second lifetime.”

Third Elder asked yet again. “What about the Buddhist sects? The books also state that Buddhism existed in ancient times, with countless followers scattered across the universe. It was a top-tier great faction in the ancient era, and its enlightened Buddhas were equivalent to immortals.”

Jiang Lianyi continued shaking her head. “It’s false. Buddhism did exist in ancient times. The four immortals were all involved in Buddhist matters. It was a top-tier great faction, but not in the way you imagine.”

Third Elder posed another question. “I also heard that you and the Dragon Ancient Ancestor ignited a fierce battle that spanned days, with meteors filling the sky and stars obliterated; Transcendent Tribulation cultivators didn’t dare watch the battle up close. You even performed the nirvana rebirth technique and were reborn in the flames, with your phoenix cries resonating throughout the universe?”

“This one is true,” Jiang Lianyi declared with certainty, her expression serious. Then, she fell into deep thought, seemingly recalling that arduous battle. She sighed slowly, lamenting that one shouldn’t dwell on matters in the past.

The five elders were taken aback, sensing the weight of history in Jiang Lianyi’s sigh. It was a loneliness no one else could empathize with.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy explained to Lu Yang, “This is her having mastered a third of the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s essence.”

Jiang Lianyi emerged from her recollections and asked, “I have just awakened, so I am unaware of current matters in the cultivation world. There is something I need to consult you all about.”

“Please speak, Senior Jiang. As long as we know it, we’ll tell you everything.”

“Do you know where my husband, the Demon Immortal, might be found?”

The five elders shook their heads in unison. “We have to disappoint you, Senior Jiang. The Demon Immortal is an immensely mysterious existence. We have no idea of his possible whereabouts, much less clues about him... Wait, you called the Demon Immortal ‘husband?’”

The five elders stared at Jiang Lianyi as if they had seen a ghost. The Demon Immortal and the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor had that kind of relationship?

Is this the knowledge of ancient great demons? Just casually mentioning something can overturn our understanding.

Gan Tian’s reaction was calm. When she was piloting the beast side, Jiang Lianyi had already promised her regarding this matter. Upon learning of the two’s relationship, she nearly fell off the beast hide along with it.

Jiang Lianyi had only been trying her luck. It wasn’t surprising to not hear useful information. “It looks like I’ll have to inquire with the Dragon Tribe.”

This place gathered major forces, including the Demon Region’s Dragon Tribe and the East Sea’s Dragon Tribe.

“Nephew Meng, I heard you’re here?” Footsteps and a hearty laugh emitted from outside the door. It was the Qiongqi Tribe’s Chieftain Jin.

Chieftain Jin had instructed his subordinates to report to him immediately if they saw Meng Jingzhou in the Demon City. His subordinates lived up to expectations and spotted Meng Jingzhou on his way to the inn. With five Dao-Seeking Sect elders accompanying him, it was hard not to be conspicuous.

Upon hearing that Meng Jingzhou had arrived, Chieftain Jin came straight to the inn arranged for the Dao-Seeking Sect. The thought of the Qiongqi Tribe becoming rich excited Chieftain Jin.

Once he had a brief conversation with the Meng Family’s leader, the latter agreed readily. It’s definitely thanks to Meng Jingzhou putting in good words for us that our Qiongqi Tribe could borrow spirit stones.

Chieftain Jin acted with impetuous energy. Hearing Meng Jingzhou’s voice from a guest room in the middle of the corridor, he pushed open the door without a second thought and announced bluntly, “Nephew, it’s all thanks to you that our Qiongqi Tribe was able to borrow spirit stones!”

Then, he saw Jiang Lianyi in the middle of the room, her hood removed and looking exceedingly conspicuous.

The two made eye contact.

Chieftain Jin quietly retreated, exited the guest room, and closed the door.

With a hook of Jiang Lianyi’s finger, the door opened. Chieftain Jin was pulled into the room by an invisible force. He desperately resisted but to no avail.

Without another word, Chieftain Jin closed his eyes and raised his hands in surrender. “I know the rules! I didn’t see anything today; I don’t know anything! Please spare my life, Ancient Ancestor Jiang!”

Jiang Lianyi was silent for a moment. In my impression, qiongqi are all tough bones. Is the change over three hundred thousand years this big?

Meng Jingzhou was puzzled. He had been in the Demon Region since leaving the Qiongqi Tribe and hadn’t yet sent any message home.

Chapter 604: The Heaven Mandate Immortal was Truly the Qilin Immortal’s Good Brother

Ordinary demons might not recognize Jiang Lianyi, but how could Chieftain Jin, the leader of the Qiongqi Tribe, not recognize her?

The Demon Immortal’s appearance was unknown. Thus, the Dragon and Phoenix ancestors were the demon race’s strongest powerhouses and idols, commanding significant status among the demons.

The ancient Dijiang’s fame was resounding, but compared to these two, it still fell short. The Dragon and Phoenix ancestors had participated in the battle for immortality. Although they were defeated, they retained their honor. On the other hand, the ancient Dijiang hadn’t even qualified to participate in the battle for immortality. The gap was obvious.

If the Little Ancestor were here, Chieftain Jin definitely wouldn’t have begged for mercy. But the problem was that he had no one backing him now. The Little Ancestor wasn’t even interested in coming after hearing that the ancient Dijiang had proclaimed himself the monarch. What am I after by acting tough against an ancient great demon of Jiang Lianyi’s caliber—a quick death from her?

Moreover, the conflict between Jiang Lianyi and the Little Ancestor is related to the Qilin Immortal. It is an internal family conflict, or rather, a conflict between the wife and mistress. Why should I get involved?

The Qiongqi Tribe is so poor. As the chieftain, I have my own way of survival—be ruthless when I should be; be cowardly when I should be.

Chieftain Jin sighed inwardly. The Little Ancestor is right. This Battle of the Great Era is more complicated than we’d imagined. Even the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor has secretly been resurrected. Considering she has the Qilin Immortal behind her, what does our Qiongqi Tribe have to compete for first place?

Wait, why can’t we just pledge allegiance to the Qilin Immortal?

At this thought, Chieftain Jin’s mind suddenly cleared, and he felt a bright future was ahead.

Jiang Lianyi wasn’t aware of how much Chieftain Jin had thought in an instant. The mere sight of a qiongqi riled her. Initially, she had intended to pick a random qiongqi to vent her anger on, but it wouldn’t be enough to teach someone like Chieftain Jin a lesson. It would just be dull.

“Look into my eyes.” Jiang Lianyi’s words seemed to encompass a certain magic, making Chieftain Jin obey her involuntarily.

Chieftain Jin met Jiang Lianyi’s gaze. Suddenly, he transformed into his original form—a patterned winged tiger—and appeared in an unknown space, where a bright moon hung high overhead. He stood on a vast sea, isolated and helpless.

Jiang Lianyi’s voice echoed above him. “You must not mention to anyone about meeting me, whether explicitly or implicitly.”

By the time Chieftain Jin returned to his senses again, he found himself back in the guest room. Everything that had happened earlier felt like a dream.

“What did Senior Lianyi do?” Lu Yang secretly asked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. To outsiders, Chieftain Jin had spaced out for a moment before recovering quickly. Lu Yang guessed Jiang Lianyi had employed some method.

“This is the Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit. It can control what the defeated must say and cannot say. She just made this little tiger keep her matters a secret.” Normally, the defeated would need to have fought Jiang Lianyi first. But the disparity in cultivation between Chieftain Jin and Jiang Lianyi was too massive, so she could directly use the Incipient Dao Fruit to control him. “She used this feature frequently in the past.”

“Why?” Lu Yang was baffled.

It was troublesome to explain. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy tilted her head and thought for a moment. “Didn’t the Qilin Immortal often sneak out to seduce female demons? In the beginning, Lianyi would put on a stern face and bluff the Qilin Immortal, and he would confess everything like pouring beans from a sack.

“Later, the Heaven Mandate Immortal taught the Qilin Immortal that as an immortal, he needed a steady character—unruffled when handling affairs and unflustered when encountering problems. The Qilin Immortal managed to learn it. From then on, no matter how Lianyi bluffed him, he wouldn’t tell the truth, becoming as annoying as meat that refuses to be cut by a gear hob.[1]

“Lianyi couldn’t defeat the Qilin Immortal and was powerless about it. Thus, she would seek out the suspicious female demons, fight them, defeat them, and then use the Incipient Dao Fruit to make them tell the truth.

“After the truth was told, the Qilin Immortal would kneel on the sword array.”

Lu Yang, “...”

The Qilin Immortal and the Heaven Mandate Immortal were truly good brothers. The Heaven Mandate Immortal taught him the lies and refined the sword array for him.

“Hmm? Haven’t I told you? It was also the Heaven Mandate Immortal who told Lianyi and Little Ling about the fake sword array. The Qilin Immortal was kept in the dark, assuming Lianyi and Little Ling had discovered it by accident; he was full of remorse when the truth was exposed.”

Lu Yang felt the situation in ancient times was complex and intricate, for schemes and intrigue existed even among immortals.

“Senior Lianyi seems very certain that the Qilin Immortal is still alive?” Based on Lu Yang’s observation, Jiang Lianyi was always pondering how to find the Qilin Immortal throughout their journey, as if she was convinced he was still alive and hadn’t been harmed by the mastermind.

“I can see that too. Since she is sure that the Qilin Immortal is alive, he is alive.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy paused before explaining, “Do you remember me saying that the Qilin Immortal could ascend to an immortal while Lianyi and Little Ling couldn’t, right?

“Lianyi was originally qualified to become an immortal. But the Qilin Immortal defeated her and achieved it first, causing her to lose the opportunity to ascend to an immortal. If the Qilin Immortal had passed away, she would feel the force suppressing her Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit vanish—she could become an immortal immediately.”

Realization hit Lu Yang.

“Cases like Lianyi and Little Ling are extremely rare among half-immortals. There were many half-immortals in the ancient era. The reason they didn’t ascend to immortals wasn’t that we five suppressed them, but that those half-immortals simply couldn’t cultivate to that stage. It was a problem of talent.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was somewhat disdainful of those half-immortals, especially the ancient Dijiang. His own talent is lacking, yet he blames the era, insisting on ascending to an immortal now.

This was also why Jiang Lianyi and Ao Ling were publicly acknowledged as the strongest below the immortals. It wasn’t because the Qilin Immortal was a good husband, but because they themselves were immensely powerful.

Ascending to an immortal through effort alone didn’t work. The most crucial factor was that spark of enlightenment. Back then, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had many choices regarding her Dao Fruit and found it difficult to decide precisely because she had many such sparks.

When the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was a half-immortal, many of her fellow half-immortals wielded the Undying Incipient Dao Fruit or the Imperishable Incipient Dao Fruit. Once an Incipient Dao Fruit was condensed into a complete Dao Fruit, it would inherently be conferred an invincible position. Who wouldn’t want to condense one? But condensing such a Dao Fruit was exceedingly challenging. Even the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wasn’t sure she could succeed without the inspiration she had received from the Epoch Immortal.

“Alright, you may go back.” Jiang Lianyi tossed Chieftain Jin out of the door.

A demon king-level qiongqi was hardly different from a small tiger in her eyes. If he can’t serve as a punching bag, it’s useless to keep him.

~~~

How could Chieftain Jin be in the mood to continue observing the kingdom-founding ceremony? Feeling as if he was granted amnesty, he raced back to the Qiongqi Tomb under the cover of night to seek an audience with the Little Ancestor.

“Little Ancestor, something terrible has happened...” Chieftain Jin scrambled to find the Little Ancestor. But the moment he tried to speak, he discovered he couldn’t utter a single word.

Seeing Chieftain Jin like this, the little girl’s expression changed slightly. “Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit? Jiang Lianyi’s method? She’s still alive?” As one of the female demons sought out by Jiang Lianyi in the ancient era, she couldn’t be more familiar with Jiang Lianyi’s methods. Zhu Tian doesn’t use the Incipient Dao Fruit in this manner.

Realizing this, her lips curled into a cold smirk. “I originally had no intention of stirring up conflict; becoming one of the top ten factions in the Battle of the Great Era would have sufficed. But since Jiang Lianyi has appeared, I shall become the eleventh faction!”

1. This is a Northern Chinese slang that refers to an intractable person because they either pester you endlessly or remain unmoved by force or persuasion. ☜

Chapter 605: Tempestuous Gathering of Wind and Clouds

Two uninvited guests arrived at a large estate within the Demon City. The Phoenix tribesmen’s faces were so dark it seemed water might drip from them.

The Demon City accommodated the other factions in inns. But for major factions like Great Xia, the Buddhist Kingdom, the Dragon Tribe, and the Phoenix Tribe, their lodgings were more high-class and arranged in estates.

The elderly Dijiang tribesman came uninvited, once again urging the Phoenix Tribe to submit to them. The Phoenix Tribe had a living fossil who personally stepped forth to decline. In a clash of this level, even the Phoenix Tribe Chieftain, Jiang Xi, could only stand by the side.

“Jiang Mingzi, as the saying goes, ‘It’s hard for a hero to find a wise master.’ The Ancient Ancestor has taken the initiative to accept you. If you join the Demon Kingdom, the position of the second greatest tribe will be your Phoenix Tribe’s. This is a rare opportunity; tread carefully and cherish it!”

The other uninvited guest was the Taowu Tribe Chieftain. With his Transcendent Tribulation cultivation, his standing there alone brought immense pressure upon the Phoenix tribespeople.

“My Phoenix Tribe will not join any faction. Please leave!” The Phoenix Tribe living fossil wasn’t having any of it. According to records left by the Ancient Ancestor, this ancient Dijiang is not an easy character to deal with. I’m afraid joining the Demon Kingdom isn’t as simple as it seems on the surface.

“Leave? Jiang Mingzi, have you misunderstood something? I am not here to invite you, but to order you!”

“What are you trying to do?!” the Phoenix Tribe living fossil yelled.

“What I’m trying to do?” The Taowu Tribe Chieftain sneered, pulling out a brilliant golden magical edict from the front of his robes. Immortal charm flowed as it sparkled with pearls and treasures. It was a top-tier immortal artifact.

“Look what this is!” The elderly Dijiang tribesman activated the magical edict with his essence blood.

The magical edict bore the imprint of the ancient Dijiang’s Incipient Dao Fruit and a single strike delivered at his full power. If one couldn’t withstand this strike, they would be branded with a master-servant mark and forced to submit to the ancient Dijiang! This was how the Taowu Tribe Chieftain had been subdued.

“A half-immortal’s magical edict!” Due to the Phoenix Tribe’s continuous inheritance, Jiang Mingzi recognized it at a glance. “Bring forth the Ancient Ancestor’s token!” As if he was facing a formidable opponent, he similarly pulled out a treasure from the front of his robes; it was an exquisitely carved and lifelike phoenix jade pendant.

A five-colored phoenix flew out from the jade pendant. It was only the size of a palm and burned with true flames, carrying a terrifying aura. The presence it emitted was no weaker than the half-immortal magical edict.

Two soundless and formless auras collided, like two ancient great demons dueling across three hundred thousand years.

Boom!

The half-immortal magical edict suddenly self-immolated, bursting into blazing flames until it became as dim as burned paper. The ancient Dijiang’s aura vanished, and the Incipient Dao Fruit imprint was riddled with holes.

“Cough...” The elderly Dijiang and the Taowu Tribe Chieftain retreated two steps, coughing up some blood.

“Please leave.” Jiang Mingzi held the phoenix jade pendant, his expression unchanged.

“Good, good, good! You’re very good!” The elderly Dijiang and the Taowu Tribe Chieftain’s fury turned into laughter. Knowing they were outmatched, they left the estate.

~~~

“Teacher Ji, is it really safe for us to come to the Demon City?” Kong Hao asked quietly, shrinking his neck. He had the old Taowu, Ji Xiong, sealed within him. Under strong recommendation from Ji Xiong, he was forced to come to the Demon City to broaden his horizons.

“Be bolder. Many humans come to the Demon City. If you keep a low profile, no one will notice you.” The old Taowu laughed confidently.

He had failed in contending for the position of chieftain and was sealed within Kong Hao’s body. Upon hearing that the Demon Region was founding a kingdom and the Taowu Tribe was involved, he insisted on coming to take a look.

“Hmm?” The old Taowu looked up and noticed two disheveled figures in the sky.

One of them was his old rival, the current Taowu Tribe Chieftain.

“What’s the matter?” Kong Hao asked.

“Nothing. Just met an expected acquaintance."

~~~

The elderly Dijiang and the Taowu Tribe Chieftain passed through several layers of guards, unable to spare the energy to acknowledge their salutes as they rushed to the depths of the Demon City.

In the Demon City’s depths, the light was dim. The ancient Dijiang revealed his true form, seated on a colossal imperial throne like a small mountain. On either side of the throne stood two rows of equally imposing and enormous figures, faintly exuding auras of the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. These were beings referred to as demon emperors in the Demon Region.

The elderly Dijiang was also at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage and feared no demon emperor. His loyalty was to the old ancestor seated on the throne. The old ancestor values hierarchy; only Transcendent Tribulation cultivators are qualified to speak with him.

The two demons slowed their pace and knelt on the ground, reporting deferentially, “Your Majesty, the Phoenix Tribe has responded.”

The ancient Dijiang opened his eyes. His pupils were frighteningly bright, like two full moons, icy and deep. “What did the Phoenix Tribe say?”

The elder replied indignantly, “The Phoenix Tribe remains unrepentant and is firm in their attitude, unwilling to submit to Your Majesty. I tried promising them the second-highest position in the Demon Kingdom after our tribe and threatening them with force should they refuse, but neither worked.

“The two of us carried Your Majesty’s magical edict and used force to pressure them. However, the Phoenix Tribe brought forth the phoenix jade pendant left by their Phoenix Ancient Ancestor to resist, and we failed to subdue them.” The elder pulled out the magical edict from the front of his robes.

The originally brilliant gold sacred edict was now tattered and unsightly. It was clear at a glance that it had suffered severe damage and was no longer usable.

The Transcendent Tribulation great demons seated in the two rows flanking the imperial throne had varied expressions. This edict contained the ancient Dijiang’s power. It was precisely with such edicts that the Dijiang envoys had subdued and controlled them back then. They had attempted to resist, but the magical edict’s power was too overwhelming and changed too rapidly for them to react in time.

Not getting the desired result, the ancient Dijiang snorted coldly. Space trembled, showing his great displeasure.

“Stupidly obstinate!” He recalled his experience in the ancient era, especially the battles among half-immortals, and his expression grew increasingly grim.

He knew the origin of that jade pendant. Jiang Lianyi liked jade flutes. The jade pendant was made with leftover jade scraps from crafting jade flutes. It was Jiang Lianyi’s token—seeing the pendant was equivalent to seeing her. freewebnovel.com

“Do they really think I fear the Phoenix Tribe? Not to mention Jiang Lianyi isn’t around; even if she were, the Phoenix Tribe doesn’t have the guts to defy me!” The difference between the me of now and the me of the ancient era is like heaven and earth.

Through his Incipient Dao Fruit, he controlled nearly a hundred major tribes, ten Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, and numerous powerful subordinates. In this process, his Incipient Dao Fruit had become increasingly refined, showing signs of condensation.

I’m no longer the same as my past self. If I can’t even handle a mere Phoenix Tribe, what was the point of risking the danger of slumbering from ancient times until now?

“The Phoenix Tribe refuses to join the Demon Kingdom. Along with them, nearly half the Demon Region’s races follow the Phoenix Tribe’s lead and are also unwilling to surrender. To unify the Demon Region and establish a Demon Kingdom, the Phoenix Tribe must be taken care of. Either they surrender, or we make them die without a burial place!

“I have already given them a chance today. In the future, when the Phoenix Tribe is annihilated, they should have no complaints...” The ancient Dijiang’s eyes gleamed coldly.

Unifying the Demon Region will help my cultivation advance further, completing the metamorphosis from a half-immortal to an immortal. While others are still waiting for the Great Era to fully awaken and await fortuitous opportunities, I have no need for that. The current lack of powerhouses in the Demon Region is my fortuitous opportunity—I will act early to prove my Dao and ascend to an immortal, thereby becoming the player who wields the chess pieces in the Great Era’s resurgence!

Unifying the Demon Region is just the first step. Next, I will unify the East Sea, subjugating the sea tribes as well. That way, I will become unprecedentedly strong!

With both the East Sea and Demon Region under my control, I will leap to become the number one faction in the cultivation world. Even Great Xia and the Buddhist Kingdom will be no match for me!

I can even go further, attacking Great Xia and the Buddhist Kingdom to unify the entire cultivation world. At that time, it doesn’t matter who awakens. Even if the Four Ancient Immortals reappear, there’s nothing to fear!

For now, what I need to do is hold a successful founding ceremony and establish the Demon Kingdom. That way, attacking the Phoenix Tribe will be justified, and no one can find fault. The Phoenix Tribe enjoys an extremely high status in the Demon Region. Acting preemptively can easily tarnish my reputation and won’t be beneficial to my image.

“Phoenix Tribe...I hope you can still be this defiant during the kingdom-founding ceremony!”

Chapter 606: I’ve Decided—You’re the One!

“There is one more matter you must attend to.” The ancient Dijiang tossed a command token to the elderly Dijiang tribesman, who hurriedly caught it, preventing it from falling to the ground. “The phoenix jade tablet you two saw at the Phoenix Tribe is called the Phoenix Command. Seeing it is equivalent to seeing Jiang Lianyi.

“This is the Dijiang Command I forged. Seeing this command token is equivalent to seeing this esteemed one. It contains the might of my Incipient Dao Fruit.

“The kingdom-founding ceremony is imminent. This is the establishment of the kingdom and our authority. It is pivotal for the Demon Kingdom’s future development and the image it builds in the world’s eyes. With all major factions present, it’s the perfect chance to let them witness the strength of our Demon Kingdom.”

The ancient Dijiang continued slowly, “The best way to display our might is to find a stepping stone. Our Demon Kingdom’s foundation is unstable, so it’s inadvisable to make enemies now and provoke the major factions.

“The Heavenly Court Creed has been in the limelight lately, claiming to be led by some Dou Heavenly Sovereign and that they originate from the Heavenly Court. It’s laughable that everyone believes it’s real. This so-called Heavenly Court Creed is the most suitable stepping stone. Their reputation is sufficient, their strength is average, and they’re a fake.”

The elderly Dijiang wore a bitter face. “But where do we find the Heavenly Court Creed?”

The ancient Dijiang looked at his descendant with disappointment. “Why bother finding them? Just have someone play the part. Their identity is fake to begin with. If we get someone to act it out, who can say ours is fake?”

The elderly Dijiang’s eyes lit up, and he praised deferentially, “The Ancient Ancestor is wise!”

The ancient Dijiang was pleased with the compliment, his brows relaxing slightly. “I heard the Heavenly Court Creed has a Dou Heavenly Sovereign, a creed leader, Heavenly King protectors, a young creed leader, and Holy Sons. Just find a few people to impersonate the Heavenly Court Creed, especially the Heavenly King protectors and the young creed leader surnamed Lu or whatnot.

“Although the Heavenly Court Creed is fake, Young Creed Leader Lu’s strength is acceptable, capable of being the number one among his peers in a place like Great Xia. Geniuses represent the future. The ability to nurture geniuses demonstrates a faction’s extraordinariness.

“When the kingdom-founding ceremony begins, get the impostor Young Creed Leader Lu to make an entrance and provoke the Demon Kingdom. I will send my disciple to make an entrance and let the two battle it out.

“After Young Creed Leader Lu is defeated, I will personally show up to expose the Heavenly Court Creed’s true colors. This way, not only will the world witness the genius I have nurtured and trample upon Great Xia, but they will also marvel at my knowledge and depth!”

“The Ancient Ancestor is wise!” The elderly tribesman was concerned and revealed a hesitant expression. “But Young Creed Leader Lu’s talent is rare in the world. If I just pick anyone, I’m afraid the major factions will see through it.”

The ancient Dijiang waved his hand. “No matter. Use the Dijiang Command to control the impostors. Order them to squeeze out all their potential, similar to burning essence blood to forcibly become stronger. That way, they will be more or less indistinguishable from the real Young Creed Leader Lu.

“Alright, if there are no issues, go ahead.”

The ancient Dijiang sighed inwardly. My descendants aren’t very smart. I have to worry about everything myself.

~~~

“Want to go out for a stroll?” Lu Yang suggested early in the morning. We’ll be idling in the inn anyway, so I might as well let Senior Lianyi go out and check out the current cultivation world.

Jiang Lianyi thought about it and felt that going out for a walk was not a bad idea. After all, finding the Qilin Immortal wasn’t urgent.

Lu Yang dressed formally, quickly washed up, and went downstairs to head out. The moment he stepped out, he ran into a new acquaintance.

“It’s you!” Qin Feng of the Jiuying Tribe glared at Lu Yang with gritted teeth.

Beside Qin Feng were the prodigies of the Demon Alliance. Seeing Lu Yang leave the inn, realization dawned upon them, and they pointed at him furiously. “You’re from the Dao-Seeking Sect!”

This brat isn’t from the Phoenix Tribe at all, but from the Dao-Seeking Sect!

“I understand now! The ones following Jiang Shishi were Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou of the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Some quick-witted demon prodigies had pieced things together. Although they hadn’t seen what these two people looked like, considering the skills displayed in the Creation Ancient Domain, only Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou fit the bill.

Actually, Lu Yang wanted to say, “There are three others in the Dao-Seeking Sect who are roughly on the same level as we are; don’t immediately assert it’s the two of us.”

But there’s no use saying this now. Their brains aren’t good, but their luck is—they guessed correctly.

Man Gu and the other two hadn’t appeared in the Golden Core category of the finals, so the world wasn’t very familiar with them yet.

Lu Yang turned around and walked back into the inn. Qin Feng and the others didn’t dare force their way in, and shouting insults would tarnish their image, so they could only block the door in indignation.

“Why did you come back?” Jiang Lianyi was about to go out when she saw Lu Yang returning expressionlessly.

“Miscalculation. I was recognized.” Lu Yang sighed, explaining the situation at the entrance and how he had made enemies in the Creation Ancient Domain.

Jiang Lianyi found the situation tricky. It’s not convenient for me to intervene in grudges between juniors. “How about I disguise you?” Having learned from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Jiang Lianyi’s disguise skills were top-notch. Although her memories were gone, her skills remained.

“That would be best!” Lu Yang was overjoyed.

Jiang Lianyi extended both hands and cupped Lu Yang’s face, kneading and rubbing it. Soon, Lu Yang’s appearance completely changed; even the elders wouldn’t recognize him.

Lu Yang went back to change his clothes. After a brief thought, he slung a sword on his back to make the disguise more thorough.

“Perfect.” Lu Yang gave a thumbs-up to his reflection in the bronze mirror.

The two walked out of the inn openly. Qin Feng and the others totally failed to recognize that it was Lu Yang. Jiang Lianyi wore a cloak, emitting an aura that kept strangers away. Qin Feng and the others didn’t dare approach her. Moreover, they could deduce she was a female cultivator from her figure, which didn’t match Lu Yang.

~~~

The Demon City was bustling, with demons and humans mingling. Although there were minor frictions, no major disturbances occurred.

Humans made up half the population in the Demon City. Demons set up shops here, hawking and peddling, while envoys from the Buddhist Kingdom sought alms with their bowls.

“Benefactor, you carry heavy resentful energy. This poor monk is willing to chant scriptures to disperse the lingering resentment. Benefactor, could you donate some spirit stones to cast a golden body for our Buddha?”

“Get lost! I worked on building the Demon City for over a month, and when it was completed, they told me it was volunteer labor! What scriptures can disperse my resentment?”

The Buddhist Kingdom envoy laughed dryly and moved on to the next potential alms-giver.

Soon, he met Master Jiechen, Master Jiesha’s junior brother. The two senior Buddhist monks joined their palms and chanted Buddhist prayers.

“Jiechen, it’s been a long time. May I know if you could donate some spirit stones to cast a golden body for our Buddha?”

“Certainly.” Master Jiechen readily took out several top-grade spirit stones from his kasaya and placed them in the Buddhist Kingdom envoy’s alms bowl, producing crisp clangs.

“Chenyuan, it’s been a long time. May I know if you could donate some spirit stones to cast a golden body for our Buddha?”

“Certainly.” The Buddhist Kingdom envoy, Master Chenyuan, took out several top-grade spirit stones from the alms bowl and returned them to Master Jiechen.

Thus, the two senior monks obtained double the merit.

Jiang Lianyi found it eye-opening. Back when we fabricated the Buddhist stories, we had the setting of seeking alms to cast golden bodies and accumulate merit. But I never expected such an efficient method of merit accumulation.

To be honest, Lu Yang also found it eye-opening.

He also saw Qiu Jin’an approach the sea tribes, asking if they would be willing to relocate to the Five-Elements Sect’s Water Branch, assuring them that the Five-Elements Sect would handle the immigration procedures. Unfortunately, it wasn’t successful. The sea tribes agreed they could visit the Five-Elements Sect, but immigration was out of the question.

The elderly Dijiang was searching for candidates for the street. After looking for a long time without finding a suitable candidate, his eyes lit up upon spotting Lu Yang.

I’ve decided—you’re the one!

Chapter 607: From Now On, You Are Young Creed Leader Lu

Selecting an impostor Young Creed Leader Lu was no easy task.

He couldn't just grab any random Golden Core cultivator off the street. No matter how tightly bound an ordinary Golden Core cultivator was to the Dijiang Command, they couldn’t become a Golden Core cultivator of Young Creed Leader Lu’s caliber.

At the very least, it had to be a Golden Core cultivator with a solid foundation. Only then would there be room for manipulation.

Secondly, they had to know how to use a sword. When Young Creed Leader Lu rampaged through the Dao-Seeking Sect, his most notable skill was his sword technique.

Moreover, this person couldn’t belong to any major faction. If a disciple from a major faction went missing, it could easily lead to trouble.

Hence, the elderly Dijiang had searched for half a day without finding a suitable candidate.

Then he noticed Lu Yang carrying a treasured sword on his back.

The ancient Dijiang had already awakened two hundred years ago. Though it seemed he had unified most of the Demon Region in just half a year, this was actually the successful result after two centuries of accumulation.

Over these two hundred years, the Dijiang Tribe had secretly gathered all sorts of intelligence, including information on prodigies in the current era. They knew the appearances of Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, Man Gu, Bai Ming of the Five-Elements Sect, and Shi Chan of the Hanging Monastery.

This sword-carrying person isn’t among the disciples the Dijiang Tribe had collected information on. He’s either a rogue cultivator or a disciple of an insignificant faction!

Perfect for impersonating Young Creed Leader Lu!

The one in the black cloak beside him looks to only be at the Fusion Stage—nothing to fear.

The elderly Dijiang secretly formulated a plan. As this place was crowded with eyes everywhere, it wasn’t convenient to act here. He patiently followed the two. As a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, unless a half-immortal appears, no one can counter me. I won’t be discovered.

“Why is someone following us?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy frowned.

Jiang Lianyi nodded. “Indeed, someone has been following us. It’s probably a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator from the Dijiang Tribe.”

“What does he want?”

“Who cares?”

“Right.”

The human, ghost, and demon continued touring the Demon City.

“We’re not allowed to enter?” Lu Yang arrived at the center of the Demon City, which was blocked off by a temporarily erected hundred-meter-high wall. Great demons at the Fusion Stage stood guard here; no one was allowed to enter unless granted permission.

“This is the heavenly altar for the kingdom-founding ceremony.” Jiang Lianyi scanned the area with her spiritual consciousness and immediately knew what it looked like inside. “It seems Zhu Tian bled a lot for this.”

The main structure of the heavenly altar was constructed from liuli-glazed white jade. Even in ancient times, this material was rare; Jiang Lianyi didn’t have any. If she wanted some, she would have to take raw materials like sand and stone to the Epoch Immortal, modify conditions like wind direction and temperature, and ask the Epoch Immortal to use his Epoch Dao Fruit to create a piece of liuli-glazed white jade.

“Oh, we can see it during the kingdom-founding ceremony then,” Lu Yang said. Seeing it in advance will ruin the mystery. “Why don’t we check out that street?” He pointed to the other side of a narrow alley.

“Sure.”

The human and the demon entered the alley. The elderly Dijiang finally seized the opportunity, holding his breath and focusing his mind before quickly following.

With a flash, he leaped through the air and appeared before Lu Yang and Jiang Lianyi. “Kid, I’ve finally got you! Made me wait long enough!”

Just as Lu Yang was about to react, the elderly Dijiang swiftly pulled out the Dijiang Command and activated it with essence blood. The almost tangible phantom image of the ancient Dijiang materialized, fangs bared and claws brandished. It passed through Lu Yang’s pupils and charged into his mental space, seeking to control him.

Wielding the Dijiang Command is like having the Ancient Ancestor present in person. Let alone a mere Golden Core cultivator, even a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator can’t withstand it!

Inside the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy pinched the ancient Dijiang phantom with one hand, her expression peculiar. What kind of move is this?

The ancient Dijiang phantom struggled like a living creature, its six limbs thrashing and its four wings flapping, stirring up a hurricane within the mental space.

Thud! Without a second thought, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy smashed her other hand onto the ancient Dijiang phantom’s head, instantly interrupting its attack.

“A half-immortal-level mental attack. That does have a bit of substance.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was confident that she was unbeatable within Lu Yang’s mental space.

At the same time, the walls of the mental space glowed, and the talisman runes constantly changed, as if charging up power for an attack.

This was the safeguard Yun Zhi had left in Lu Yang’s mental space to ensure his safety here.

With the ancient Dijiang phantom stopped by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, the talisman runes on the walls dimmed and merged back into the walls, as if they had never appeared. Exerting slight force with her right hand, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy crushed the ancient Dijiang phantom, causing it to burst apart.

The ancient Dijiang phantom put up no resistance from start to finish.

Unfortunately, Lu Yang was controlled by the Dijiang Command. His eyes became vacant, his arms hung limply, and his whole body relaxed, no longer regarding the elder with vigilance.

“You too!” The elderly Dijiang aimed the Dijiang Command at Jiang Lianyi and activated it. Jiang Lianyi was also controlled and showed no reaction.

“What’s your name? Which sect are you from?” The elderly Dijiang wanted to confirm again that the person he found was suitable.

“I’m Yun Yang from the Heaven’s Gate Sect.”

“Yun Yang? No sect?” The elderly Dijiang tribesman mumbled, recalling the information he possessed on Great Xia’s geniuses. There was no Yun Yang.

“What about this person next to you?” He turned his gaze to Jiang Lianyi, whose black cloak obscured her features.

“She’s my shifu, Su Yiren.”

“The secluded Fusion cultivator, Su Yiren. So it’s her.” The elderly Dijiang understood. Few cultivators in Great Xia knew of Su Yiren, much less him, who resided in the Demon Region.

“Are you skilled with a sword?”

“Yes.”

“You two are very lucky. The Ancient Ancestor has selected you to impersonate the Heavenly Court Creed at the kingdom-founding ceremony in two days. You are no longer Yun Yang, but the Heavenly Court Creed’s Young Creed Leader Lu.”

“Yes, I am Young Creed Leader Lu!” Lu Yang declared in a resonating voice.

“Good attitude.” The elderly Dijiang nodded in satisfaction. “As for you, Su Yiren, you are a Heavenly King protector of the Heavenly Court Creed.”

Under the black cloak, Jiang Lianyi rolled her eyes and ignored him.

The elderly Dijiang paid no heed to it. “Yun Yang, your task is to impersonate the Heavenly Court Creed at the kingdom-founding ceremony, fight our tribe’s prodigy, and after a fierce battle, be defeated by our prodigy!”

“Yes, I promise to complete the mission!” Lu Yang replied in a sonorous tone.

The elderly Dijiang activated the Dijiang Command again. “I order you to unleash your full potential, no matter the price! You must reach Young Creed Leader Lu’s level in the shortest time possible!”

Right afterward, Lu Yang turned red all over, as if he was burning. He collapsed to the ground and curled into a ball, clutching the clothing over his heart and letting out a heart-rending wail.

“So painful...so hot...power...power is continuously surging out!”

All power comes with a price. Lu Yang couldn’t withstand this power. He rolled on the ground, beads of sweat the size of beans breaking out on his forehead. Soon, his hair was completely soaked with sweat.

Sizzle, sizzle, sizzle... Lu Yang’s temperature rose higher and higher, evaporating the sweat droplets and producing a sizzling steam.

Amidst the steam, Lu Yang slowly rose, having adapted to this power.

The elderly Dijiang was overjoyed. As expected of the Dijiang Command bestowed by the Ancient Ancestor! I didn’t expect its effects to be this amazing!

“Your Excellency, I have reached Young Creed Leader Lu’s level!”

Chapter 608: The Kingdom-Founding Ceremony Commences

“Perform a set of sword techniques for me to take a look.” Under the elderly Dijiang's order, Lu Yang couldn’t control his body, obeying the elder.

Lu Yang’s long sleeves danced with the sword, whose edge was unstoppably sharp, overcoming everything in its path. Wherever it passed, the air was sundered.

The Slashing Word Mantra and the Breaking Word Mantra were executed one by one. They were all lethal moves that even Nascent Soul cultivators would balk at facing head-on.

“Good, very good!” The elderly Dijiang laughed heartily. If I didn’t know this was an impostor, I would truly think this is Young Creed Leader Lu.

He took out two masks and a painting from his storage ring. “These are human skin masks forged by this esteemed one. Inject spirit energy, and they will allow you to change into any appearance you desire.

“This is Young Creed Leader Lu’s appearance. Yun Yang, you shall use this painting as a reference to turn into Young Creed Leader Lu. freewebnovel.com

“As for you, Su Yiren, few have seen your true face, but we cannot rule out the possibility of encountering someone who recognizes you. Wear this mask and change your appearance as you please.”

The two accepted the human skin masks. They were as light as cicada wings and cool to the touch. With practiced ease, Lu Yang wore the mask and transformed himself into Young Creed Leader Lu.

Jiang Lianyi went through the motions perfunctorily, altering her appearance to resemble sixty to seventy percent of her original looks before removing her hood to reveal the disguise.

“Next is the acting. The look in your eyes is wrong—they lack the sense of vicissitudes and a weathered depth that bears the weight of years.

“What is the Heavenly Court Creed? It is the continuation of the ancient Heavenly Court. After three hundred millennia, one should possess a mental state that has witnessed massive transformations in the world—where the blue sea has turned into mulberry fields—and experienced the vicissitudes of life—where the people around are no longer the same. Your gaze should be vast, tinged with nostalgia, and brimming with disdain for the modern era.

“Also, the Heavenly Court Creed was a major organization of the ancient era—the most prosperous and powerful period in the cultivation world. As the young creed leader and a Heavenly King protector, you must exhibit pride for the ancient era!”

Lu Yang, “...”

You’ve really thought everything through.

When Lu Yang had made his appearance as Young Creed Leader Lu, these were almost the exact thoughts he had. It was supposed to be a form of psychological suggestion to help himself quickly get into character.

With that in mind, Lu Yang let out a derisive snort. “What dogshit Dijiang Tribe? What ancient Dijiang? When the tiger is absent from the mountain, the monkey proclaims himself king. He was merely someone defeated at the hands of Dou Heavenly Sovereign, not even qualified to join our Heavenly Court!”

Jiang Lianyi snorted coldly and wore an icy countenance as she regarded the elder with contempt, her frigid gaze utterly devoid of emotion.

“Yes, precisely this feeling!” The elderly Dijiang slapped his thigh, astonished that the two had gotten it right on the first try. “Excellent! It seems you master and disciple are very talented in this aspect.”

The elderly Dijiang was meticulous in his work. He proceeded to relay more information regarding the Heavenly Court Creed.

Lu Yang listened, nodding frequently. It seems the other party’s intelligence on the Heavenly Court Creed is extremely accurate and without error.

“Alright, in two days, at the kingdom-founding ceremony, you two will act according to my arrangements. Until then, revert to your original forms. Behave as usual and do not let anything slip.”

“Understood.”

The elderly Dijiang nodded, then departed to report his successful result to the ancient Dijiang, leaving Lu Yang and Jiang Lianyi behind.

A moment passed before Jiang Lianyi broke the silence.

“What now?”

Lu Yang shrugged. “Don’t ask me. I’m currently under the Dijiang’s control. I do whatever they tell me to.”

Jiang Lianyi nodded. “Me too.”

~~~

Having already gained plenty in the Demon City, the pair didn’t continue strolling around. They returned to the inn and informed the others of the events. As the elders listened to their account, they slapped their thighs in regret.

“Tell me, just tell me—why do I never encounter such good fortune?!” The five elders’ hearts ached as if the Taciturn Daoist Priest had passed away.

Meng Jingzhou was also filled with regret. I’m an almighty Holy Son of the Heavenly Court Creed, yet I didn’t get to show my face at such a pivotal event.

Lu Yang patted Meng Jingzhou’s shoulder ruefully. “It’s all fate.”

Gan Tian remained silent at the side. I belong to the Dao-Seeking Sect, not the Heavenly Court Creed.

~~~

Two days passed in the blink of an eye. The kingdom-founding ceremony officially commenced.

The towering walls erected around the heavenly altar were dismantled. From a distance, the heavenly altar dazzled with blinding white rays.

“Is that liuli-glazed white jade? Such a huge piece?”

The visiting cultivators were visibly moved. Even the Transcendent Tribulation experts were inwardly shocked. The heavenly altar was not constructed from blocks of liuli-glazed white jade but was carved from a single piece. It wasn’t an exaggeration to call it a priceless treasure!

The heavenly altar was divided into nine layers, corresponding to the nine major cultivation realms.

The attendees were classified into two categories. The first consisted of factions personally invited by the Dijiang Tribe, such as the Buddhist Kingdom and the Dragon Tribe of the East Sea. The Dijiang Tribe dared not slight these factions, providing them with the best audience seats and even spirit fruits and meals.

The second category comprised rogue cultivators or small factions that turned up uninvited. These minor factions surrounded the perimeter of the heavenly altar, their viewing experience entirely up to chance.

Posing as rogue cultivators, Lu Yang and Jiang Lianyi temporarily parted ways with the elders. Gan Tian intended to continue training in the Demon Region, so she was also among the crowd of rogue cultivators.

“Old Qiu, we meet again,” First Elder greeted jovially with cupped fists. Seated to his left was Qiu Jin’an.

It was inappropriate to put on a sour face and be impolite in a public setting, so he could only respond with a smile.

“Second Imperial Prince, so you’re the one who has come this time.” First Elder stood up and called out across several sect delegations.

Great Xia had sent not the First Imperial Prince Jiang Qun, but the Second Imperial Prince Jiang Zhu.

Jiang Zhu stood tall and upright, his demeanor martial and imposing. Accomplished on both literary and martial fronts, he was rumored to harbor ambitions to vie for the throne. He cupped his hands and returned the greeting with the courtesy due from a junior.

“Fellow Daoist Ao Li, it has been two hundred years since we last met, hasn’t it? Is everything well with the Old Dragon Emperor?” Seated to First Elder’s right was Ao Li of the East Sea Dragon Tribe, an envoy sent by the Old Dragon Emperor.

Ao Li sported dragon horns atop his head, and he was decorated with jewels from horns to toes. The value of his attire alone likely surpassed the total wealth of an ordinary Fusion cultivator.

Seeing that First Elder was seated beside him, Ao Li’s expression turned unpleasant. He snorted, unwilling to engage in unnecessary conversation. “The old palace leader is well.”

“Look at you, such an attitude makes us appear estranged! People might think there’s some conflict between us. Have you forgotten the time I assisted you in overcoming your heart devil tribulation?”

At the mention of this matter, Ao Li’s face grew even more unpleasant.

Two hundred years ago, he was afflicted with a heart devil tribulation. Due to the Dragon’s inherently licentious nature, his heart devil tribulation was a lust tribulation. For a while, the East Sea Dragon Tribe floundered.

First Elder happened to be visiting back then. He stepped forward and forcibly rendered Ao Li impotent through pills and acupuncture, thereby allowing him to overcome the heart devil tribulation.

At the time, his heart devil had manifested as all manner of beauties to tempt him, yet he couldn’t do anything even if he wanted to, leaving even the heart devil at a loss for what to do.

Afterward, Ao Li consulted famous physicians and spent a century before he was finally cured and regained his ability to partake in bedroom affairs.

First Elder was magnanimous and paid no mind to Ao Li’s attitude, instead greeting the Buddhist Kingdom’s envoy, master Yuanchen. “Master Yuanchen, we haven’t met in fifty years. I trust you have been well.”

Master Chenyuan sat with steady poise. Seeing First Elder greeting him from a distance, he chuckled and placed a hand before his chest, responding out of courtesy. “Monks do not speak falsehoods. Truthfully speaking, I hadn’t expected to meet you here, Benefactor. What wretched luck.”

Chapter 609: Chieftain Jin and the Nine-Netherworlds Creed

“Master Yuanchen, you are too heartless. When you were young and traveled throughout Great Xia seeking alms with a counterfeit ordination certificate, you were caught by the authorities and nearly imprisoned for the crime of possessing forged official documents. It was only after I intervened and explained that the authorities didn’t press charges.”

Great Xia had stringent requirements for the qualifications of monks and Daoists. Monks from the Buddhist Kingdom or disciples of the Hanging Monastery were treated equally. They needed to pass examinations and undergo review—only by holding an ordination certificate could one be recognized by the court as a monk. This approval would permit them to beg for alms and perform rituals. Otherwise, it would be illegal.

In Master Chenyuan’s youth, he came to Great Xia to propagate Buddhist teachings, and his first task was to obtain the ordination certificate.

At the mention of this matter, Master Chenyuan became even more restless. “If you hadn’t informed me that I needed an ordination certificate to preach in Great Xia and then sold me a counterfeit one, how could I have been arrested by the authorities?”

First Elder declared with righteous conviction, “You were the one who approached me first, claiming the people of Great Xia lived in abject misery, plunged into deep water and scorching fire—an abyss of suffering. You said you came to Great Xia to help the commoners escape their predicament and guide them to your Buddhist Kingdom to chant Buddhist scriptures and renounce mundane life.

“I told you the people of Great Xia lived better than those in the Buddhist Kingdom, but you refused to believe me. I simply wanted you to enter prison to see for yourself. Even the prisoners weren’t living in such abject misery. How could the common people possibly be as you had described?

“Later, when I saw how fiercely you resisted arrest, I stepped in to explain the circumstances.”

First Elder and Master Chenyuan sat in the front row, with Ao Li of the East Sea Dragon Tribe between them.

As Ao Li listened to their argument, his heart itched, and he temporarily forgot his own enmity with First Elder, instinctively asking, “So did the authorities let Master Chen Yuan go?”

“Not exactly. Although he didn’t know the certificate was fake, which didn’t constitute the crime of knowingly possessing forged documents, he didn’t understand Great Xia’s rules. He had crossed the border directly, which constituted illegal entry, so he was still arrested. And while they were at it, they arrested me too.”

“Why did they arrest you?” Ao Li asked, not quite following.

“Because I forged the certificate.”

“Oh, right.”

Master Chen Yuan closed his eyes to rest his mind, refusing to engage further with First Elder.

First Elder continued scanning the seating area for familiar faces. Since they were outside the sect without the Taciturn Daoist Priest present, First Elder’s words and actions represented the Dao-Seeking Sect. On such an occasion, he had to take the initiative and manage the sect’s diplomatic relations. He had traveled extensively in his youth. The East Sea Dragon Tribe, the Buddhist Kingdom, the Demon Region Dragon Tribe, the Phoenix Tribe, and the Qiongqi Tribe—all had his acquaintances.

“Is Little Jin not here?” First Elder noticed the seat reserved for the Qiongqi Tribe Chieftain was empty and found it strange. Would he really miss such a major event as the Demon Region’s kingdom-founding ceremony?

“You know Chieftain Jin?” Ao Li couldn’t help but ask again.

“Of course! How could I not know him? Back when Little Jin accidentally stumbled into a diabolic creed, it was us, the Dao-Seeking Nine, who intervened in time and fished him out.”

Ao Li grew even more curious. “Which diabolic creed?”

“Qin Jiunian, shut your mouth!”

Chieftain Jin gasped for breath as he arrived late. Hearing First Elder bring up this matter, he shot him a warning glare.

Two nights prior, he had encountered Jiang Lianyi and immediately raced back to his tribe to report to the Little Ancestor. Upon learning that Jiang Lianyi had reappeared in the world, the Little Ancestor had a feeling that unforeseen incidents might occur at the kingdom-founding ceremony and instructed him to attend the ceremony posthaste.

The territories of the Dijiang and Qiongqi tribes spanned nearly half the Demon Region. Chieftain Jin had pushed himself to the brink of exhaustion just to make it in time.

And the first thing he heard upon his arrival was First Elder dredging up his dark history.

Among the leaders of the major factions, Chieftain Jin was relatively young, only just over nine hundred years old.

When he just reached the Nascent Soul Stage nine hundred years ago, he felt the Qiongqi Tribe was stagnant and rigid in their thinking. He feared that if this persisted, they would only grow poorer.

To seek a way out, he left his homeland and illegally entered Great Xia. As he lacked proper identification, he lingered in the black market, and by chance, he joined the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

After working in the Nine-Netherworlds Creed for some time, he met a wealthy young master. This young master shared his fondness for wine, women, and gambling, and often picked up the tab. The two quickly became friends. The young master lived a life of debauchery, yet his money never seemed to run out, which Chieftain Jin was terribly envious of.

Once, he tried to ask about the young master’s background, inquiring which wealthy ancestral clan he hailed from.

The young master replied that he wasn’t from an ancestral clan—the money he spent wasn’t given by his family but earned by himself.

This piqued Chieftain Jin’s curiosity further. He pressed for details on the young master’s money-making methods and asked whether he could get involved.

At first, the young master was unwilling. After Chieftain Jin was at his beck and call and attended to his every need by working like oxen and horses, he finally managed to persuade the young master.

The young master said a friend of his had invented a lifespan-extending pill formula. Although the improvement wasn’t significant, it was enough to make cultivators nearing the end of their lifespans desperate to get their hands on it. Investing in this venture now would promise great returns, where investing one hundred spirit stones would yield one hundred and twenty back—the more one invested, the more one earned.

Hence, Chieftain Jin tentatively invested twenty thousand spirit stones. A year later, the young master gave him twenty-four thousand back.

That night, Chieftain Jin was so excited he couldn’t sleep, convinced a golden money-making opportunity had arrived.

However, he wasn’t a reckless person. Worried the venture might be unstable, he tested the waters for two more years.

For three consecutive years, the profits were substantial. The young master hadn’t lied!

The path to riches was right before him!

Unfortunately, one could never forecast the wind and clouds—no one could anticipate when things would go awry. This matter was discovered by Chieftain Jin’s superior, a branch leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

The branch master squeezed Chieftain Jin away and began dealing directly with the young master.

Some time later, Chieftain Jin found himself being hunted by the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. He had to flee while trying to figure out why.

Even after he escaped back to the Demon Region, he still couldn’t understand why the Nine-Netherworlds Creed chased him down.

Two hundred years ago, he inadvertently mentioned this story when chatting with First Elder. It was only then that he learned that the young master he had known back then was none other than Eighth Elder.

The Dao-Seeking Nine had devised an elaborate scheme for the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, swindling them until they bled with nothing left. And he had been the very first member in the creed to have fallen for it.

It was likely out of sheer fury and the desire to vent his anger that the then Nine-Netherworlds Creed had ordered his death, but Chieftain Jin had narrowly escaped.

A little over a year ago, he discovered three Nine-Netherworlds Creed followers had sneaked into the Demon Region. Reminded of his days of being hunted, his pent-up rage flared, and he swatted the three followers to death with a single claw strike.

The matter of his joining the Nine-Netherworlds Creed and getting deceived by the Dao-Seeking Nine was definitely not something he could allow First Elder to reveal. It’s too embarrassing. His tiger-like eyes widened menacingly as he glared at First Elder with hostility.

First Elder spread his hands, gesturing that he wouldn’t speak of this matter. I’m just here to reminisce; I have no ill intentions.

First Elder was about to continue locating more familiar faces for a chat when the deep, resonant toll of a bronze bell rang out. Its sound seemed to emanate from a bygone era, reverberating through the heavenly altar.

Mist began to rise from the heavenly altar. Within it, the colossal figure of the ancient Dijiang flickered in and out of view, shrouded in mystery.

The white clouds in the sky shifted and morphed into auspicious clouds.

The kingdom-founding ceremony had officially begun.

Out of courtesy, First Elder had no choice but to temporarily shelve his plans for further conversations.

Chapter 610: The Ancient Dijiang’s Lifelong Learning

Dang— Dang— Dang—

Nine tolls of the bell rang out. The auspicious clouds at the horizon morphed into multifarious forms of a hundred different demons, each lifelike and with a unique demeanor. They represented the demon races that had pledged allegiance to the Dijiang Tribe.

The hundred demon clouds shifted once more, bowing reverently toward the heavenly altar before reverting to simple white clouds. They drifted down like snowflakes or mist, scattering over the altar.

The heavenly altar became shrouded in a hazy veil, akin to the mist at the beginning of primordial hundun chaos—indistinct, inscrutable, and profoundly mysterious.

Music began to play. The notes of dizi flutes flowed like a river, and the melodies from guqin were ethereal like illusions. They intertwined with the harmonious rhythms of drums and se[1], creating a peaceful atmosphere. Countless humans and demons alike were immersed in the mellifluous tunes.

A figure the size of a small mountain appeared alongside the music. It moved upon the altar, enveloped by endless mist. One could faintly discern that it was an ancient being with six legs and four wings. This ancient being was crimson like the sun, especially conspicuous within the mist.

Dong!

The music changed, swelling with fervor, strength, and valor, imbuing the audience’s hearts with zeal. Races of weaker willpower found themselves swayed by the music’s influence, feeling an urge to follow the Dijiang Tribe into battle, charging forward and breaking the enemies’ lines to expand territories.

The ancient being danced upon the altar. Its movements were graceful and precise, displaying the most orthodox ancient dance. Beating its four wings, it stirred up a gale that felt like the beginning of primal hundun chaos, where heaven and earth were split apart. It transformed into a sun, blazing gloriously atop the nine-layered altar, radiating brilliant light in all directions.

It was a half-immortal being—the ancient Supreme Lord Zhu Tian.

The major factions had come prepared. As if they had agreed to it beforehand, they took out recording orbs to document the entire process.

“Is that the legendary ancient Dijiang?”

“So scary. I feel like he’s looking at me.” Someone shuddered under Zhu Tian’s nearly imperceptible yet palpable oppressive aura, their legs trembling so violently they could barely stand. It was due to the oppressive aura of Zhu Tian, but also the immense weight of ancient history.

“An ancient half-immortal—one who hails from the most prosperous ancient era and listened to the sermons of the Four Ancient Immortals,” others murmured in awe. That was the greatest era because four immortals existed, and the number of half-immortals and Transcendent Tribulation cultivators was staggeringly high. The present era couldn’t compare at all.

For most people, the ancient era was history, a legend. But for Zhu Tian, these were events he had personally lived through. This fact alone placed him above any modern-era cultivators.

“The Dijiang Tribe is very proficient in music?” Lu Yang was surprised, noting that the musicians responsible for the heart-stirring performance earlier were all Dijiang tribespeople. This wasn’t a skill that could be honed overnight.

Jiang Lianyi replied, “The Dijiang Tribe has always been very proficient in music and dance. Zhu Tian is a prolific master of this art. Music can inspire the heart, but it can also beguile the heart. Zhu Tian is well-versed in music, and building upon this, he comprehended the Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit, which is capable of controlling living beings.

“In ancient times, whenever my husband and the others held their sermons, Zhu Tian would always perform beforehand. His combat strength was average, but his performance skills were first-rate.”

“Why do the people around us seem to have an impulse to submit upon seeing Zhu Tian?” Lu Yang was quick to notice the unusual behavior around them.

“He’s using an Incipient Dao Fruit. He wouldn’t dare to employ its power here openly. This is the most superficial level of control, considered a form of psychological suggestion. Using it now is probably to enhance the atmosphere.” Jiang Lianyi’s expression turned peculiar. As a fellow wielder of the Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit and a fellow Daoist who had studied the Dao of maintaining lofty airs with the Heaven Mandate Immortal, Zhu Tian’s methods could not escape her eyes.

Ten figures emanating terrifying auras slowly walked forth. They were of varied forms, only slightly smaller than Zhu Tian’s massive frame. Some appeared old and decrepit, while others brimmed with vitality... Nonetheless, they represented absolute power.

These were the ten Transcendent Tribulation demon emperors under Zhu Tian’s command!

One first-tier half-immortal, ten demon emperors, and nearly a hundred major races—this lineup was even more formidable than what the second-generation Great Yu Imperial Preceptor had amassed for his attempt at resurgence!

“Look! Isn’t that the Baihu Tribe’s Grand Elder? Wasn’t it said he had perished? He’s actually alive?!”

“He’s still alive! And he’s an old demon emperor at the Advanced Transcendent Tribulation Stage!”

“And that one! That’s the Taowu Tribe’s chieftain. Rumor has it that there was another Transcendent Tribulation taowu who vied with him over the position. The two fought one-on-one, and he single-handedly killed his opponent!”

“Is that for real? He killed someone of the same level?”

“How could it be false? Go inquire around the Taowu Tribe; everyone knows!”

“Is that nine-headed snake the Jiuying Tribe’s old chieftain?”

The origins of each Transcendent Tribulation demon emperor were gradually identified. The Fusion cultivators present were filled with fear and trepidation. Supreme Lord Zhu Tian had prepared too thoroughly. Under such a force, it was likely that even the Dragon and Phoenix tribes couldn’t resist, compelled to surrender and pledge allegiance!

Zhu Tian composed himself for a moment before slowly speaking with a solemn expression. “The Great Era is imminent, yet the demon race is scattered like loose sand, with everyone fighting their own battles. This pains this monarch deeply. How can a Demon Region like this protect itself in the Battle of the Great Era?
