“Before my deep slumber, I received a request from the Qilin Immortal. He wished for me to lend a hand and save the Demon Region in times of crisis.

“I am not one who covets power. But since I have been entrusted by the Qilin Immortal, and the Great Era is upon us, I fear a repeat of the ancient era’s tragic situation. This is why I seek to unify the demon race and establish the Demon Kingdom. Only by combining the strength of all tribes into a single rope can we overcome the tribulations and calamities of the Great Era and preserve the demon race’s power!

“Since the Qilin Immortal perished, the demon race is missing a standard-bearer. Although I lack talent and cannot reach the Qilin Immortal’s heights, I have once exchanged blows with numerous half-immortals. My fellow Daoists were generous to hold me in high regard, conferring me the flattering title of ‘Number One Below Immortals.’ I am truly unworthy of such praise.”

Zhu Tian’s tone grew somber, as if he found the title “Number One Below Immortals” too exaggerated, not in line with his low-profile nature, even if he did possess such strength. It also seemed he was reminiscing about those fellow Daoists who had passed away and lamenting their early passing, which had left the heavy burden of unifying the Demon Region on his shoulders.

Then, Zhu Tian’s eyes brightened. He pulled himself out of his memories of ancient times and rallied his spirits. This is not the time to sink into despondency. I must focus on the present and shoulder the great responsibility that awaits me.

With a resolute gaze, Zhu Tian announced in a sonorous voice that echoed throughout the entire Demon City, “Let the heavens bear witness! Let the Four Immortals bear witness! The departed are no more, and the ancient era cannot be pursued. The tribulation of the Great Era is imminent. For the sake of the countless demons in this world, this monarch hereby declares the establishment of the Demon Kingdom, with this monarch as its first ruler!”

Suddenly, dark clouds gathered, lightning flashed, and thunder boomed. Four purple lightning bolts as thick as water vats struck down, as if the Four Ancient Immortals were witnessing this historic moment and granting their approval for Zhu Tian to establish the kingdom.

Zhu Tian shook with excitement, warm tears welling in his eyes. “Zhu Tian kowtows in gratitude to the Four Immortals!”

The shills planted below the stage by the Dijiang Tribe clapped ardently, their applause thunderous and deafening.

Jiang Lianyi, “...”

Entrusted by my husband, “Number One Below Immortals,” talismans to create lightning, planting shills to lead the applause—your preparation is really thorough.

Jiang Lianyi suspected that Zhu Tian had applied all his lifelong learning from the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s lessons here.

Lu Yang’s expression was solemn. For the first time, I’ve met an opponent whose acting skills are on par with mine.

1. The se or guse is a Chinese plucked instrument. It is said to have evolved to the modern zheng. The guqin and se are said to be the predecessors of the guzheng. The se has been lost to time, and there are efforts to reconstruct it. It was supposed to have 25 strings, but the ancient se displayed in museums no longer have strings. ☜

Chapter 611: Launching Assaults

Everyone held their breath. The descent of the four immortal lightning bolts signified the establishment of the Demon Kingdom, with Zhu Tian as its first ruler.

This journey had not been in vain, for they had witnessed the founding of the Demon Kingdom with their own eyes.

Zhu Tian’s face was stern. He turned his gaze upon the Phoenix Tribe and addressed them in a deep voice. “Phoenix Tribe, the Demon Kingdom is established. Now is the time allies are needed. If you are willing to join now, this monarch promises you will be treated generously!

“If you are unwilling, due to the imminent arrival of the Great Era’s tribulation, for the sake of the demon race, I will have no choice but to employ certain methods!”

The visiting major factions were inwardly shocked. Is Supreme Zhu Tian planning to capitalize on this momentum, subduing the Phoenix Tribe and unifying the Demon Region in one go?

The Phoenix tribespeople felt a chill in their hearts. They had anticipated that Zhu Tian would move against them after establishing the Demon Kingdom, but they hadn’t expected the assault to come so swiftly.

The Phoenix Tribe’s old chieftain, Jiang Mingzi, rose to his feet and flicked his sleeve, snorting coldly. Wisps of flames drifted out from his body as he assumed a defensive stance. “Supreme Lord Zhu Tian, don’t think I’m unaware of your intentions—unify the Demon Region, unify the East Sea, and the Demon Kingdom will leap to become the greatest faction in the world. Your subsequent plan is to attack Great Xia and the Buddhist Kingdom!

“By then, aside from your Dijiang Tribe, any other race will be cannon fodder, dragged to the frontlines to battle, only to satisfy your ambitions!”

Zhu Tian released an oppressive aura combined from his own and that of the ten Transcendent Tribulation demon emperors. The oppressive aura pressed down like a towering mountain upon Jiang Mingzi, causing his bones to creak audibly.

His expression was icy, his gaze tinged with contempt as he watched Jiang Mingzi struggle desperately. “You, junior, have no manners! Never mind you, even Jiang Lianyi would have to address this monarch as ‘fellow Daoist’ if she saw me! Your knowledge is shallow, and you haven’t experienced the events of antiquity, so you’re unable to share my perspective. You know nothing of the true horrors of the Great Era’s tribulation! How are you qualified to speculate on my thoughts?!

“You pit me against the entire world based on nothing but unfounded drivel. You really don’t know how the character for ‘death’ is written!” Zhu Tian emitted a terrifying aura. His fury stemmed not from Jiang Mingzi’s wild speculation; on the contrary, it was because Jiang Mingzi’s conjecture was correct.

With the Demon Kingdom newly founded, its foundation was unstable. It was not yet able to face two formidable enemies like Great Xia and the Buddhist Kingdom simultaneously. He had to feign outrage and denounce Jiang Mingzi’s words as utter nonsense.

I didn’t expect the Phoenix Tribe to have clever individuals too. A pity their cleverness was used in the wrong place!

Jiang Mingzi subtly slipped a hand into the front of his robe. He still possessed several supreme treasures left by his ancient ancestor, capable of delivering a ruthless blow to Zhu Tian in a critical moment.

Two figures appeared, standing shoulder to shoulder beside Jiang Mingzi.

“That’s the Demon Region Dragon Tribe’s old ancestor!”

“And from the East Sea Dragon Tribe too!”

The Demon Region’s Dragon and Phoenix tribes shared glory and loss. If the Demon Kingdom subjugated the Phoenix Tribe, the Dragon Tribe would be next. They could not simply stand by and watch Zhu Tian treat the Phoenix Tribe this way.

The two Dragon tribes had sent Fusion cultivators to attend the ceremony on the surface, but two Transcendent Tribulation cultivators had secretly come.

Together, the Dragon and Phoenix tribes had three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators!

“Overestimating your capabilities.” Zhu Tian sneered. At my command, the ten Transcendent Tribulation great demons will fight it out with the three Dragon and Phoenix Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. Once these three are defeated, branding them with master-servant marks will be straightforward.

His battle strategy was like rolling a snowball—controlling every enemy he defeated and allowing his own influence to grow larger and larger. He dared to announce himself the “Number One Below Immortals” by borrowing the words of those in ancient times; this was the source of his confidence. With myself and ten Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, victory is guaranteed even if I face an ancient immortal!

However, Zhu Tian also dared not act rashly. Among these three individuals was a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator from the East Sea Dragon Tribe. If he truly attacked a member of their tribe, conquering the East Sea in the future would likely be fraught with difficulties.

Both parties sank into a stalemate for a moment.

Fortunately for Zhu Tian, he had long anticipated this scenario.

“Haha! The demons have established a nation and are on the verge of unification. How could such a momentous event occur without our Heavenly Court Creed?” Someone below the stage laughed heartily.

Those nearby quickly moved aside, leaving a circular space. In the center was Young Creed Leader Lu and a black-cloaked figure.

The two leaped into the air, landing upon the heavenly altar. Though they were only two people, they faintly formed a tripartite standoff.

“Who are you?!” Zhu Tian frowned, looking at these two figures in displeasure.

“It’s Young Creed Leader Lu of the Heavenly Court Creed!”

“It’s him! He came too!”

“Makes sense. Supreme Lord Zhu Tian is an ancient half-immortal. It would be strange if the Heavenly Court Creed didn’t show up.”

“It’s said that the Heavenly Court Creed’s origins lie in the ancient Heavenly Court Creed, presided over by Dou Heavenly Sovereign—a true immortal!”

“Is this a war between ancient factions?”

“Who’s the one in black robes? Also a Heavenly King protector?”

“It’s possible!”

The crowd below the stage grew excited. The appearance of the Heavenly Court Creed made the situation even more chaotic, and the audience wondered if a fight would break out.

Mu Baiyi and Vice Creed Leader Shi hid within the crowd, finally witnessing the Heavenly Court Creed’s entrance.

“The Heavenly Court Creed indeed came. Young Creed Leader Lu was already in the Demon Region when Supreme Lord Zhu Tian sent invitations to the various major factions. His appearance here in the Demon Region at such a critical juncture must be due to ulterior motives!”

“Exactly. But we simply don’t know who that black-cloaked figure is. If they’re merely a Heavenly King protector, they probably can’t handle this situation. To stand as Zhu Tian’s equal, could it be that the creed leader of the Heavenly Court Creed has come?”

The two discussed in whispers. Although the Dijiang Tribe hadn’t invited them, it didn’t prevent them from coming to watch the spectacle.

In the plan that Young Creed Leader Lu had given the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, one item was “External Connections with the Demon Region.” Initially, we were puzzled. With so many demon races, who were we supposed to connect with?

Now the answer is revealed. With Zhu Tian unifying the Demon Region, we need to connect with the Demon Kingdom!

“Could this also have been within Young Creed Leader Lu’s predictions...or if we push it further, could the Demon Kingdom’s establishment by Zhu Tian also be the work of the Heavenly Court Creed?”

The two exchanged a glance, noticing the fear in each other’s eyes. This is merely the young creed leader, yet he already possesses such terrifying shrewdness. What kind of figure must the sect leader be?!

Terrifying.

The corners of Zhu Tian’s mouth lifted in a cold smirk. “Heavenly Court? A meaningless thing!” The Heavenly Court was something fabricated by the Four Ancient Immortals. How could it possibly be real?

Keen observers detected the hostility in Zhu Tian’s tone. He doesn’t seem to...acknowledge the Heavenly Court Creed?

Just as Lu Yang was about to improvise a few more lines, a voice dripping with disdain rang out. It came from the Dijiang Tribe’s section of the main seating area.

“How is it that any stray and dog can simply enter the heavenly altar as and when they please?” The voice’s owner pushed off with both feet, flying onto the heavenly altar. His chin was slightly raised as he looked down on Lu Yang derisively.

“So you’re that legendary Young Creed Leader Lu, who fought to a draw with the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Lu Yang. The seemingly impressive Young Creed Leader Lu is actually hardly remarkable in person!”

“In my view, whether it’s you or Lu Yang, you’re both overhyped geniuses, nothing more than monkeys proclaiming themselves kings during the tiger’s absence in the mountain.

“You are...?”

“Zhu Yunwu!”

Zhu Yunwu, the personal disciple of Supreme Lord Zhu Tian and the Dijiang Tribe’s peerless prodigy!

Chapter 612: One-Sided Suppression

Lu Yang paid no heed to the nonsense Zhu Yunwu was spouting. Raising his sword, he snickered. “What an arrogant junior. If you refuse to accept this, why not settle it through a duel?”

“Fine!” What do I, Zhu Yunwu, have to fear?! Not to mention that this Young Creed Leader Lu is an impostor; even if the real one were here, I wouldn’t be the slightest bit afraid!

Zhu Yunwu cut an imposing and handsome figure. His clothes were so bright they seemed to gleam white. Every part of his appearance was immaculately groomed, down to his neatly trimmed nails.

Some demon maidens who admired him screamed at the sight of their beloved.

“Big Brother Zhu is here!” The prodigies of the Demon Alliance were thrilled to see Zhu Yunwu making such a powerful entrance, his demeanor alone rivaling that of the young creed leader of the Heavenly Court Creed.

“Zhu Yunwu. Tch, why is he here?” Ao Yue clicked his tongue, reluctant to face him.

“Is this Zhu Yunwu very powerful?” Meng Jingzhou transmitted an auditory message to Jiang Shishi.

This was a moment that would decide the Phoenix Tribe’s fate. Jiang Shishi stared nervously at the altar, her palms sweating. Meng Jingzhou’s question temporarily diverted her attention. “Extremely powerful, even more powerful than me or Ao Yue! When he debuted, he wasn’t particularly remarkable. At best, he was on par with someone like Qin Feng, nowhere near me or Ao Yue.

But half a year ago, Zhu Yunwu appeared and challenged the prodigies of the various tribes one by one. Even Ao Yue and I were defeated by him.”

“He became that powerful so suddenly?”

Jiang Shishi shook her head. “It wasn’t sudden. I only learned afterward that he had been taken in as a disciple by Supreme Lord Zhu Tian since childhood. He was always powerful; his previous losses to Ao Yue and me were because he had been biding his time and concealing his abilities.

“Half a year ago, Supreme Lord Zhu Tian emerged and began operating covertly within the Demon Region to unify the demon race. That’s when Zhu Yunwu revealed his true strength!”

She sighed. “The personal disciple of a half-immortal is truly fearsome. In terms of innate talent, Ao Yue and I are no weaker than Zhu Yunwu. But his shifu is Supreme Lord Zhu Tian—this is where the gap lies. Supreme Lord Zhu Tian is a terrifying existence who rose during the glorious ancient era of prodigies and lived until now. His knowledge and experience likely surpass that of both my and Ao Yue’s shifu combined.”

~~~

Zhu Tian was more than willing to let Young Creed Leader Lu face his own disciple. This way, I can demonstrate the high standards of my tutelage.

The battle of establishing authority is now!

Zhu Tian voluntarily withdrew, ceding the space on the heavenly altar to Lu Yang and Zhu Yunwu.

The Dragon and Phoenix tribes and Jiang Lianyi did the same.

The once lively heavenly altar was left with only two individuals. All eyes were upon them. Everyone wished to know which of these two peerless prodigies was stronger.

Lu Yang drew his sword—the Yaoguang Sword, one of the Seven-Star Sword Set. It measured three feet and four inches, glistening with an inherent glow.

Zhu Yunwu let out a low cry and shifted into his original appearance—six legs and four wings. His steps were light, and his form was agile. He looked like he was dancing, leaving countless afterimages in his wake.

“That’s the Dijiang Tribe’s Stunning Swan Footwork! Moving like a stunning swan, stirring dragons and serpents from the land!” A demon elder recognized Zhu Yunwu’s technique. It’s said that this footwork has been lost to time, with nobody in the Dijiang Tribe capable of performing it. For the young Zhu Yunwu to do so, he must have been taught by Supreme Lord Zhu Tian himself!

Hundreds of thousands of sword qi surged upward from both sides of Lu Yang’s body, swirling with five-colored radiance. It was a breathtaking spectacle that illuminated the heavenly altar.

“Let me see just how formidable this sword cultivator famed for offensive prowess truly is!” Zhu Yunwu’s voice was icy and merciless, laced with a trace of mockery.

His footwork changed again, integrating the movement of his wings into his already nimble steps. His four wings became four swords, slicing through space and sweeping across the ninth level of the heavenly altar like a myth reborn.

Lu Yang answered with his sword. The hundreds of thousands of sword qi transformed into raging tidal waves, crashing down layer upon layer like a magnificent lotus in full bloom.

Boom!

In the clash of the two powerhouses, Zhu Yunwu was overpowered. He was sent flying backward, slamming squarely into the carved railing of the heavenly altar.

“What?!”

The crowd was astonished. Zhu Yunwu was defeated after just one exchange?

Meng Jingzhou looked at Jiang Shishi silently. “This is the fearsome Zhu Yunwu you spoke of?”

Jiang Shishi was dumbfounded, never imagining Zhu Yunwu to lose so quickly.

Zhu Tian was furious. What kind of joke is this? This wasn’t part of the plan! If Zhun Yunwu is humiliated, how do I still establish authority in this authority-establishing battle?

He activated his Incipient Dao Fruit, attempting to forcibly control Lu Yang.

To his horror, no matter how he tried, the other party seemed completely unaffected.

This brat isn’t under control at all!

What exactly are my subordinates doing? Using the Dijiang Command to control a Golden Core cultivator to impersonate Young Creed Leader Lu is such a simple task. Yet they still botched it?

The elderly Dijiang was dripping with cold sweat. He activated the Dijiang Command until it smoked, yet Lu Yang showed no signs of being controlled.

Lu Yang pressed his advantage, executing a sword mantra. The Yaoguang Sword emitted a resplendent stellar light, turning into a meteor that shot toward Zhu Yunwu, who had fallen at the edge. Lu Yang didn’t hold back; he had been going all out from the beginning.

Zhu Yunwu’s head was still spinning from the severe sword blow he had received earlier. Sensing danger, he instinctively rolled over. The Yaoguang Sword grazed past him. It was the closest of the closest shave!

Zhu Yunwu regained his clarity, but still couldn’t figure out what was happening. Wasn’t I told to just go through the motions? That the other party is an imposter and will surely be no match for me?

What was with that sword technique just now?

Damn it! Even the real Young Creed Leader Lu would probably be at this level! freewebnovel.com

Zhu Yunwu was no pretty vase; his battle achievements had been earned through real combat. Although the current situation is outside the plan, now that things have already come to this, I will have to fight for real!

Knowing he could no longer hold back, he unleashed his full power. “Heaven-Treading Step!”

His six legs galloped, treading upon the sky. Each step was frighteningly heavy, causing even the space to shake. This was his strongest trump card, the ultimate move he had used to defeat Ao Yue. Realizing his opponent’s terrifying strength, he was clear that any probing or holding back would only be to his disadvantage. Thus, he decisively employed his ultimate technique.

Zhu Yunwu took two steps and hovered in the air, as if he was ascending an invisible staircase. This wasn’t achieved through spells or wings—rather, these two steps were so fast and heavy that they temporarily compressed the air into a solid state!

Lu Yang recalled the Yaoguang Sword. The sword qi hummed, dazzling in its colorful resplendence. He wielded all kinds of sword techniques effortlessly, a sight that would make even masters of Sword Dao feel ashamed.

The peerless prodigies of the human and demon race clashed once more. The sound shook the heavens, and light blazed intensely, like a sun exploding. In the blink of an eye, the two had exchanged hundreds of moves, their techniques too rapid to follow with the eye.

Their contemporaries gasped at how terrifying and fearsome the two were. Only those Fusion cultivators who could clearly see the process of their battle understood that while Zhu Yunwu was indeed fearsome as a half-immortal’s disciple, Young Creed Leader Lu was even more terrifying—their combat was not an exchange of blows but a one-sided suppression, with Young Creed Leader Lu thrashing Zhu Yunwu!

What terrifying combat prowess this is!

Hundreds of thousands of sword qi swept across everything unbridled. Zhu Yunwu employed several ultimate moves, but it was all in vain. He simply could not withstand Lu Yang’s sword moves.

Even Jiang Lianyi inwardly sighed in amazement. Lu Yang’s talent in Sword Dao is far too fearsome.

Everlasting-jiejie doesn’t know sword techniques, which means Lu Yang’s sword techniques are either self-taught or guided by an expert.

If it’s the latter, that’s understandable.

But if it’s the former, that would be too terrifying.

Chapter 613: Unbeatable at the Golden Core Stage

Swoosh! With a horizontal sweep of the Yaoguang Sword, one of Zhu Yunwu’s wings was severed. It fell to the ground, blood gushing forth.

“Huff, huff, huff...” Zhu Yunwu’s eyes were bloodshot, his handsome face contorted. After hundreds of exchanges, he understood completely—he was no match for his opponent by relying on his own strength alone.

In that case, I have no choice but to use the essence blood Shifu bestowed me.

As Zhu Yunwu wiped the blood from the corner of his mouth, he swallowed a drop of essence blood. This was Zhu Tian’s essence blood and was immensely precious. It allowed Zhu Yunwu to unleash power at the Nascent Soul Stage while still at the Golden Core Stage.

An endless stream of power surged from within his body. The wounds corroded by sword qi sizzled and smoked, healing rapidly. Even his severed wing regenerated, a new one taking its place.

“Again!” Zhu Yun took the initiative, charging at Lu Yang. “Heaven-Treading Step!”

Lu Yang hadn’t expected Zhu Yunwu’s attack to be so ferocious this time. He raised the sword before his chest to block the blow and retreated several steps to disperse the force.

The two became locked in combat once more, but unlike previously, Lu Yang could distinctly feel that Zhu Yunwu was far stronger than he had been. He felt a pang of nostalgia for the finals held in Great Xia.

If an opponent fouled, one could report it to the referee and have them penalized. This isn’t an option now; the referee is on the opponent’s side. Reporting is useless.

Every one of Zhu Yunwu’s strikes was forceful and heavy. Lu Yang shifted from offense to defense, continuously neutralizing Zhu Yunwu’s fierce assaults.

Guarding Word Mantra.

This was a sword move Lu Yang seldom employed. He had always believed the best defense was a fierce offense. But this situation was special. Unless he was a dual physique and sword cultivator, clashing head-on with Zhu Yunwu would only make things difficult for himself.

Zhu Yunwu trod upon the sky, leaping high into the air. His rear four legs accumulated strength before his front hooves smashed down toward Lu Yang with devastating force.

Having anticipated this, Lu Yang evaded in advance, causing Zhu Yunwu to step on empty air.

Zhun Yunwu twisted his body mid-air and altered his trajectory, charging at Lu Yang once again.

Clang! The Yaoguang Sword was sent flying, landing a distance away.

“Let’s see how you fight without your sword!” Zhu Yunwu sneered, assured that victory was within his grasp. He heaved a sigh of relief. Although there were some twists and turns, it’s fine as long as I win.

Qin Feng and the others cheered, having witnessed Young Creed Leader Lu’s defeat.

“I thought this Lu guy had some skill, but it turns out he’s nothing special.”

“I was actually worried about Big Brother Yunwu for a moment there. I really lack discerning eyes.”

“Exactly, exactly. How could Big Brother Yunwu lose?”

Lu Yang looked at his Yaoguang Sword that had been knocked away and scratched his head somewhat awkwardly.

Picking it up is impossible; Zhu Yunwu wouldn’t give me the chance. Should I pick one from the other six swords and continue a war of attrition?

Never mind, let’s listen to the Unbeatable Golden Core.

Lu Yang sighed, acknowledging that the Unbeatable Golden Core’s method was still superior. He took out a pill and swallowed it, feeling a warm current coalesce within his dantian.

~~~

Below the stage, Seventh Elder exclaimed softly, “This pill...”

“Old Seven, you recognize it?” Fifth Elder asked through an auditory message.

“This is the Spring-Revival Yang-Restoration Pill I refined for Lu Yang.”

“It sounds like a pill that restores spirit energy.”

“That’s precisely what it is. This kid has one move that will make him unbeatable among his peers once executed. Even I couldn’t withstand it when I lowered my cultivation to the Golden Core Stage. But this move simply drains too much spirit energy, which is why he asked me to refine the pill.”

“What move?”

Seventh Elder chuckled but didn’t answer.

~~~

“Die!” Zhu Yunwu roared, his four wings beating. He trod the sky and severed souls, sealing off all paths of escape.

Lu Yang retreated two steps, then flipped his right hand. Instantly, the winds shifted and dark clouds churned. The space on the ninth level of the heavenly altar solidified, and Zhu Yunwu’s speed slowed infinitely.

Zhu Yunwu felt his surroundings were no longer like air but seawater. No, it’s even more viscous than seawater, and it’s restricting my movement.

“Look, what is that!” Qin Feng cried out involuntarily, gazing at the sky in a daze.

A colossal hand pierced through the dark clouds, pressing down. Despite its slow movement, it was unavoidable, with nowhere to dodge. This palm didn’t seem to be aimed at the heavenly altar, but at him. A sense of powerlessness washed over him.

“Cosmos in Palm!” Zhu Tian recognized the move at a glance. He watched the scene in disbelief, his spirit platform going blank for an instant.

Is this a joke? Even if this is countless times smaller than the real Cosmos in Palm, this is still a move that can only be executed by Transcendent Tribulation cultivators! How could a Golden Core cultivator possibly perform it?!

Just how terrifying must his talent for spells be?

The truth was laid bare before him. He had to believe it even if he didn’t want to. A Golden Core cultivator performing a theoretically impossible move meant no Golden Core cultivator could withstand this move!

The major factions could no longer remain seated. This move had overturned their understanding. They saw that Young Creed Leader Lu had consumed a pill to restore spirit energy, not temporarily boost his combat power.

In other words, this was his true level of ability.

He was unbeatable at the Golden Core Stage.

This move was a bona fide divine spatial ability. It could seal the space beneath the palm, which was why Zhu Yunwu couldn’t move.

Boom! The single hand blotted out the sky and sealed space, covering the heavenly altar.

Gulp.

Qin Feng and the others swallowed hard upon witnessing this scene. The strength displayed by this move was too horrifying. If Zhu Yunwu was the idol whom the Demon Alliance prodigies chased after, this move was a peak that filled them with despair, extinguishing even their desire to chase after it and catch up.

It was utterly despairing.

Among the audience watching the battle was Kong Hao, who had once been Young Creed Leader Lu’s opponent. After falling into a disadvantageous position, he had used the power of the old Taowu and was punished by the referee.

“Teacher Ji, could I withstand this move?”

“I advise you to quickly learn body takeover methods, lest I have to die alongside you.”

Witnessing this scene, the five elders secretly discussed among themselves.

“This is almost catching up to Niece Yun’s level at the Golden Core Stage, right?”

“More or less.”

The giant hand vanished, and dust billowed, obscuring the view of the heavenly altar. The altar’s array prevented others from probing with their spiritual consciousness.

“Is Zhu Yunwu dead or alive?”

“He’s moving; he’s still alive!”

Originally, people had been speculating on who would win the battle between the two.

But after Cosmos of Palm was unleashed, people only wanted to know if Zhu Yunwu was dead or alive.

Merely surviving was already an achievement.

“Didn’t expect this, did you? I’m still alive.”

Wings quivered, dispersing the dust. Zhu Yunwu surprisingly appeared vibrant and full of energy, his injuries far lighter than anyone had imagined.

“Broke through to the Nascent Soul Stage?” Lu Yang’s control over the battlefield was exceedingly strong. He had noticed that upon executing Village in Palm, a unique burst of force had erupted from Zhu Yunwu’s location, negating most of the attack.

This was a breakthrough to the Nascent Soul Stage.

“I’ll give you some credit for having discerning eyes.” Despite Zhu Yunwu’s unforgiving remark, he was inwardly filled with lingering fear.

If I hadn’t broken through in that life-or-death moment, I might have died under that palm. Given Shifu’s cold-blooded nature, he wouldn’t have cared whether I lived or died.

“How’s that! Let’s see how you fight now!” Zhu Yuwu seized the initiative once more.

That previous move had exhausted his spirit energy. He’s already an arrow at the end of its flight, a spent force and no longer a threat. I will absolutely not give him another chance to ingest a pill.

In contrast, I have broken through mid-battle and am now brimming with spirit energy.

The balance of power has shifted.

“Heh.” Lu Yang couldn’t help but shake his head and laugh.

“What are you laughing at?” Zhu Yunwu was displeased.

Lu Yang slowly raised his head, his gaze like a torch that could seemingly see through a person’s heart. Zhu Yunwu grew flustered under his stare.

“You don’t actually think you’re the only one who can break through to the Nascent Soul Stage, do you?”

Chapter 614: Nascent Soul Breakthrough

Zhu Yunwu’s pupils constricted. The feathers on his four wings stood on end, and his smile froze on his face.

As Lu Yang’s opponent, he knew all too well just how formidable Lu Yang was. If he’s allowed to break through to the Nascent Soul Stage, I’m afraid that even burning my essence blood wouldn’t be enough to defeat him!

Lu Yang strode toward Zhu Yunwu, his footsteps echoing—tap, tap, tap. After each step was a slight pause. The sound didn’t seem to come from his feet stepping on the heavenly altar but from trampling upon Zhu Yunwu’s spirit platform. His attitude was leisurely, as if he was strolling through the garden, not bothering with Zhu Yunwu.

He had originally been at the Ninth-Layer Golden Core cultivation realm. If he wanted to break through, he could have done so at any time. However, his plan had been to tour the Demon Kingdom first and return to the Dao-Seeking Sect to break through slowly. It was, after all, a major realm breakthrough—he felt it deserved a sense of ceremony.

Unfortunately, there was a change in plans.

Seeing the situation turn dire, Zhu Yunwu let out a low cry and attacked first, seizing the initiative! I mustn’t let him break through successfully!

His four wings vibrated, and his six hooves trod upon the sky, causing space to shake. Zhu Yunwu fought with everything on the line, resembling a torrential mudslide crashing down.

Completely unprepared, Lu Yang was sent flying and slammed into the heavenly altar’s railing.

“Huff, huff... So you’re really at the end of your rope.” Zhu Yunwu laughed heartily, relaxing immediately.

That’s right. The heaven-covering huge hand seal has already depleted all his spirit energy. Where would he get the strength to break through? I was too nervous.

Lu Yang spat out a mouthful of blood. The bloody spittle landed on the pristine white liuli-glazed jade, particularly conspicuous. He wiped the blood from the corner of his mouth and stood up, walking toward Zhu Yunwu with that same confident smile of assured victory still on his visage.

“Again.”

Zhu Yunwu’s eyes instantly reddened. Fear spread through his heart. Like a maddened bull, he launched a frenzied assault on Lu Yang.

Each time, Lu Yang didn’t dodge, meeting Zhu Yunwu’s strikes head-on. But with each of Zhu Yunwu’s attacks, the distance Lu Yang was knocked back shortened.

The last time, Lu Yang had only retreated half a step.

Amidst the repeated impacts, cracks appeared on the surface of his golden core. A milky white light spilled from the fissures, rapidly healing Lu Yang’s injuries.

Zhu Yunwu charged up for another strike.

Lu Yang finally moved.

He extended his right palm and exerted force abruptly, pressing down on Zhu Yunwu’s head and forcibly stopping this attack.

Zhu Yunwu looked up at Lu Yang with a face of utter disbelief, only to be greeted by a face wreathed in smiles...and a Lu Yang at the Nascent Soul Stage.

Bones cracked and popped. In that short span of time, Lu Yang had undergone a round of tempering his bones. His physical constitution was no longer the same as before, like the difference between clouds and mud.

His essence, qi, and mind had merged into one. Using the accumulated Unbeatable Momentum as a catalyst, they intertwined within his dantian and gave birth to a bizarre and wondrous power.

The Unbeatable Golden Core had shattered completely. Abundant spirit energy burst forth, coursing through all his meridians. A frightening vortex of spirit energy formed above the heavenly altar, madly pouring down into Lu Yang’s body, replenishing his withered meridians and nourishing the newly born infant.

Within his dantian, an infant the size of a fingertip curled into a ball, emitting a peaceful, milky white glow. It accepted the spirit energy from the outside world and continuously grew until it reached three inches in height and could move freely. Only then did it stop absorbing.

Unlike a real born child, the nascent soul was pale and tender, its face full of excitement and a joyous smile.

“Is that all?” Lu Yang’s muscles tensed. His body was like a large dragon with power thrumming through it. He delivered a punch squarely into Zhu Yunwu’s face.

“How is this possible?!” Zhu Yunwu couldn’t believe it. How can my opponent not only break through to the Nascent Soul at will, but also possess such power immediately after breaking through? Doesn’t he need to consolidate his foundation and undergo the process of burnishing his nascent soul?!

When ordinary cultivators broke through to the Nascent Soul Stage, their cultivation would be unstable, and they would require time to stabilize it.

But Lu Yang was the wielder of the strongest golden core and never lost a single battle at the Golden Core Stage. The Unbeatable Momentum he formed from his continuous victories could directly help consolidate his foundation, so he had no need to go into seclusion to stabilize his cultivation.

Zhu Yunwu had never encountered such a situation. Caught off guard by Lu Yang’s rapid succession of changes, he missed the initiative. Lu Yang didn’t even need to use his sword techniques. By relying on just his fists and feet, he could suppress Zhu Yunwu.

“I will definitely win!” Zhu Yunwu went berserk. Disregarding the consequences, he burned his essence blood to temporarily boost his combat power.

The surrounding crowd gasped in alarm. Zhu Yunwu’s foundation was unstable. If he burned his essence blood to break through at this moment, even if he won this round, it would likely be extremely difficult for him to make further breakthroughs in the future!

A faint silhouette of Zhu Tian appeared behind Zhu Yunwu. As the ancient ancestor of the Dijiang Tribe and their most powerful existence, Zhu Tian was the source of their bloodline. The appearance of Zhu Tian’s phantom was one of the characteristics of burning essence blood—borrowing power from ancestors to defeat a powerful foe!

Zhu Yunwu roared, completely unhinged.

Lu Yang took out a pill and flicked it into Zhu Yunwu’s mouth with his index finger while the latter roared.

Zhu Yunwu wanted to spit it out, but Lu Yang stepped forward and pushed his chin upward. By reflex, Zhu Yunwu swallowed the pill.

“What did you feed me?!” Zhu Yunwu cried out in horror. He felt the power gained from burning his essence blood dissipating rapidly. This pill had forcibly interrupted the process of his essence blood combustion.

Lu Yang beamed as he explained. “Realm-Breaking Pill. It can help someone at the Foundation Establishment Stage break through to the Golden Core Stage. At the same time, it can also help someone at the Nascent Soul break through to the Golden Core Stage.”

When Lu Yang had asked Seventh Elder to concoct the Spring-Revival Yang-Restoration Pill, the latter had just successfully concocted the Realm-Breaking Pill. To celebrate, Seventh Elder had gifted one to Lu Yang.

Zhu Yunwu’s heart sank. As I thought, not only is the power from burning my essence blood disappearing, but even my cultivation realm is plummeting!

He was completely flustered. How am I supposed to fight like this?

“Trash!” Zhu Tian was incensed. I’m now certain that the one on the heavenly altar is the real Young Creed Leader Lu. Where else would such a peerless genius appear from?

Regardless, Zhu Yunwu absolutely can’t lose here.

This is a matter of face and dignity!

This is the very first battle after the founding of the Demon Kingdom. If we get defeated by the Heavenly Court Creed, this humiliation will be the ridicule of my lifetime.

He separated a wisp of his divine mind and attached it to Zhu Yunwu’s body.

“Shifu...”

“Trash! Let me handle this!” Zhu Tian temporarily took control of Zhu Yunwu’s body, halting the fall of his cultivation realm.

“Rise!” He commanded softly.

Zhu Yunwu’s cultivation realm returned to the Nascent Soul Stage!

Lu Yang had just learned from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy that his opponent had changed from Zhu Yunwu to Supreme Lord Zhu Tian. He was utterly exasperated. Is it not enough that your Demon Kingdom’s referee is biased? Now even the referee is taking the field?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was indignant about the unfairness on Lu Yang’s behalf. She rolled up her sleeves and charged forward. “This grandson Zhu Tian has been cunning and slippery since the first time I met him. How dare he fight like this now? Step aside and let me handle this!”

Lu Yang invoked the deity to possess him, granting the Everlasting Immortal Fairy free rein to act.

Meanwhile, Zhu Tian was berating Zhu Yunwu inside the mental space.

“Disgraceful brat! You can’t even defeat an opponent like this and have to force your shifu to intervene personally. Watch closely how your shifu fights!”

Zhu Tian controlled Zhu Yunwu’s body and shook off his lethargy. He was prepared to counterattack when he was met with Lu Yang’s fist smashing into his face with a clang, leaving him disoriented. He could even faintly hear something about an “Immortal Fairy Fist Technique.”

Zhu Yunwu watched this scene without uttering a word, silently and humbly learning from it.

Chapter 615: Just Because You Haven’t Heard of It, Does That Mean the Heavenly Court Doesn’t Exist?

The Immortal Fairy Fist Technique rained down upon him with a series of pops and cracks. No defensive method was effective. It was as his opponent could see through all his weaknesses. Every punch landed on a vulnerable point, causing excruciating pain.

The crowd of onlookers didn’t know that the identities of the two combatants on the heavenly altar had silently been elevated, but it was plain to them that Zhu Yunwu was suffering an even more brutal beating than before.

Zhu Yunwu studied his shifu’s moves intently, feeling he was gaining great insight. Perhaps this is Shifu’s purpose.

Seeing that defensive methods were useless, Zhu Tian changed his combat tactics, adjusting his posture to make the blows less painful. What struck Zhu Tian as strangest was that his opponent’s moves felt terribly familiar, as if he had been beaten the same way back in the ancient era. But upon careful recollection, he couldn’t match them to any opponent in his memory.

Strange.

The pain yanked him out of his memories and back to reality. This can’t continue. I have to create distance and make a comeback.

He deliberately revealed a flaw, baiting the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to attack. As he expected, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy took the bait and aimed for his vulnerable points. Seizing his opportunity, Zhu Tian jumped to the right.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had anticipated this. She also jumped to the right and continued pummeling Zhu Tian. I’ve long figured out all of Zhu Tian’s attack patterns.

After eight or nine attempts, Zhu Tian finally flew into the sky, panting heavily as he put distance between himself and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. He looked at her, an inexplicable fear gripping his heart.

This wasn’t fear born from the earlier beating, but a remnant of the ancient era—a fear hidden deep within his heart.

Zhu Tian’s eyes turned icy. He twisted his round body, his steps shifting and his four wings beating like instruments playing in harmony. There was an indescribable coordinated beauty to it, as if hundreds of people were performing together—different instruments, different roles, and different rhythms—yet it sounded melodious, as if it was always meant to be so.

This was one of his unique arts. Its power was astonishing; only those at the Nascent Soul Stage barely qualified to execute it.

Above the heavenly altar, gigantic waves surged, resembling the great flood that ended the ancient era. The waters carried an intent of corrosion and annihilation. Even a single drop would cause skin to sizzle and smoke upon contact. If one was unfortunate enough to be engulfed by the flood, not even their bones would remain.

“He’s summoning a flood! What dance is Zhu Yunwu performing? Does anyone recognize it?”

“It seems to be the legendary Dance of Immortal Fall and World Destruction. It’s Supreme Lord Zhu Tian’s unique dance; only he can perform it. That’s no ordinary flood; it’s the cataclysmic deluge from the ancient era, which once wiped out numerous stars!”

“Looks like Supreme Lord Zhu Tian holds this disciple in very high regard.”

“This Young Creed Leader Lu is also no simple figure. He’s been suppressing Zhu Yunwu and beating him from start to finish. The fame of ancient geniuses is indeed something else.”

Hearing the discussion below, Lu Yang grew somewhat nervous. “This is called the Dance of Immortal Fall and World Destruction? Could it be that a half-immortal actually died under this move?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hand. “Only the name sounds intimidating. In reality, it’s nothing special.

“During the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s lessons, he had mentioned that for those at the Transcendent Tribulation or half-immortal stages, regardless of a technique’s actual power, its name must sound awe-inspiring. He called this ‘gaining the upper hand through prestige and momentum.’ I don’t believe in that. A technique’s effectiveness is what matters most. As for the name, anything will do.”

Lu Yang, “...”

The world-ending deluge coalesced and churned in the air. The faster the four wings beat, the more floodwaters were generated. Toward the end, the waters swelled until they blotted out the sky, even heavier than storm clouds. If they poured down, the entire heavenly altar would inevitably be submerged. The flood’s scope was so massive that even attempting to flee by flying would be futile.

“Go!” Zhu Tian beat his four wings. The world-ending deluge lost its supportive force and came crashing down toward the heavenly altar with a thunderous roar.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was not at all afraid. She pointed her index finger at a point in space, producing a small “pop.” The moisture in the air vanished abruptly, as if an invisible hand was moving upstream, erasing all the water above the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, including the world-ending deluge.

“Water-Repelling Mantra.”

“How is this possible?!” Zhu Tian’s eyes widened in incredulity. My proud technique was dismantled just like that?

Water-Repelling Mantra? This kind of spell has been lost to time; only ancient cultivators would know it. Could it be that my opponent really hails from the ancient era?

“Oh no!”

Above the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was not only the world-ending deluge but also Zhu Tian himself.

Zhu Tian felt the water in his body rapidly disappearing. He withered and became as desiccated as a corpse that had been dead for a year. If I force myself to move, my body might just fall apart.

“La—warm spring, flowers bloom, life awakens—” Zhu Tian sang loudly. This was the Song of Spring from the Ballad of the Four Seasons. Spring symbolized revival, enabling one to restore their peak condition. After his revival, it only took him two hundred years to return to his peak—a recovery for which the Song of Spring deserved much credit.

“He does have a knack for singing,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy muttered. Zhu Tian often sang to liven the atmosphere before the sermon sessions began in the past.

She soared into the air, riding the clouds and mist, continuing her battle with Zhu Tian amidst the skies.

The Immortal Fairy Fist Technique was ever-changing and all-encompassing. Zhu Tian’s various attacks were deftly neutralized by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy with ingenious methods. Her fist technique had originated from the various herb fists. Herbs could be medicine and poison; in the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s hands, she could switch between them at will. Even if Zhu Tian hadn’t forgotten the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s combat style, he would still have been miserably thrashed when battling her as peers in the ancient era.

“Enough!”

Zhu Tian could no longer control himself. A wisp of his spiritual consciousness returned to his original body. Hollering at the top of his voice, he brutally terminated the contest. The Nascent Soul Stage was too distant a memory for him; he had long forgotten the methods that could be employed at the Nascent Soul Stage and couldn’t defeat Young Creed Leader Lu.

Zhu Tian was as massive as a mountain. As his four wings vibrated, he whipped up a hurricane and flew onto the heavenly altar. The hurricane sent the crowd reeling, with many being blown off their feet.

Ten Transcendent Tribulation demon emperors followed close behind, encircling Lu Yang.

Zhu Tian revealed a cruel smile, looking at Lu Yang as if he was already a dead man. “Despite roaming the ancient era as I pleased, I’ve never heard of any ‘Heavenly Court.’ You, a junior, fabricated a nonexistent Heavenly Court and call yourself Young Creed Leader Lu, sullying the ancient era’s reputation! Do you find this monarch, an archaic cultivator, beneath you?

“Considering that your cultivation journey wasn’t easy, I was initially unwilling to expose your identity. But you have repeatedly caused trouble at the founding ceremony of our Demon Kingdom! Where does that leave our demon race’s face and our Demon Region’s dignity?

As soon as Zhu Tian’s words left his mouth, the crowd below erupted into an uproar, shocked that Supreme Lord Zhu Tian would expose such a secret.

“There was no Heavenly Court in ancient times? Does that mean the Heavenly Court Creed is fake?”

“Then who exactly is this Young Creed Leader Lu...”

“How’s that possible?! If the Heavenly Court Creed is fake, then was Dou Heavenly Sovereign defeating Great Yu cultivators also fake?”

“That’s not impossible?! Maybe it’s a play orchestrated by Great Yu cultivators to divert the world’s attention!”

“Supreme Lord Zhu Tian is a figure of immense stature; he definitely wouldn’t lie about something like this!”

Mu Baiyi and Shi Huagu exchanged a glance, doubt rising in their hearts.

The Heavenly Court Creed is fake? How’s that possible?! Then who’s the person cooperating with us, and what is their origin?

But with Supreme Lord Zhu Tian’s words, they felt compelled to believe it.

“Could we have been deceived?”

While the crowd was abuzz with discussions, a cold voice resounded throughout the entire Demon City. The voice seemed to be laughing, mocking the foolishness of the world and Zhu Tian’s ignorance.

“Zhu Tian, just because you haven’t heard of it, does that mean the Heavenly Court doesn’t exist?”

“Who’s speaking?!” Zhu Tian scanned his surroundings nervously, releasing his spiritual consciousness to scan the area. This voice was eerily familiar, causing his hair to stand on end.

A figure in black robes flew out, landing lightly on the heavenly altar and standing protectively in front of Lu Yang.

“Who are you?!” Zhu Tian demanded, wary as though he was facing a formidable foe. He had a sense of foreboding and stared fixedly at the black-robed figure.

The black-robed figure pushed back their hood, revealing a peerless and exquisite face. The person looked at Zhu Tian with an ambiguous smile, their gaze containing disdain and contempt.

“One of the Heavenly Court Creed’s Four Regents, the Great Emperor of Extreme Southern Nirvana—Jiang Lianyi.”

Chapter 616: Astonishing the World

“One of the Heavenly Court Creed’s Four Regents, the Great Emperor of Extreme Southern Nirvana—Jiang Lianyi.” Her voice was soft as she introduced herself. Silence fell over the entire place the moment she pushed back her hood, allowing Jiang Lianyi’s self-introduction to be heard clearly.

“The Phoenix Ancient Ancestor?”

I tested him with ancient secrets and used lie-detection spells; his identity is real! It seems to me that Supreme Lord Zhu Tian is just a sore loser! He only said that out of desperation!”

An uproar broke out among the crowd. Let alone minor cultivators, even long-renowned experts of the cultivation world could not remain seated. They rose in shock, staring fixedly at Jiang Lianyi and searing this scene into their minds. Even if the human cultivators from the Buddhist Kingdom and Great Xia hadn’t seen Jiang Lianyi’s appearance before, they had heard of her reputation.

This was a puissant personage famous since the ancient era, far more famous than Zhu Tian. Over three hundred thousand years of history, she had become close to a deity-like existence for the demon race.

The faith of the demon race was the Demon Immortal, whose appearance was unknown. Thus, Jiang Lianyi was the one whom the demons would respond to with a single call.

The demons’ reactions were even more intense. They were so excited that their brains were flushed with blood. They floundered in panic, tongue-tied and their bodies trembling uncontrollably. Many demons had tears in their eyes as they knelt on the ground emotionally, crying out that an immortal had manifested and paying their respects to Jiang Lianyi. Even those at the level of a great demon king were no exceptions. They felt genuine reverence for Jiang Lianyi from the bottom of their hearts, kneeling and bowing to her to pray for her protection.

It was as if an ancient myth had been reborn.

Zhu Tian relied on the power of his Incipient Dao Fruit to make the demons submit, while Jiang Lianyi made the demons switch allegiance with her mere presence. The members of the Demon Alliance were wavering, uncertain which side to lean toward.

The Transcendent Tribulation cultivator from the East Sea Dragon Tribe rubbed his eyes vigorously, wondering if his old eyes were failing him and he was hallucinating. He couldn’t believe the scene before his eyes. The Old Dragon Emperor had thought the Phoenix Tribe was in danger and specifically sent him to aid them.

Help them my ass! From what it looks like now, the Phoenix Tribe’s ancient ancestor is still around. How could anything happen to the Phoenix Tribe? This is an existence on par with our own Ancient Ancestor. Unless an immortal appears, who could oppose her?

The Transcendent Tribulation cultivators from the East Sea Dragon Tribe and the Demon Region Dragon Tribe looked toward Jiang Mingzi and the Phoenix Tribe. They wanted to know if the Phoenix Tribe was aware of Jiang Lianyi’s existence and whether this was their trump card.

Turning their heads, they saw Jiang Mingzi weeping like a child, wiping away tears and snot.

As the individual with the highest cultivation in the Phoenix Tribe, he was their pillar and backbone. Every major matter depended on him to make a decision. Many demons eyed the treasures the Phoenix Tribe possessed like tigers circling their prey. A single misstep from him could consign the entire tribe into irredeemable ruin; the pressure was immense.

Zhu Tian forcing the Phoenix Tribe to choose sides had pushed him into a dilemma. But now, the Ancient Ancestor has returned. There’s finally someone above me. My burden can be laid down at last.

The Phoenix tribesmen’s reactions were even more extreme than Jiang Mingzi’s. They were all crying their eyes out. Some couldn’t even maintain their human forms, transforming into phoenixes representing the Five Virtues.[1] Their phoenix cries resounded unceasingly throughout the Demon City. As for the younger-generation prodigies, the moment they saw Jiang Lianyi, their spirit platforms went blank, and they lost all perception of the outside world.

Only Meng Jingzhou, who had met Jiang Lianyi before, could remain clear-headed. “Damn it! Why am I not the one standing on the heavenly altar? I could beat a fellow like Zhu Yunwu too.” We had agreed to return to the sect together and break through to the Nascent Soul Stage. This grandson Lu Yang doesn’t keep his word, breaking through mid-battle and stealing the spotlight.

The old Taowu sealed within Kong Hao was also stupefied. The changes in the Demon Region were completely beyond his imagination. I just wanted to witness the Demon Kingdom’s founding and see how my enemies are faring. How did it turn into this situation?

Besides, a mighty figure like the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor is only “one of the Four Regents” in the Heavenly Court. Just how terrifying must the strength of the ancient Heavenly Court be?

Seeing everyone’s reaction, the five elders felt slightly comforted. This is how it should be! It’s not just us who reacted like this upon seeing the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor. Everyone is the same.

Deathly silence draped over the heavenly altar.

Among the ten demon emperors, some had genuinely pledged allegiance to Zhu Tian, while others were controlled by his Incipient Dao Fruit. Regardless of which case they fell under, the moment they saw Jiang Lianyi, they felt the timidity of a junior facing a senior.

Zhu Tian had even broken out in a cold sweat. The current demons may not know Jiang Lianyi’s identity, but as an ancient great demon, how could I not know?

The wife of the Qilin Immortal.

These few words alone can elevate Jiang Lianyi’s status to another level, totally overshadowing me.

Damn it! Why did Jiang Lianyi have to pop up at such a critical juncture?

In terms of one-on-one combats, Zhu Tian was not afraid. I admit that Jiang Lianyi was strong and ranked in the first tier of half-immortals. But I’ve controlled so many demons, and my Dao Fruit is near completion. Our strength is comparable.

Calm down, calm down. Zhu Tian took in deep breaths repeatedly, settling his mood to ponder the issue with a cool head and organize his thoughts.

Hasn’t it already been confirmed? I haven’t felt the suppression of the Qilin Immortal’s Dao Fruit, which means the Qilin Immortal has perished. With the Demon Kingdom established, I have a powerful army. A mere Jiang Lianyi won’t stir up waves. If not for this, I wouldn’t have dared to borrow the Qilin Immortal’s name at the founding ceremony to justify my position.

“What, you don’t recognize me anymore?” Upon seeing Zhu Tian lost in thought, Jiang Lianyi spoke with a cold sneer, showing no mercy.

Zhu Tian was unwilling to fall out with Jiang Lianyi now. He assumed human form and cupped his fists with a smile. “Greetings, Fellow Daoist Jiang. It has been three hundred thousand years since we last met. Your elegant demeanor remains as ever.

“However, why haven’t I heard of the Heavenly Court? When did you join it, fellow Daoist?” Zhu Tian wanted to control the Phoenix Tribe and use them as pawns. He undoubtedly also coveted the supreme treasures she had left for them.

How could Jiang Lianyi possibly give Zhu Tian face under such circumstances? “Since when must I report to you about joining the Heavenly Court? Let alone you, even the Qilin Immortal wouldn’t dare to meddle in my affairs like this!”

Hearing the two’s conversation, the crowd below once again erupted into heated discussions, their expressions alit with excitement. A layer of the ancient era’s mysterious veil was lifted publicly!

“The ancient Heavenly Court truly existed?!”

“Why have I never heard of it? I thought the Heavenly Court recorded in books was just something the ancient immortals wrote for fun.”

“This Young Creed Leader Lu was the bona fide number one prodigy of ancient times. No wonder he defeated Zhu Yunwu.”

“Young Creed Leader Lu is a disciple of Dou Heavenly Sovereign—an immortal’s disciple!”

The crowd marveled at Young Creed Leader Lu’s talent and luck.

He has such a great shifu.

Zhu Tian frowned. “What exactly is this Heavenly Court...”

The corners of Jiang Lianyi’s mouth lifted in a mocking smile as she looked down at Zhu Tian. “The Heavenly Court is an existence known only among immortals; it’s related to the secrets of immortals. If I weren’t the Qilin Immortal’s wife, I wouldn’t have been qualified to be privy to it.

“As for you, do you think you are qualified?”

Chapter 617: Senior Brother Lu and I Studied Under Dou Heavenly Sovereign

Zhu Tian was rendered speechless, his expression shifting unpredictably like a storm. Despite his current bluster and swagger, unifying the Demon Region and establishing the Demon Kingdom, he hadn’t been like this in the ancient era.

Back then, many were stronger than him. Putting aside the humans, among the demons alone, the dragon, phoenix, and qiongqi were all more powerful than him. In terms of ancient secrets, Jiang Lianyi undoubtedly knew far more than he did.

Two dijiang whispered to each other. “Who is the Qilin Immortal?”

Academic circles had long proposed the theory that the Demon Immortal was the Qilin Immortal, but they had always lacked substantial evidence. Today, through the conversation of these two ancient great demons, they confirmed the Demon Immortal’s identity.

The two dijiang were flabbergasted. Their eyes met, and they held their breath. Realizing the gravity of the matter, they couldn’t control their voices.

This is heaven-shocking news!

But no one had imagined the Qilin Immortal would let go of old grudges so thoroughly that they became husband and wife!

The complexions of those races who had secretly targeted the Phoenix Tribe instantly turned pale. If Jiang Lianyi’s return had made them abandon their covetous designs on the Phoenix Tribe’s treasures, after they learned of her relationship with the Qilin Immortal, their worry was whether they would face reckoning.

Before, they could still say Jiang Lianyi wasn’t unbeatable, for above her was the Qilin Immortal.

But now, who would dare say that?

The Jiang Lianyi now represented the Qilin Immortal’s will; she was the supreme heaven of the demon race!

“About the legitimacy of the Demon Kingdom...” freewebnovel.com

Despite being fellow sentient beings with spirit intelligence, there were differences in strength and status. But no matter the disparity, one couldn’t possibly act as if they were deaf to the curses from those of lower status.

I’m the number one below immortals, and along with ten Transcendent Tribulation great demons, this lineup can be considered unbeatable among half-immortals. I refuse to believe we can’t take down a single Jiang Lianyi!

Jiang Lianyi, you brought this upon yourself!

Zhu Tian’s pupils constricted as a sense of foreboding wrapped his heart.

Chapter 618: This Trip to the Demon City Is Worthwhile; We Must Come Again if the Demon Kingdom Holds Another Founding Ceremony

Discovering that the master-servant marks had vanished, the Transcendent Tribulation great demons hurriedly retreated, distancing themselves from the battlefield.

If we get involved in a battle between half-immortals, we would die even without knowing how.

Besides, even if we manage to defeat Jiang Lianyi, what if the Qilin Immortal appears to settle the score with us? No matter how strong Supreme Lord Zhu Tian is, he can’t be stronger than an immortal.

Some were truly loyal to Zhu Tian. If they achieved victory, it would count as a meritorious service in aiding the rising monarch, granting them boundless prospects.

It’s not too late for me to atone for my sins with meritorious contributions.

The East Sea Dragon Tribe’s old ancestor aimed at the Jiuying Tribe’s old ancestor and released an endless stream of seawater from his storage ring. Merging with it, he transformed into a terrifying divine dragon of the seas, whose single claw could shred mountains.

The Jiuying Tribe was the ultimate form of the serpent race. Dragon and serpent rose from the land; the two races had been rivals since ancient times.

Jiang Mingzi pulled out a large banner and unfurled it to reveal a painting of phoenixes crying out at Mount Qi.[1] This was a Five Virtues banner left by their ancient ancestor and one of the supreme treasures.

“Damn it!”

Seeing Jiang Mingzi get serious, the Taowu Tribe Chieftain felt his scalp go numb. He had just advanced to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, while Jiang Mingzi was a veteran at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, not to mention that Jiang Mingzi wielded a supreme treasure. The gap between them was absurdly huge.

But now that things have come to this, I can only brace myself and fight.

~~~

On the heavenly altar, Lu Yang and Zhu Yunwu saw that the battle between the two half-immortals was about to erupt. Without a second thought, they jumped straight down from the altar.

“Dance of Immortal Fall and World Destruction!” Zhu Tian began to dance, his steps carrying an intent of destruction and annihilation. The entire Demon City shook, as if it was doomsday.

This was worlds apart from the power of the dance performed while controlling Zhu Yunwu.

Towering floodwaters formed waterspouts, eight of them positioned according to the Bagua, blocking all paths of escape.

Jiang Lianyi extended her hand and produced a jade flute. This was the jade flute that had hung on the wall of the fourth level of the Creation Ancient, demonstrating Jiang Lianyi’s fondness for it.

Her vermillion lips lightly touched the blowhole, and her fingertips covered the finger holes. She closed her eyes in concentration. Her long hair fluttered in the gentle breeze while she played the dizi flute as if she was intoxicated.

The crisp sound of the dizi flute penetrated the blockade of the eight waterspouts. It was as though the entire world had become utterly silent. If the eight waterspouts represented extreme motion, the clear flute sounds represented extreme stillness.

Motion and stillness met.

Crack. The temperature plummeted. The eight waterspouts began to freeze from their bases. In an instant, the tornadoes became pillars of ice. The temperature in the Demon Region dropped sharply to zero degrees, causing spectating cultivators to breathe out visible puffs of air.

“Go!” Jiang Lianyi lowered the jade flute, hooked her index finger, and lifted it upward.

The eight frozen waterspouts shattered into blocks of ice, forming a long dragon that smashed toward Zhu Tian.

“Space, congeal!” Zhu Tian shouted.

The space above his head continuously compressed, forming a spatial rampart that blocked the onslaught of ice blocks.

Seeing the two’s attack range exceeding the heavenly altar, with residual waves sweeping toward them, the onlookers hastily retreated to the Demon City’s gates to watch the battle unfold. They still firmly held their recording orbs, determined to record this whole process. The recording orbs had been activated since the commencement of the kingdom-founding ceremony.

Chapter 619: Battle of Half-Immortals!

The Baxia Tribe Chieftain’s price gouging made Chieftain Jin grind his teeth in frustration. But when he thought about how spectacular this battle was, he figured describing it vividly with mere words would require the skills of a professional storyteller.

Zhu Tian performed a kip-up, planning to spring up from the ground.

But how could Jiang Lianyi give him that chance? She jumped down from the heavenly altar and delivered a kick to Zhu Tian in the creator, causing him to nearly vomit his intestines.

Cough! Pinned under Jiang Lianyi’s foot, Zhu Tian’s several attempts at getting up failed, and he flew into a rage.

“I was merely letting you have two moves! Don’t think you’re really anything impressive!” Zhu Tian didn’t expect Jiang Lianyi to be this difficult to deal with.
