If that’s the case, Jiang Lianyi should still need a long time to recover her peak strength.

However, upon exchanging blows, he discovered that Jiang Lianyi was in her peak condition as in ancient times, without the slightest weakness and exhaustion. This is why I suffered such a great loss.

Damn it! How is this possible?!

With a roar, he transformed into his original form and increased in size as he rammed Jiang Lianyi flying.

Jiang Lianyi trod on air twice consecutively and stabilized herself mid-air, utterly unruffled. Her arms shifted, and she transformed into a five-colored phoenix.

The phoenix spread its wings and soared high. Its body was covered in bright, five-colored feathers. Sunlight pierced through the feathers, shining upon the earth and turning into resplendent, five-colored light.

Minor cultivators found their hidden injuries gradually vanishing when the five-colored light shone on them.

The demon race’s strongest state was fighting in their original forms. The two half-immortals reverted to their true forms and held nothing back as they launched fierce assaults.

Zhu Tian kicked off with his two feet, kicking over the meticulously refined liuli-glazed white jade heavenly altar. The altar was also a magical treasure!

The nine-tiered heavenly altar, several hundred meters high, smashed fiercely toward Jiang Lianyi. The latter whirled her wings around and caught the heavenly altar, dispersing its force and coating it in a layer of lightning before hurtling it back.

Zhu Tian opened his mouth, releasing invisible sound waves that immobilized the heavenly altar. Under the sonic assault, the altar shook with a subtle yet violent tremor before being hurled back at Jiang Lianyi again.

If Jiang Lianyi dared to touch the heavenly altar the same way as before, both the altar and the lightning would explode. She had long seen through Zhu Tian’s little scheme and commanded space to seal the heavenly altar.

“Returning it to you.”

The heavenly altar was like a toy in the hands of these two half-immortals, tossed back and forth. Only the spectating cultivators knew that with each exchange, the altar carried layer upon layer of attacks. If it exploded, even a veteran Transcendent Tribulation cultivator would probably be severely injured.

Finally, the heavenly altar could no longer withstand the accumulated layers of attacks and exploded between the two.

The four battles of two half-immortals and six Transcendent Tribulation great demons dazzled the onlookers, who wished they had several more pairs of eyes.

There were many Fusion cultivators present. Even if they could roughly follow the battles of Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, a combat at the half-immortal level was truly beyond their comprehension. However, this didn’t prevent them from unanimously choosing to watch the half-immortal battle.

The spirit energy within a thousand-li radius was drained, controlled by the two half-immortal great demons.

The two demons fought from the sky to the ground, and then from the ground back to the sky. Along their path, space was shattered, leaving devastation in their wake. The six battling Transcendent Tribulation great demons kept their distance from the fight, fearing they would be caught in the crossfire.

The sky was a riot of colors and unusual phenomena: heavenly maidens scattering flowers, the phoenix emperor arriving in splendor, and phoenixes born from the Wutong tree...

Following these were thunder and lightning. Two colossal shadows battled behind the thunderclouds, only allowing a glimpse of their stunning figures when lightning flashes illuminated them.

Zhu Tian danced gracefully, like a winged pig performing a dance. A solemn and murderous song accompanied his dance movements. “Speak not of a bountiful autumn harvest; after autumn comes the executioner’s blade falling on heads...”

Seeming to sense something, Jiang Lianyi beat her phoenix wings and flew sideways. An imperceptible blade grazed past, slicing off several of her phoenix feathers.

“The Song of Autumn from the Ballad of the Four Seasons?”

Proficient in music, Jiang Lianyi softly chanted a tune that also carried murderous intent.

Two different melodies resounded overhead, morphing into visible ripples that stirred spatial waves. Killing intent lurked everywhere, and ambushes lay in all directions!

Suddenly, torrential rain poured from the sky, hitting the ground with a relentless patter.

“Hmm? Not rain. This is... seeds?” Lu Yang picked up a seed from the ground but couldn’t identify its origin.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy informed him. “This is the seed of the Dragon-Locking Vine. Your era probably doesn’t have it.”

“Dragon-Locking Vine?”

“As the name implies, this thing once bound Ao Ling.”

Lu Yang recalled the Everlasting Immortal Fairy mentioning that Jiang Lianyi and Ao Ling were similar in strength, with a forty-sixty split. Jiang Lianyi had a forty percent chance of victory, while Ao Ling had a sixty percent chance.

The Dragon-Locking Vine seeds took root where they landed, sprouting and growing robustly. In an instant, the entire Demon City was overgrown with the vines, like countless hands reaching for the sky. It was a somewhat eerie sight.

The Dragon-Locking Vines grew rapidly, suddenly bending to surround and envelop Zhu Tian. The latter beat his four wings, which were like four invincible heavenly sabers capable of cleaving heaven and earth in two. This move had always earned him success.

This time will be no different. The four wings released four saber qi, hacking the Dragon-Locking Vines into pieces.

But immediately, Zhu Tian noticed something abnormal. The severed ends of the Dragon-Locking Vines had vigorous flames burning, as though the vines had been hollowed out and filled with fire.

“Oh no! This is Nirvana True Fire!”

The Dragon-Locking Vines regrew. Zhu Tian continued to beat his wings to sever them, but no matter how much he slashed, the vines would always grow back—endless and inexhaustible.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy explained to Lu Yang, “The Dragon-Locking Vine is an immortal vine specially bred by Jiang Lianyi. It was baked with Nirvana True Fire, allowing a wisp of flames to fuse into the seeds. When the Tree-Planting Mantra is used, it will take root and sprout, and the Dragon-Locking Vine will become an immortal vine that grows eternally with the power of the Nirvana True Fire.

“Under the control of the Incipient Dao Fruit, the Dragon-Locking Vine moves according to Lianyi’s will. It is flexible and adaptable, practically impossible to guard against.

“Little Ling didn’t anticipate this move back then. She was caught off guard and tied up tightly.”

Zhu Tian was similarly bound by the Dragon-Locking Vines, his six wings wrapped around him like zongzi leaves.

Unresigned to be tied up like this, he bellowed with ire. “Heaven-Earth Manifestation!”

He transformed into a ten-thousand-zhang giant beast. Muscles bulging, he attempted to break free by brute force. Seeing that growing big didn’t work, he shifted back to human form, trying to slip through the gaps in the vines.

Under Jiang Lianyi’s control, the Dragon-Locking Vines could shrink or enlarge. No matter what form Zhu Tian took, it bound him tightly, making escape impossible.

“You forced my hand!” Zhu Tian glowered with fury and opened his mouth wide.

Countless ancient ghost souls spewed forth, forming a spectral army. The ancient ghosts manifested in various forms—humans, demons, and even demon spirits. These were losers of the ancient war, devoured by Zhu Tian and refined with the power of his Incipient Dao Fruit.

“It’s the legendary March of Spectral Soldiers! All demons, retreat!”

Some Transcendent Tribulation great demons were horrified. This was a notorious legend from antiquity. When the spectral soldiers marched across the land, the earth was scorched for a thousand li, with not a blade of grass growing, and even planets became barren. It was a taboo among the demon race, often used to frighten children.

So the origin of this legend is Supreme Lord Zhu Tian!

Lu Yang couldn’t help but find this move familiar.

“You’re right to find it familiar. The Tiger Tribe learned this move and adapted it into the method of tiger-henchman ghosts, also the origin of the phrase ‘acting as a henchman to a tiger,’” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said in a carefree manner.

Jiang Lianyi spat out a ball of flame. Its temperature was even higher than the sun’s. This was the source of Nirvana True Fire!

She bit the tip of her tongue, and a drop of essence blood fell onto the Nirvana True Fire, which emitted a phoenix cry and transformed into a phoenix identical to herself.

This was the true Phoenix Nirvana!

The Nirvana True Fire, supremely tough and imbued with yang energy, was the ultimate bane of ghosts, demons, and evil!

Chapter 620: The Victor Becomes the King, the Loser Becomes a Bandit; The Strong Prey on the Weak

Tens of thousands of ancient spectral soldiers arranged themselves in uniform and orderly formations. Many among these spectral soldiers had become legends, passed down through later generations. It was a truly powerful lineup.

Later, they were all defeated under Zhu Tian’s hand.

If Zhu Tian lacked real capabilities, he wouldn’t have dared to proclaim himself emperor.

The phoenix formed from the Nirvana True Fire had a temperature comparable to the sun. The demon city was cast from metal, yet the metal battlements showed signs of melting under such terrifying heat, let alone the cultivators below.

It was said that cultivators were impervious to heat and cold, but when temperatures reached such extremes, they could only rely on their cultivation to endure it. Those protected by elders could manage and hold on. But for someone like Kong Hao, who came to the Demon City alone, the only option was to flee the city and watch the battle from a distance.

“Go!” Zhu Tian commanded. The spectral soldiers marched in ranks as a dark mass in the sky, carrying a petrifying and cold aura as they pressed down toward Jiang Lianyi.

“Explode.” The Nirvana True Fire phoenix spread its wings and soared, blazing like the scorching sun, whistling forward as fast as lightning.

The two forces collided and blasted. Yin and yang converged, forming a massive Taiji symbol in the air. Immediately after, the Taiji symbol exploded. The Nirvana True Fire phoenix dissolved into sparks, scattering across the sky.

Yet more than half of the spectral soldiers remained.

Seeing this, Zhu Tian burst into laughter.

“Condense!” Unmoved, Jiang Lianyi uttered a command softly, employing the power of her Incipient Dao Fruit to control the Nirvana clone, making it reform.

The Nirvana clone charged into the spectral soldiers and exploded once more.

“Condense!”

Zhu Tian was dumbfounded. I’ve never heard of anyone’s clone exploding, recondensing, and then repeatedly exploding again!

Wait, this move seems somewhat familiar. I had encountered it in the ancient era. Who was it again?

Watching this scene, Lu Yang’s eyes twitched. This move is indeed familiar. Isn’t this the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s favorite fighting style?

Without an Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit, she made do with the Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy remarked, “Although Lianyi has lost her memory, it looks like she hasn’t forgotten my teachings.”

Boom! The Nirvana clone blew up on Zhu Tian, stirring a cloud of dust. The blast left Zhu Tian in a wretched state, his wings charred.

Zhu Tian sang the Song of Spring, rushing to restore his condition before the next wave of attacks.

“Condense!” The Nirvana clone coalesced once more.

Zhu Tian stood solemnly, prepared for battle. As the Nirvana clone charged toward him, he controlled space, forming a rampart to block the next explosion.

Suddenly, the space behind him rippled. Jiang Liangyi traversed space, arriving behind him.

“Oh no!”

A gigantic phoenix silhouette emerged behind Jiang Lianyi. Surrounding her were countless avian beasts: Zhuque (Vermillion Bird), Qingluan, Chongming, Bifang...

“Homage of Ten Thousand Birds! That’s the legendary Homage of Ten Thousand Birds!” a great demon below exclaimed.

“The Phoenix Ancestor subdued all birds. Ten thousand birds revere the Phoenix Ancestor as their sovereign. That’s how the saying that the phoenix is the king of birds came about in later ages!”

The enormous phoenix silhouette spread its wings. The ten thousand birds transformed into feathers, becoming part of the phoenix. The phoenix silhouette soared skyward, then dove down.

Zhu Tian looked up. It was as if a phoenix bathed in fire had burst forth from the sun, striking fear into the heart. He wanted to evade it, but everything in his surroundings suddenly slowed down, including himself.

“Spatial Lockdown... No, this is Time Stop!” Zhu Tian’s expression was one of incredulity. I never imagined Jiang Lianyi’s Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit would be able to stop even time!

So she had never used her full strength all this time!

Time stopped. Zhu Tian lost all perception of the outside world. When time resumed its flow, the phoenix silhouette was already at an unavoidable distance.

Boom! The phoenix’s beak pierced through Zhu Tian, pinning him to the ground!

“What just happened? Why did Zhu Tian suddenly stop moving?” Lu Yang was puzzled. At that distance, Zhu Tian could have dodged, but he didn’t move, as if an immobilization spell had struck him. freewebnovel.com

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy saw through the trick. “It’s not that he didn’t move; it’s that everyone didn’t move for one breath. Lianyi controlled time, stopping it.

“It’s only because you have this immortal with you that you could see the entire battle clearly. To others, it looked like the phoenix silhouette suddenly jumped in front of Zhu Tian, and he was hit because he couldn’t dodge in time.”

“Time Stop? Senior Lianyi can even do something like that?!” Lu Yang was flabbergasted.

“The Play-Dead Technique is about seeking life through death, deceiving time. In a sense, it’s prevailing over time. That’s why she can stop time. However, this unconventional way of overcoming time is ultimately not the proper path, so she can only stop time for one or two breaths.

“If it were the Epoch Immortal, stopping it for eight hundred or a thousand years wouldn’t be a problem.”

In a battle between half-immortals, one or two breaths were sufficient to decide victory or defeat.

“As for why she didn’t use it before, it was probably to conceal her abilities. Exposing one’s trump card in front of everyone isn’t wise. Not to mention, did you see her use an immortal artifact at all?”

Lu Yang pondered about it. That’s true. Senior Lianyi definitely has an immortal artifact refined by the Heaven Mandate Immortal, but she hasn’t brought it out. This already speaks volumes.

“The victor becomes the king, and the loser becomes a bandit. Zhu Tian, do you accept defeat?” Jiang Lianyi returned to human form, looking down at the gravely injured Zhu Tian on the ground, her voice icy.

Zhu Tian was dejected. He had also figured out the key point behind his defeat and accepted it wholeheartedly. Even if we fight again, the result will be the same.

“I admit defeat.”

Jiang Lianyi made no further remarks. She brought her index and middle fingers together and lightly tapped her brow, activating her Incipient Dao Fruit. A master-servant mark formed and branded itself onto Zhu Tian.

In the law of the jungle, the strong prey on the weak; the victor becomes the king, and the loser becomes a bandit. This was a principle both believed in. Otherwise, they wouldn’t have formed the Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit.

Jiang Lianyi had already defeated Zhu Tian in the ancient era. But back then, the Four Immortals governed the world, so there was no need to control him. Today was different. If Zhu Tian was left uncontrolled, he might play other tricks. Moreover, Zhu Tian now knew she could stop time. This matter couldn’t be leaked.

“Your establishment of the Demon Kingdom is beneficial to the human race. I will not bar you from doing so. The Phoenix Tribe can also join the Demon Kingdom.” With the master-servant mark, Zhu Tian was the ruler of the Demon Kingdom in name, and Jiang Lianyi was the true ruler of the Demon Kingdom. “You act ostentatiously, showing off your sharpness. If you continue like this, you will drag the demon race into an abyss of eternal doom.”

All things aside, Zhu Tian’s intention of invading Great Xia alone is a road to inevitable demise. Jiang Lianyi had heard the Everlasting Immortal Fairy mention that Great Xia had more than one immortal.

Zhu Tian was clearly unwilling, but he lost, so he had to listen to whatever Jiang Lianyi said.

After the smoke dispersed, the crowd saw Zhu Tian admitting defeat on the ground, as well as the victor, Jiang Lianyi, whose visage remained icy despite her victory. Due to the two half-immortals’ intimidating power, no one dared to draw close.

“Senior Brother.” Jiang Lianyi walked toward Lu Yang, respectfully calling out to him.

The crowd automatically parted to clear a passage for her. Fortunately, Lu Yang was mentally prepared and appeared unruffled on the surface. He even nodded steadily, displaying the airs of a young creed leader. In addition, Lu Yang walked in front, with Jiang Lianyi trailing behind him by half a step, demonstrating a distinct hierarchy between them.

Lu Yang cast a glance at Zhu Tian and said placidly, “Let’s go. The Demon Kingdom is nothing special.”

The two left the Demon City under the reverent gazes of many experts. They vanished into thin air, mysterious, unfathomable, and inscrutable.

Chapter 621: Impermanence of Destiny

“Whew, it’s finally over.” Lu Yang and Jiang Lianyi arrived at a location far away from the Demon City and peeled away their Invisibility Talismans.

“It’s not over yet. I used the power of my Incipient Dao Fruit to control Zhu Tian. There are many eyes here; let’s look for him once the crowd has thinned.”

~~~

The battle between half-immortals grabbed the most eyeballs, while the three other battles between Transcendent Tribulation cultivators drew considerably less attention.

Among the three battles, the one between Jiang Mingzi and the Taowu Tribe Chieftain featured the greatest disparity in strength, making the outcome the most foregone conclusion.

Backed by the ancient ancestor, Jiang Mingzi’s combat style became even more ferocious and wild. Ever since the Taowu Tribe joined the Demon Kingdom, their chieftain, Ji Youming[1], had been humiliating the Phoenix Tribe by borrowing the monarch’s authority. However, the Phoenix Tribe dared not retaliate out of fear that it would give the Demon Kingdom a pretext for war.

Now, they finally had the chance to strike back.

“Jiang Mingzi, I think we can sit down and talk this over,” Ji Youming beseeched as he coughed up large mouthfuls of blood, a chill seeping into the bottom of his heart. It’s clear he is not holding back and is bent on beating me to death.

“Talk to your mother! You will die today!” Jiang Mingzi’s temper had always been irascible, but his position had restrained him from such outbursts previously.

“Fine fine fine! You’ve forced my hand!” Enraged, Ji Youming burned his essence blood and spewed mist from his mouth, summoning lightning.

The lightning that had appeared during the battle between Zhu Tian and Jiang Lianyi had not been cast by either of them, but by Ji Youming.

“All-Encompassing Heaven Immortal Lightning!”

The lightning seemed to form an entire world, with mountains, rivers, beasts, and plants manifested from thunder appearing above the clouds. Then, that world crumbled, and the lightning morphed into a cyan-purple molten torrent that crashed down violently toward Jiang Mingzi. freewebnovel.com

Several Fusion cultivators noticed the commotion, and their eyes twitched. Had they been beneath that lightning, they feared not even their bones would remain.

“I hereby establish the rule: [For three breaths, you cannot dodge]. Old bastard, die!” Ji Youming roared in rage.

Jiang Mingzi unfurled the Five Virtues Great Banner and shook it vigorously. As the huge banner fluttered, the five ancient characters for Virtue, Righteousness, Benevolence, Propriety, and Credibility were especially striking. The cyan-purple molten lightning fell upon the banner but displayed not a shred of its power.

“How is this possible?!” Ji Youming was shocked. This move is one of my trump cards. How could it be neutralized so effortlessly?

Jiang Mingzi sneered. Why would I reveal to him that the Five Virtues Great Banner is a top-tier defensive treasure capable of disrupting yin and yang and is impervious to all spells?

“I hereby establish the rule: [For three breaths, you cannot dodge]!”

“Impermanence of Destiny!” An inexplicable power coalesced at Jiang Mingzi’s fingertip.

Sensing danger, Ji Youming turned to flee. But bound by the rule where he couldn’t escape for a breath, he had no choice but to resist it head-on.

“Don’t think you’re the only one who can defend!” Ji Youming produced a lion's hide from his storage ring and held it before him. It was a defensive magical treasure refined from the corpse of the previous tribe chieftain, Ji Xiong.

Jiang Mingzi’s finger pierced the supposedly indestructible lion hide and touched Ji Youming’s brow.

“What have you done?!” Ji Youming felt that something had changed, but he couldn’t put a finger on it.

Jiang Mingzi wouldn’t divulge the features of his technique to his opponent.

The two continued to battle. Ji Youming’s moves repeatedly faltered and were riddled with mistakes—the circulation of his cultivation technique stuttered, his hand seals were a beat too slow, and all sorts of mishaps plagued him.

Impermanence of Destiny was a karma-type divine ability that lowered the opponent’s luck for a period of time. In other words, it cursed Ji Youming with a streak of misfortune.

The two exchanged hundreds of moves. Ji Youming was already outmatched by Jiang Mingzi, and with the defense of the Five Virtues Great Banner, all attacks against Jiang Mingzi were nullified. Compounded by Ji Youming’s wretched luck, he blundered repeatedly. For these several hundred exchanges, he was essentially taking a beating.

Jiang Mingzi struck with ruthless brutality, each blow aimed to kill, until finally...

“Ah—”

Jiang Mingzi transformed into a thousand-zhang phoenix and ripped open Ji Youming’s chest with steely talons.

Seeing the situation turn dire, Ji Youming ejected his soul from his body, burned his lifespan, and fled without hesitation.

“Hmph, you run pretty fast.” Jiang Mingzi snorted coldly, not expecting Ji Youming to escape so decisively. Unless Jiang Mingzi also burned his own lifespan, he couldn’t catch up to Ji Youming. “Did I fight too fiercely and scare him off?”

Jiang Mingzi paid no further mind to Ji Youming, storing his corpse in his storage ring before heading to the Demon City to find his ancient ancestor.

~~~

“Huff, huff, huff—” Ji Youming shuddered with lingering fear. Seeing that Jiang Mingzi didn’t give pursuit, he ceased burning his lifespan.

“I’d likely be discovered along the way if I return to the tribe in a soul state. I’ll take over someone’s body and use their body to return!”

Ji Youming arrived outside the city, where minor cultivators without their shifu or elder guarding over them had gathered. They were too timid to enter the city to watch the battles.

Any one of them would do.

“I’ll choose you!” Without another word, he charged into the spirit platform of a young cultivator.

The young cultivator’s soul was seated in meditation when he saw Ji Youming and jumped in fright.

“Boy, what’s your name?” Ji Youming grinned menacingly. Currently in his true form, his visage was so hideous that it could make children stop crying.

“I-I’m Kong Hao,” the young cultivator stammered.

“Kong Hao? I’ll remember you... Wait, where did these iron bars come from?”

Just as Ji Youming was about to attack Kong Hao and take over his body, he found himself separated from Kong Hao by a set of iron bars.

“This is a seal! Why is there a seal inside you? Who does it seal?” Ji Youming was perplexed when a familiar cold voice suddenly spoke.

“It’s sealing me, of course!”

Ji Youming whirled around and spotted another taowu locked behind the bars. Trembling all over, he cried out. “Ji Xiong!”

Ji Xiong was blind in one eye. Something seemed caught in his throat, making his laughter hoarse and grating. Anyone could hear the schadenfreude in it.

“Ji Youming, you disrespected your elder, rebelling to steal my position as chieftain. Have you ever imagined a day like this?”

“Y-you...what are you trying to do?!” Were he in peak condition, he naturally wouldn’t fear the old chieftain. But he had just emerged from a bloody battle with Jiang Mingzi and was at his weakest. If he faced the old chieftain now, he would only be in for a beating.

“What I’m trying to do? Keep you locked in here with me, of course!” Ji Xiong roared, suppressing Ji Youming.

This was the place Ji Xiong was sealed. Ji Youming could leave, but how could Ji Xiong allow his enemy to escape?

After being trapped here for so many years, he hadn’t figured out how to break the seal, but he had figured out how to cast a seal!

~~~

Half a day later, the battle in Demon City concluded. The clash between the two ancient half-immortals shocked the world.

Ji Youming was missing, his fate unknown.

The battle between the two Transcendent Tribulation dragons and the elderly Dijiang and the Jiuying Tribe old ancestor ended without a victor, but any discerning observer could tell that this was a public facade. The elderly Dijiang and the Jiuying Tribe's old ancestor were seriously injured and required prolonged recuperation.

~~~

In the Demon City’s imperial palace, Zhu Tian assumed human form and sat upon the throne that symbolized authority.

“Your Majesty...” The elderly Dijiang, swathed in bandages, attended to him at his side.

“Enough, withdraw. You’re not needed here.” Zhu Tian waved impatiently.

After the elderly Dijiang left, a male and a female figure appeared in the palace. They were none other than Jiang Lianyi and Lu Yang. Occupied by only three people, the vast palace felt exceptionally empty.

Zhu Tian rubbed his hands together cordially and greeted them with a smile, offering the throne. “Fellow Daoist Jiang, please sit. The chair was cold, so I warmed it for you.”

Jiang Lianyi turned to Lu Yang. “Senior Brother, would you like to sit?”

Lu Yang, “...”

Me, a human, sitting on the throne of the Demon Kingdom’s ruler?

Lu Yang turned to Zhu Tian. “Would you like to sit?”

After much back-and-forth, Zhu Tian finally took out two additional thrones from his storage, resolving the issue.

The three chairs were arranged in a circle, quite like fellow villagers chatting around a stove.

Jiang Lianyi voiced the question that weighed heaviest on her heart. “Do you know where my husband is?”

“Ah, he’s still alive?”

1. His name “Youming” literally translates to “have life.” ☜

Chapter 622: Fear-Stricken Zhu Tian

The moment the words left his mouth, Zhu Tian felt like his life was hanging by the thinnest thread, his fate uncertain.

Jiang Lianyi cast a cold glance at Zhu Tian but did not strike.

She had no other choice. Worried that Zhu Tian might lie, she secretly used the power of her Incipient Dao Fruit to compel him to speak everything that came to mind and to not withhold any information from her.

Zhu Tian hastily tried to salvage the situation, like mending the pen after the sheep were lost. “I said I thought the Qilin Immortal had long died.” Right afterward, he wished he could give himself two resounding slaps for his big mouth.

In the past, I’d always weighed my words carefully. How did it become like this today? Why am I blurting everything without using my brain?

Jiang Lianyi, “...”

It seems forcing someone to speak the truth also has its drawbacks. Never mind, it looks like Zhu Tian doesn’t have clues to my husband’s whereabouts, much less whether he’s alive or dead.

As Zhu Tian calmed himself, cold sweat drenched his back, and his hands and feet turned icy.

Jiang Lianyi’s question implies that the Qilin Immortal is undoubtedly alive. I haven’t felt the suppression of a superior Dao Fruit only because of my inadequate cultivation.

The Qilin Immortal is alive, yet I dared to make a move on Jiang Lianyi...

Zhu Tian didn’t dare to imagine the consequences. If I cross paths with the Qilin Immortal, even multiple lives wouldn’t suffice!

“Do you know Everlasting-jiejie?”

“Who?” Zhu Tian’s visage was of utter bewilderment. He had never heard of the name.

“This immortal.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy showed her face confidently, darting out from Lu Yang’s body. After all, Zhu Tian is branded with a master-servant mark, so he can’t divulge my identity.

When Zhu Tian saw the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, his hair immediately stood on end. He wondered if he was hallucinating and shot to his feet, unable to control his voice. “An immortal!!”

Having lived through the era where the Four Ancient Immortals ruled and often attended their lectures, I can’t be any more familiar with immortals. This power that seems bottomless at a glance definitely belongs to an immortal!

To think an immortal is hiding within this Young Creed Leader Lu!

He connected this to the matter of the ancient Heavenly Court. Could this immortal be Dou Heavenly Sovereign, the ruler of the Heavenly Court and the fifth ancient immortal?

No wonder Young Creed Leader Lu hadn’t been controlled by the Dijiang Command. Previously, I thought Jiang Lianyi had intercepted it, but now, it looks like it was the work of this immortal.

Zhu Tian suddenly realized that despite being an ancient great demon, his knowledge of ancient times was pitifully shallow, like a frog at the bottom of the well; he only understood matters at the surface level.

“Oh well, it seems like it’s yet another person who doesn’t recognize this immortal.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pouted, unsurprised. Lianyi is the closest to me and extremely strong among half-immortals, but even she can’t remember me. It’s far more unlikely for the likes of Zhu Tian to remember me.

Zhu Tian was astute enough to produce a fourth throne for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to sit upon.

The four of them sat in a circle and continued their chat in an atmosphere highly reminiscent of rural life.

“Tell us, what made you decide to slumber, and why did you choose to revive now?”

“This matter traces back to the cataclysmic battle fought by the Four Ancient Immortals. It’s just that I never learned who their opponent was...” As Zhu Tian spoke, his gaze toward the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was filled with even more panic.

The Heavenly Court’s ruler, the hidden fifth immortal, and the enemy of the Four Ancient Immortals—could this mighty expert be the opponent the Four Ancient Immortals faced back then?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy glared. “Don’t look at me. Keep going.”

“Oh, oh.” Zhu Tian hurriedly calmed his fearful heart, feeling as though he had just walked the line between life and death.

It’s as easy as flipping a hand for the Qilin Immortal to kill me. If this Heavenly Court Ruler could battle the Four Ancient Immortals, I’m afraid her strength is beyond even the Qilin Immortal’s.

If she had acted at the heavenly altar earlier...

Zhu Tian shuddered.

Judging by how Young Creed Leader Lu enjoys a close relationship with the Heavenly Court Ruler, if I can’t curry favor directly with her, currying favor with Young Creed Leader Lu can be considered a roundabout way to achieve the same end.

Zhu Tian continued, “Fellow Daoist Jiang, you witnessed that battle too, didn’t you? That was a realm we half-immortals could never reach, a chasm too vast to cross, plunging everyone into despair...”

Jiang Lianyi corrected him, “I wasn’t in despair.”

“...plunging me into despair,” Zhu Tian rephrased. “At the time, I contemplated. Nothing in this world is eternal. The Four Ancient Immortals couldn’t govern the world forever. Since I couldn’t shine in their era, why not enter slumber and awaken when no immortals—or better yet, no half-immortals—remain in the world?

“The more I pondered about it, the better the idea seemed. Soon, I gathered a trove of natural treasures suited for deep slumber, placed them in a coffin, and buried myself.

“I left a message for my descendants to resurrect me in an era without immortals. This became a top secret known only to successive chieftains of the Dijiang Tribe, passed down through generations.

“Two hundred years ago, my descendants awakened me. When I awoke, I chuckled and thought it was truly a great era. A half-immortal could be unbeatable!

“After that, I spent two hundred years recovering my strength and establishing the Demon Kingdom. The Demon Kingdom was just established this morning when you all came over to attack.”

Seeing that Zhu Tian genuinely knew nothing relevant, Jiang Lianyi didn’t waste any more time questioning him and prepared to leave. “As I stated before, the Phoenix Tribe will become a member of the Demon Kingdom. With the Demon Region unified, you must focus on governing the Demon Nation well. I will be supervising you at all times.”

In the ancient era, immortals governed tens of thousands of inhabited stars; half-immortals were slightly inferior, governing a few hundred. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was an exception, governing only one star.

Zhu Tian had experience in governance.

Leaving the Demon City’s imperial palace, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy returned to Lu Yang’s body.

“Where to next?”

“To the Phoenix Tribe.”

~~~

Qiongqi Tribe.

A petite figure carefully studied the recording orb Chieftain Jin had spent a fortune to acquire, her expression solemn. The battle between two half-immortals was worth examining repeatedly.

“It’s indeed Jiang Lianyi, and at her peak condition no less.” The petite figure clicked her tongue. She had assumed Jiang Lianyi had just awakened and was far from her peak condition. But now, it appeared that Jiang Lianyi could perform grand and unrestrained moves, resolving the fight with Zhu Tian without even using her trump cards.

“Could it be that A’Shi gave her some good stuff?” she murmured to herself.

“Little Ancestor, regarding our next step...” Chieftain Jin inquired timidly from the side.

“Join the Demon Kingdom first. It isn’t obvious in the recording orb, but based on Jiang Lianyi’s character, she surely would have imprinted a master-servant mark on Zhu Tian. This Demon Kingdom belongs to Zhu Tian in name, but in reality, it is Jiang Lianyi’s.

“With Jiang Lianyi present, the unification of the Demon Kingdom is already a foregone conclusion. It would be unreasonable for our Qiongqi Tribe to keep refusing to join. Better to join now and still retain some initiative.”

The petite figure had clashed repeatedly with Jiang Lianyi in the ancient era and knew her personality all too well. Using the smokescreen to imprint a master-servant mark might fool others, but it wouldn’t fool me.

Chapter 623: Returning to the Phoenix Tribe

In the Phoenix Tribe, three Transcendent Tribulation old ancestors sat in a row, looking especially nervous.

The East Sea Dragon Tribe’s envoy, Ao Li, the Demon Region Dragon Tribe’s chieftain, and the Phoenix Tribe’s chieftain were also present, though they weren’t even qualified to sit.

Aside from them were elders from both races, great demons who had once left indelible marks in the Demon Region and carved out formidable reputations. With the rise of newer generations, they had retired into leisurely lives. They enjoyed immensely high statuses within their tribes, and even the chieftain had to treat them politely. Members of the two races had assembled here to await the Phoenix Ancestor’s return.

Originally, after Jiang Mingzi killed Ji Youming, he had intended to look for the Phoenix Ancestor in the Demon City. Unfortunately, he was a step too late. By then, the half-immortal battle had concluded, and Lu Yang and Jiang Lianyi had departed.

Reckoning that the ancient ancestor would surely return home for a look, he had hurried back to the Phoenix Tribe to wait. He had been waiting ever since, not even sparing the time to refine Ji Youming’s corpse.

The two Dragon tribes had thought similarly, convening at the Phoenix Tribe, thus leading to the current scene.

At the moment, the periphery of the Phoenix Tribe was thronged with various demon tribes, all here to curry favor with the Phoenix Tribe. Previously, the Phoenix Tribe was regarded as the number one tribe in the Demon Region because of its deep foundation; they were powerful, but not quite to the extent of commanding respect from the masses.

However, things were different now. With the Phoenix Ancestor returning, no one would believe the Phoenix Tribe even if they claimed they weren’t powerful.

“We’re so envious of you. With the Phoenix Ancestor’s return, your Phoenix Tribe is about to rise.”

Chapter 624: Changes at the Nascent Soul Stage

On the journey back to Great Xia, while everyone else rested, Lu Yang finally found time to comprehend the mysterious marvels of the Nascent Soul Stage. Since his breakthrough to the Nascent Soul Stage on the heavenly altar, events had followed one after another, leaving him no opportunity to study this new cultivation realm properly.

“The power of space...” Lu Yang opened his hand, and the space above his palm subtly twisted. It tore, stretched, and warped, forming a vortex-like shape.

One of the characteristics of the Nascent Soul Stage was the preliminary mastery of spatial power.

Storage rings were the most typical spatial-type magical treasures. To forge one, the minimum cultivation was the Nascent Soul Stage. For larger spaces, Divine Transfiguration or Fusion experts were needed.

For instance, the Dao-Seeking Sect’s identity jade tablets were a special type of storage ring, all crafted by Fifth Elder. Before Yun Zhi gave Lu Yang the Qingfeng sword, the most valuable magical treasure on him was his identity jade tablet.

Lu Yang could feel that his speed, strength, agility, spiritual consciousness, and other traits had undergone world-shaking changes. The so-called “Great Xia’s number one prodigy Lu Yang” is nothing compared to me now!

He also discovered that his mental space had expanded more than tenfold, now comparable to the size of a football field. It displayed mental strength usually observed only at the Divine Transfiguration Stage. If he wished, he could crush any Nascent Soul cultivator with spiritual consciousness attacks alone; at best, these opponents would become dizzy, and at worst, they could turn into idiots.

Lu Yang slowly closed his eyes. Focusing his mind and spirit, he uttered softly, “Out-of-Body Soul!”

He was left with only an empty body. His soul emerged and explored the outside, feeling a cool breeze—the Yin-Wind that permeated the world and was perceptible only to souls. To souls with unstable foundations, it was a calamity, but to Lu Yang’s soul, it was merely a slightly chilly wind and posed no threat.

In this soul-out-of-body state, his perception abilities were elevated to another level. This was another feature of the Nascent Soul Stage, though Lu Yang had been capable of this since the Foundation Establishment Stage.

Back then, he had obtained ghost servant commanding techniques after slaying the tiger demon. After cultivating this technique, he could command his own soul as if it were a ghost servant, achieving the out-of-body effect of souls.

However, his soul had been too fragile then; the slightest disturbance could injure it, potentially damaging his foundation in severe cases. This was why he had never employed this move.

Therefore, for a cultivator to attempt body takeover, two conditions were necessary: first, one’s cultivation must at least reach the Nascent Soul Stage; second, one must comply with the Body Takeover Law and only proceed with body takeover after undergoing procedural approval.

“It’s said that when one’s soul is out of the body, it can roam ten thousand li, witnessing the vast blue seas in the morning and viewing Mount Cangwu by dusk. Perfect chance to test it.” Lu Yang chuckled excitedly.

His soul completely left his body. He pushed forward at full speed, curious to see how fast he could fly.

Then, he watched helplessly as his physical body, seated cross-legged on the cloud, grew farther and farther away. The auspicious cloud was piloted by Jiang Lianyi, moving at an astonishing speed that simply couldn’t be compared to the flying speed of Lu Yang’s soul.

“Hey—wait for me!” Lu Yang’s soul hastily shouted.

“You rascal.” First Elder noticed something amiss with Lu Yang. He chuckled and scolded him as he pulled Lu Yang’s soul back.

Lu Yang rubbed the back of his head sheepishly and flashed a foolish smile before continuing to examine his changes. Looking inward, he spotted a white, plump nascent soul in his dantian. Beside it was the Everlasting Immortal Fairy laughing so uproariously she doubled over, tears streaming from her eyes.

“Hahaha, you even dared to detach your soul from your body while Lianyi was driving the cloud. Aren’t you afraid she might leave you behind?!”

Lu Yang’s face darkened, not wanting to be mocked by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “Immortal Fairy, what are you doing in my dantian?

“What kind of question is that? Where this immortal goes is none of your business.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy planted her hands on her hips. Is there anywhere I can’t go in Lu Yang’s body?

“Enough about this. Look at your nascent soul; does it look a bit like me?”

Lu Yang rolled his eyes, thinking the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was spouting nonsense again. “How is that possible? My nascent soul naturally looks like me... Holy crap, it really does resemble you a bit!”

The nascent soul was fair and chubby, utterly adorable. Its countenance resembled that of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

What’s going on?!

“Have you forgotten? When I was the acting sect leader, you helped me handle sect affairs, and I helped you cultivate. In other words, part of your Golden Core cultivation was attained by me on your behalf.

“It’s only natural that the nascent soul bears a slight resemblance to me.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Had I known this, I would never have let you cultivate in my stead no matter what. You should have handled the sect affairs yourself.

But it’s too late for regrets now.

“What purpose does this nascent soul serve?” Lu Yang had heard about the boundless marvels and mysteries of the Nascent Soul Stage. Spatial power and the out-of-body ability went without saying, but the most pivotal aspect was the nascent soul itself.

The quality of the golden core and the cultivation technique practiced during the Golden Core Stage directly determined the nascent soul’s strength.

Considering the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, a senior in cultivation, was present, he figured it would be more convenient to ask her directly.

At the mention of this topic, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy grinned, appearing exceedingly smug. “This nascent soul was obtained from the shattering of the Unbeatable Golden Core! All the essence of the Unbeatable Golden Core is concentrated in this infant! Thus, your nascent soul is hugely different from ordinary ones. Other nascent soul cultivators release their nascent souls and control them to fight.

“In theory, when you release your nascent soul at the Nascent Soul Stage, it can fight on its own.”

“That smart?” Lu Yang was startled. This is equivalent to having two of me. When using wood clones, I wouldn’t have to spare attention to control them anymore; I could engage in two battles simultaneously.

This is truly multiplying my combat power!

All my painstaking efforts to maintain a hundred-percent win rate at the Golden Core Stage were not in vain!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued, “Hence, I named this type of nascent soul ‘Unbeatable Nascent Soul!’”

“...Can we change the name?”

“Fine then.”

“The Unbeatable Nascent Soul is indeed powerful, but if you want it to fight on your behalf, there’s a prerequisite.”

“What prerequisite?”

“You need to defeat your nascent soul.”

Lu Yang’s head was filled with question marks.

But considering my peerless combat prowess, defeating my own nascent soul shouldn’t be difficult.

“Want to give it a try?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy urged.

“Let’s try!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pulled Lu Yang’s soul and nascent soul into the mental space and instructed him, “Carefully feel it—isn’t there an invisible threat connecting you and your nascent soul?”

“Yes, I can feel it.”

“Sever that thread! You must use your imagination and picture that this thread really exists, and that you hold a pair of scissors capable of cutting it!”

Lu Yang followed her instructions step by step, severing the connection to his nascent soul.

The moment the connection broke, the nascent soul opened its eyes and charged fiercely at Lu Yang.

“So fast!” Lu Yang exclaimed. “But it’s still not my match!”

Before ten minutes had passed, Lu Yang lay on the ground, being pummeled by his nascent soul. Gasping for breath, he looked at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy with the last ounce of his strength. “Immortal Fairy, why is this nascent soul so strong?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded, speaking matter-of-factly. “Didn’t I already tell you? This is the Unbeatable Nascent Soul. If even you can beat it, how could it be called unbeatable?”

Chapter 625: Senior Brother Dai, We Have Some Matters to Report

In ancient times, tribes were formed on the basis of blood ties, regardless of whether they were humans or demons. Sects only came into being after the end of the ancient era; Jiang Lianyi had never seen one.

Previously, when she listened to Lu Yang’s explanation, she hadn’t paid much mind to it. But now, seeing it for herself, she realized she had underestimated the concept of a sect.

Why did demons revere pure blood? It was ultimately because pure blood represented strength. Every race devoted itself to nurturing pure-blooded demons to bring out the potential in their bloodline.

On the other hand, sects focused not on bloodline but on talent, teaching according to individual aptitude and allowing them to excel in their own way. It was clearly much more than the demons’ approach.

Pillar and mainstay, my ass! I can’t handle these two brats’ affairs at all!

The first time you two went out, you joined the Everlasting Creed, and then it was destroyed.

The second time you two went out, you discovered Junior Brother Li Haoran was the reincarnation of the former Nine-Netherworlds Creed Leader.

The fifth time you went out, you met three Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivators in Hanshui City, captured them, and brought all three back.

This time, Meng Jingzhou planned to break through to the Nascent Soul Stage. Returning to his cave abode, he saw the old horse idly chewing grass at the entrance in a leisurely and contented manner.

“Old Horse, I’m back from the Demon Region. You really missed out this time; this trip was hugely rewarding!”

Regardless of whether the old horse was willing to listen, Meng Jingzhou directly told him about his experiences in the Demon Region for the past half a year.

After listening to the full story, the old horse hated his timidity, which resulted in him missing out on witnessing the half-immortal battle. Had I known they had the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor backing them, why would I be afraid? I could have swept through the Demon Region!

I can’t be like this anymore. Next time, next time I must follow this kid out to see the world!

~~~

“I wonder if Senior Lianyi has met Big Senior Sister yet.” Lu Yang was slightly concerned.

He ascended the mountain, familiar with the path to the summit. At the top, he found a worried Gan Tian, with no sign of Yun Zhi or Jiang Lianyi.

Gan Tian sat by the stone table with her hands clasped and thumbs circling each other, restless and plagued with worry.

“Third Senior Sister, where are Big Senior Sister and Senior Lianyi?”

“Ah, it’s Little Junior Brother. I have no idea what happened just now. Senior Lianyi proposed testing Big Senior Sister’s skills as soon as she saw her, and Big Senior Sister gladly agreed. Considering the commotion from their duel might be too big, they headed to an alternate space carved open by Big Senior Sister. I’ve been waiting here since.”

Lu Yang sucked in a cold breath. Senior Lianyi, you have a head of steel, challenging Big Senior Sister right out of the gate.

“Third Senior Sister, are you worried Big Senior Sister might lose?”

Gan Tian sighed and motioned for Lu Yang to sit, voicing her concern. “I’m worried that Senior Lianyi will have her Dao heart crushed despite having just returned to the world. In the past, Big Senior Sister didn't know how to hold back. Just based on what I know, several old seniors had their Dao hearts shattered by her, and it took centuries to recover their Dao hearts.”

“How did they recover their Dao hearts?” Lu Yang was curious. It was his first time hearing that a Dao heart could heal, though the price was immense. To think they needed centuries.

“Basically, they suppressed their cultivation realms, disguised themselves as juniors, and swaggered among them. Usually, they would first endure ridicule, being looked down on for their low cultivation realm, poor talent, and how they were doomed for life. Then, they would rise in resistance, unleash some power, and strike back.”

“They started from the Qi Training Stage and joined minor sects. When they reached the Foundation Establishment Stage, where the small sects limited their growth, they moved to medium sects, then it’d be the Golden Core Stage, Nascent Soul Stage...repeating the process I described.

“And you know what? This method worked pretty well. A few old seniors even found their soulmates during this and happily married their much younger partners like old cows eating tender grass. Rekindling a second spring in life, they rejuvenated their spirits and felt younger than before. Under the power of love, their strength even advanced to a higher level.”

Lu Yang, “...”

So the old seniors spent centuries showing off and slapping faces, huh?

As the two spoke, the space above them warped, and human-form Jiang Lianyi fell from the sky, crashing to the ground and stirring a cloud of dust.

Lu Yang and Gan Tian hurried forward to check on her, only to see her breathing cut off with no traces of life; she couldn’t be more dead.

“Senior Lianyi, are you alright?”

Hearing Lu Yang’s words of concern, Jiang Lianyi revived, sitting up abruptly with lingering fear.

“That was such a close shave. I never expected such a powerful junior in future eras. Fortunately, I committed suicide before losing and ended the battle, just barely managing to call it a draw with her!”

Chapter 627: Another Hidden Enemy

Jiang Lianyi recalled the earlier battle, finding it heart-stopping and extremely perilous. “As expected of our creed leader—truly powerful.

“Just now, I fought Creed Leader Yun in an alternate space. Within mere breaths, we exchanged hundreds of moves and were locked in a stalemate. The intricate schemes and intrigue involved are far too complex to describe in a short time!

“Creed Leader Yun’s attacks were fierce and sharp, showcasing the splendor of later eras. People say the present cannot compare to the past, but I believe that is utterly wrong. As the pinnacle of later generations, Creed Leader Yun proves it!

“The two of us battled vigorously, causing space to shatter, time to shake, and primal hundun chaos energy to spread.

“I originally intended to use the Nirvana Rebirth method to unleash my potential and engage in a final showdown with Creed Leader Yun. Unfortunately, the portal to the alternate space opened, and I accidentally fell out. The battle ended without a clear victor, so it can only be considered a draw!”

Lu Yang, “...”

Gan Tian, “...”

Lu Yang thought, With Senior Lianyi’s mindset, her Dao heart won’t be crushed even if she loses.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was quite satisfied with Jiang Lianyi’s performance. “As expected of my unofficial disciple to have used such a method at a critical juncture to maintain your win rate. You are teachable and have a promising future!

“Since I could fight Lass Yun to a draw, with you and the second-in-command helping, the scales of victory will surely tip in my favor when the time comes!”

After all, when both parties have equal strength, even the slightest change can alter the battle’s outcome!

Yun Zhi flew out from the alternate space. Hearing Jiang Lianyi’s account of the battle, she felt somewhat helpless. Weren’t you the one who said you wanted to show me the mighty divine abilities of ancient times, then seized the initiative to launch hundreds of moves in mere breaths; and after I blocked them and struck back, you immediately cast the Play-Dead Technique and fled the alternate space?

“Big Senior Sister,” Lu Yang greeted obediently.

“Nascent Soul Stage? Not bad. Your foundation is solid. Even though you have just broken through, you don’t need to consolidate your foundation. As expected of one with the Unbeatable Golden Core.” Yun Zhi nodded. Lu Yang’s cultivation progress was rapid, demonstrating that he hadn’t slacked off during the past half a year in the Demon Region.

“Third Junior Sister, Sixth Elder has been mentioning you often. Now that you’ve returned to the sect, it’s best to visit her. Don’t make the elder come to you; that would go against propriety.”

“Alright.” Facing Yun Zhi, Gan Tian shed the unruly and lawless demeanor she had displayed in the Demon Region, becoming well-behaved and doing whatever she was told.

After Gan Tian descended the mountain, Yun Zhi motioned for Lu Yang to sit. Jiang Lianyi could also sit on a stone chair.

“Big Senior Sister, these are the local specialties I brought back from the Demon Region.” Lu Yang produced four imperial thrones from his identity jade table as though he was presenting treasures. They were gifts Zhu Tian insisted on giving him before they left the Demon Region.

Replacing the stone chairs with imperial chairs instantly changed the atmosphere.

“Little Junior Brother, Senior Everlasting, what did you do in the Demon Region? And how was Senior Lianyi resurrected?” Yun Zhi’s placid tone held a hint of helplessness. To be honest, I was truly stunned when Third Junior Sister appeared with Jiang Lianyi.

No need to guess—this matter is no doubt related to Little Junior Brother and Senior Everlasting.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy emerged and took a seat in a half-crouching posture.

The human, demon, and ghost detailed their experiences in the Demon Region, particularly emphasizing their discovery of the world’s structure, the recording left by Qilin Immortal, and the battle of the Four Ancient Immortals against the mastermind behind the scenes.

Yun Zhi fell silent for a long time. This is genuinely an unexpected harvest. “Battles between immortals cannot be decided quickly, especially since the mastermind likely wields the Karma Dao Fruit, making them even harder to deal with. But to have fought the Four Ancient Immortals for seven days and nights without a clear outcome, the mastermind is stronger than I’d anticipated.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded. “I think so too.” She then added indignantly, “Who knows what that rascal Qilin Immortal is plotting, or if he’s asleep? Lianyi caused such a huge commotion in the Demon Kingdom, yet he didn’t show himself.”

This was also one of the reasons Jiang Lianyi had shown up at the Demon Kingdom’s founding ceremony.

Her presence on the heavenly altar implied that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had revived; this was information she planned to convey to the Qilin Immortal. Despite all that, he hadn’t appeared, indicating his situation was complicated—either he had entered slumber for some reason, or he was unable or couldn’t meet the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

In the recording orb, the Qilin Immortal had spoken heroically, uttering things like “The enemy is too dangerous, leave everything to me,” “Wife, you will definitely see the Everlasting Immortal Fairy,” and “I’m happy you’ve revived, Everlasting Immortal Fairy.”

Perhaps the Qilin Immortal was ambushed by the mastermind after his bold words.

Yun Zhi shook her head gently and analyzed calmly, “Actually, there’s another possibility, right? It’s just that you two are unwilling to consider it.”

Lu Yang was puzzled, looking at Yun Zhi in confusion.

In contrast, the expressions of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Jiang Lianyi turned unpleasant.

Yun Zhi continued, “The Qilin Immortal perished, the suppression vanished, and a half-immortal leveraged this opportunity to become an immortal, reforming the suppression.”

Lu Yang’s heart sank. This is possible. “But isn’t the Immortal Ascension Tribulation supposed to be massively grand and impossible to conceal? Could a half-immortal become an immortal unnoticed?”

Yun Zhi replied, “It’s true that the commotion during an Immortal Ascension Tribulation is massive, but it’s not impossible to conceal. For example, it could be hidden by the clash between two armies or the fluctuations of half-immortals fighting. Someone became an immortal in this way a hundred thousand years ago.

“However, the likelihood of the Qilin Immortal having perished is small. After all, due to the nature of his Dao Fruit, he is destined to be extremely hard to kill. If a battle of that level had occurred, ancient texts would have recorded it; the commotion from such a battle couldn’t have been veiled.”

Hearing this, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Jiang Lianyi look slightly relieved. freewebnovel.com

Yun Zhi continued, “Hearing Senior Lianyi’s description of the battle of the Four Ancient Immortals brings me to another question. Do you remember the immortal who tried to seize the Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit?”

Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded. They naturally remembered.

After the Everlasting Immortal was born, a shadowy figure hid nearby, ready to snatch the Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit. Subsequently, Yun Zhi detected his presence and destroyed him, later discovering the shadowy figure was similar to an immortal’s clone. Yun Zhi found the sensation familiar, recalling she had fought the shadowy figure’s main body before. The entity had entered Great Xia and was repelled by Yun Zhi.

Yun Zhi stated, “The other party is undoubtedly an immortal, but not at the level to battle the Four Ancient Immortals for seven days and nights.”

“Did they hide their strength?” Lu Yang guessed.

Yun Zhi shook her head. “I could sense whether he was holding back; that was his true level.”

“Could he have been severely injured and have yet to recover?”

“That’s also impossible. Any injury would have healed in three hundred thousand years. When I fought him, I didn’t sense any injury on him.”

Lu Yang furrowed his brows. This means that aside from the mastermind, there is another hidden enemy. Even if he’s not as strong as the mastermind, he’s still at the level of an immortal and not to be underestimated. Things are getting troublesome.

...Wait, why did I subconsciously assume he is my enemy? I’m only at the Nascent Soul Stage; am I even worthy?

Lu Yang realized something was wrong. Since when has my perspective become this lofty?

Chapter 628: Huge Commotion From Nascent Soul Breakthrough

Lu Yang realized he had grown somewhat conceited in his mentality. He forced himself to calm down quickly and analyze his combat power.

As the strongest Golden Core cultivator advancing to the Nascent Soul Stage, I can potentially challenge those ordinary Basic Divine Transfiguration cultivators. With my intelligence, I may even defeat them.

In other words, I possess combat power equivalent to the Basic Divine Transfiguration Stage.

Additionally, by invoking divine possession to ask the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to intervene and performing Big Senior Sister Animal Form Fist to summon Big Senior Sister, I can boost my combat power to another level.

Calculating all these advantages, I could actually contend with an immortal.

“Senior Lianyi, would you be interested in becoming a guest elder of our Dao-Seeking Sect?” Yun Zhi invited.

“Become a guest elder of your Dao-Seeking Sect?” Jiang Lianyi’s expression turned odd. As the true master of the Demon Kingdom, the Ancient Ancestor of the Phoenix Tribe, the number one below immortals, and someone who has just fought to a draw with you, how could I join your sect with my status?

Besides, I still don’t know the benefits of being the Dao-Seeking Sect’s guest elder or the duties it entails.

Yun Zhi paused, then added, “Senior Everlasting is our Dao-Seeking Sect’s first guest elder.”

“With such a warm invitation, it’s hard to refuse!” Jiang Lianyi replied.

The corners of Yun Zhi’s mouth curved into a faint smile. “In that case, Senior Lianyi, welcome to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Senior Lianyi, you are our Dao-Seeking Sect’s second guest elder. However, since your public identity is one of the Heavenly Court’s Four Regents, openly joining the Dao-Seeking Sect may easily lead to speculation about the relationship between the Heavenly Court and our sect. Hence, please keep your guest elder status a secret.” freewebnovel.com

“That makes sense. So what are the benefits of joining the Dao-Seeking Sect? Do I need to do anything? For example, how long must I stay in the sect?”

“It’s already our Dao-Seeking Sect’s honor if you could become a guest elder, Senior. How would we dare to restrict your freedom? We simply ask that you lend a hand only if the Dao-Seeking Sect faces danger in the future. In return, if you see anything you fancy in the sect, just inform me, and I can gift it to you. Places like the scripture library will also be open to you.”

Jiang Lianyi pondered. I’m not at a loss. Plus, Everlasting-jiejie is also a guest elder.

If we find Ao Ling, she’ll also become a guest elder and have to call me senior sister.

Either way, it’s a good deal.

As for the Dao-Seeking Sect items, nothing catches my eye for now. But the scripture library is a good place and amasses the most knowledge in the cultivation world. I ought to take a look.

“Senior Lianyi, what do you plan to do next?”

Jiang Lianyi contemplated it seriously. “The world after three hundred thousand years is unknown to me. I plan to explore this unfamiliar cultivation world and search for clues about my husband and Little Ling. If I can find leads on the other three immortals, that would be even better.”

“That is only right.” Yun Zhi took out a jade tablet and pushed it toward Jiang Lianyi.

“This is...?”

“A map of the cultivation world. There might be minor inaccuracies, but it’s generally correct.”

Jiang Lianyi didn’t stand on ceremony. “Then thank you, Creed Leader.” We’re all family now; refusing would make us appear estranged.

“As for Little Junior Brother, since you have reached the Nascent Soul Stage, you should diligently compile the Nascent Soul section of the Clear Heart True Nature Mantra. I will inspect it.”

Lu Yang immediately felt the pressure multiply and a big headache coming on. His heart, originally happy about returning from the Demon Region, turned cold. Writing cultivation techniques again? I’m afraid I won’t be able to leave the scripture library for the next month.

“Senior Lianyi, would you like to go to the scripture library with me?” Lu Yang invited Jiang Lianyi upon seeing she had intentions on heading there.

“Very well.”

Yun Zhi casually wrote a note and handed it to Jiang Lianyi. “Show this to the person guarding outside the scripture library, and they’ll let you in.”

Before Jiang Lianyi descended the mountain, she altered her appearance to prevent other members of the Dao-Seeking Sect from recognizing her.

As they went down the mountain, they saw many sect disciples running in one direction, seemingly to watch some spectacle.

“That’s...the direction of Old Meng’s cave?” Lu Yang remembered Meng Jingzhou saying he intended to shatter his golden core to form a nascent soul. He’s probably breaking through to the Nascent Soul Stage now.

He changed his mind at the last minute and headed to Meng Jingzhou’s cave abode.

Lu Yang arrived late. Many other disciples had already crowded in front of Meng Jingzhou’s cave abode, so Lu Yang and Jiang Lianyi could only watch from the back.

Jiang Lianyi had a good impression of the youngster who always accompanied Lu Yang. He possesses Nirvana True Fire and such exuberant yang energy that even the Phoenix Tribe, famed for our pure yang energy, can’t compare.

Before Meng Jingzhou’s cave abode, unusual phenomena abounded. Endless purple mist shrouded the peak, golden lotuses fell to the ground and took root, and phantom images of arhats chanted sutras. The scenery displayed much greater fanfare than that of Lu Yang’s breakthrough. It was no wonder that so many people had gathered here to watch.

Numerous disciples pointed and marveled at the wondrous sight, astonished by Meng Jingzhou’s talent.

“Look at the purple mist! This is the Purple Qi Talisman that can only be redeemed for ten thousand contribution points!”

“And the Falling Golden Lotus Talismans! Each golden lotus costs five thousand contribution points! There must be more than a hundred golden lotuses here!”

“And the Buddhist chants and arhat projections... Oh my heavens, how many contribution points does all this cost?”

“Listen! There’s even phoenix cries! Could it be the legendary Phoenix Nirvana?!”

In terms of wealth, few in the Dao-Seeking Sect could match Meng Jingzhou. Even the Divine Transfiguration disciples exclaimed in awe, thinking they would never dare spend so extravagantly.

Lu Yang’s eyelid twitched. Old Meng and I had initially planned to stir some commotion when breaking through to the Nascent Soul Stage back at the sect. After all, a cultivator only gets one chance in a lifetime. We naturally have to make it grander.

This inspiration came from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s story about the Nine-Layers Immortal’s immortal ascension.

I just didn’t expect Old Meng to cause such a huge commotion.

Old Meng’s talent is similar to mine; breaking through to the Nascent Soul Stage is a matter of a single thought. Despite the wondrous phenomena having lasted half an hour, he still hasn’t broken through, like he’s having constipation. That can only mean one thing—he’s waiting for the show to finish before breaking through.

As this thought arose, the unusual phenomena changed again. Arhats chanted sutras with the power to purify hearts, phantom images of ancient civilians circled Meng Jingzhou’s cave abode while kneeling in worship, and smiling mighty experts bestowed blessings with flowers in hand...

Nascent Soul aura waves burst from the cave, piercing the firmament. Everyone present could feel the tyrannical power in the air.

“Look, Junior Brother Meng has two nascent souls!”

Above the cave, two nascent souls identical to Meng Jingzhou were half curled up, with their heads and feet touching each other’s, emitting supremely strong energy.

Gradually, the two nascent souls spun faster, forming a perfect circle.

A senior male disciple scrutinized the two nascent souls and said slowly, “It resembles the Taiji diagram. The two nascent souls spin, separated by a line flowing like water between them. These two nascent souls symbolize one yang and one yang!”

Lu Yang, “...”

Since when is the Taiji diagram one yang and one yang?

Chapter 629: A Whole New World

Lu Yang even suspected the senior male disciple who shouted about the Taiji diagram was a shill hired by Meng Jingzhou.

Jiang Lianyi clicked her tongue in amazement as she watched. Despite having witnessed the cultivation concepts from numerous prodigies and talents in ancient times, this was her first time hearing of a Taiji diagram with one yang and one yang. Is this the cultivation philosophy after three hundred thousand years?

No wonder the Phoenix Tribe doesn’t fare as well as humans now—their thinking isn’t as advanced.

Meng Jingzhou had forked out his own money to buy most of the unusual phenomena, but the two nascent souls forming a pure-yang Taiji diagram was a genuine phenomenon.

Lu Yang was glad no unusual phenomena had appeared when he formed his nascent soul. If there had been any phenomena, it would probably have been the Unbeatable Nascent Soul giving me a brutal thrashing.

That would have been too embarrassing.

Oh wait, it would be embarrassing for Young Creed Leader Lu—nothing to do with me.

Jiang Lianyi pondered and noticed another peculiarity with Meng Jingzhou. “This is the first time I’ve seen someone with two nascent souls.”

Lu Yang was curious. “Were there no cultivators who developed two nascent souls in the ancient era?”

Jiang Lianyi shook her head gently. “A few did develop two golden cores, but they had different properties. Upon reaching the Nascent Soul Stage, according to the Yin-Yang Conservation Law, they would merge into one golden core before shattering to form a nascent soul.

“Do you know why the Nascent Soul is not just called Soul but has the character ‘Nascent’ added in front?”[1]

“Please enlighten me, Senior.”

“‘Nascent’ carries the meaning of origin, first, and primary. Simply put, the Nascent Soul Stage refers to a ‘primordial infant.’”

“So?”

“So, this little Meng fellow isn’t at the Nascent Soul but at the ‘Two Infants Stage.’”

Lu Yang’s eye twitched. Senior Lianyi’s naming skills are on par with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded in the mental space. “The name is not bad! It fits the actual thing perfectly!”

Lu Yang, “...”

Can’t you at least call it the “Double Infants Stage?”

Meng Jingzhou didn’t care about the name of the cultivation realm; he simply knew he had dual nascent souls.

The two nascent souls retreated into the cave abode with a whoosh. The various unusual phenomena transformed into petals, raining down beautifully.

With a wide smile, Meng Jingzhou pushed open the door to his cave abode, refreshed and delighted with his breakthrough.

Only Lu Yang knew he was delighted about the perfect conclusion of his performance.

“Congratulations, Junior Brother Meng! Shattering the golden core to form a nascent soul, your future is boundless!”

“Two nascent souls are unheard of! Junior Brother Meng, you have made history! This calls for a celebration!”

“Congratulations on achieving the Nascent Soul Stage, Senior Brother Meng! We must regard you as our idol and boldly strive forward!”

“Not at all, you flatter me; you’re exaggerating, fellow senior brothers and senior sisters. I’m just an ordinary Nascent Soul cultivator. I don’t deserve such praise.” Despite what he said, Meng Jingzhou was so jubilant that his heart blossomed with flowers.

Once the crowd had mostly dispersed, Lu Yang and Jiang Lianyi walked over.

“Old Lu, you’re here! Did you see my performance? Serves you right for breaking through early! Now you can’t enjoy such treatment!” Meng Jingzhou boasted smugly.

Heartless brat, who told you to go against your conscience and break through first!

Upon spotting Jiang Lianyi beside Lu Yang, his expression shifted, and he hurriedly bowed. “Greetings, Senior Lianyi.”

Although Jiang Lianyi had changed her appearance, Meng Jingzhou wasn’t stupid. The person beside Lu Yang could only be Jiang Lianyi.

Hearing Meng Jingzhou’s words, the old horse galloped over and spoke in the human tongue. “Greetings, Phoenix Ancestor!”

This is the legendary Phoenix Ancestor, second only to the Demon Immortal! I never imagined I’d get to meet her in this lifetime!

“Holy crap, old horse, you can speak?” After all these years, this was Meng Jingzhou’s first time hearing the old horse talk.

Jiang Lianyi glanced at the old horse. “Demon king level. Are you this kid’s guardian?”

The old horse didn’t dare hide anything. “Entrusted by Elder Brother, I am to ensure no one else beats him to death before Elder Brother can do it himself.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Dad, you really hold grudges, huh? I’ve almost forgotten what I did.

Fortunately, Meng Jingzhou wasn’t one to hold grudges. He quickly tossed aside his father’s grudge toward him and discussed the matter of his Nascent Soul Stage with Lu Yang.

“Congratulations, Old Meng. Senior Lianyi said it’s her first time seeing someone with twin nascent souls; it’s unprecedented. So, you’re now not at the Nascent Soul Stage but the Two Infants Soul Stage.”

Meng Jingzhou wanted to question what a terrible name it was, but considering it was given by the Phoenix Ancestor—who was right before him—he didn’t dare criticize it.

“...Good name.”

“Well? What unusual changes have you noticed at the Nascent Soul Stage?” Lu Yang asked eagerly. You have two children! It must feel different from the ordinary Nascent Soul Stage.

“My strength goes without saying; it’s definitely been elevated. The main thing is I feel my blood has changed.”

“Your blood has changed? What changed?”

With a straight face, Meng Jingzhou replied seriously, “It can boost yang.”

“...Are there other changes?” Lu Yang looked at Meng Jingzhou strangely. Old Meng is not far away from becoming Tang Monk’s flesh now—everyone will want a bite of him.

“There should be, but I haven’t found them yet. I’ll need to explore slowly.”

With the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s precedent allowed Lu Yang to learn its features directly. However, Meng Jingzhou had no reference, so he could only research step by step.

“What about you? How’s your nascent soul?”

Lu Yang immediately grew spirited. “My nascent soul was personally guided by an ancient immortal herself! It’s called the Unbeatable Nascent Soul! It can fight automatically, executing the most suitable move with the most suitable force at the most suitable opportunity to defeat enemies. Even I am no match for it as an opponent!”

Meng Jingzhou sucked in a breath. Old Lu’s nascent soul sounds so incredible, completely out of my league.

Lu Yang said, “Alright, you have just broken through and need to stabilize your cultivation realm. Senior Lianyi and I shall not disturb you further.”

“I won’t see you off then.”

According to the rules, outsiders were not allowed in the scripture library.

Seeing Yun Zhi’s note, Zhou Lulu didn’t question further. “Go in then. Remember not to damage the books.”

“Understood.”

The two went to the second floor, which housed Golden Core and Nascent Soul cultivation techniques. When Lu Yang compiled the Golden Core chapter of the Clear Heart True Nature Mantra, he had stayed here for a full month.

“Senior, feel free to look around. I’ll go study cultivation techniques now.” Lu Yang temporarily bade goodbye to Jiang Lianyi.

After Lu Yang left, Jiang Lianyi brimmed with interest as she examined these cultivation techniques she had never heard of, sensing the rapid changes of the times.

“Great Sun Dharma Body Art, Crane Cry Art, Farming Art... Hmm, why is this book hidden?”

She noticed the cultivation techniques on the bottommost shelf of the bookshelves on the east side were rarely touched and covered in dust. They were likely common manuals seen in the market.

Pushing these aside, she found a hidden compartment behind, extremely well-concealed. She opened it and found a book inside.

“Dragon Phoenix Transformation?”
