Chapter 630: This Tribulation Is Written in the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s Destiny

Jiang Lianyi’s expression was one of slight bafflement. Judging by the title, this should be a cultivation technique related to the Dragon and Phoenix tribes. It seems to be a spell for humans to temper their bodies.

“I never saw techniques for humans to transform into dragons or phoenixes in the ancient era. Is this a recent creation?”

Curious, she carefully opened the book.

Then, all sorts of indecent vocabulary jumped out before her eyes, vividly describing the mating process of dragons and phoenixes. It truly gave her a shock, and she dropped the book as if she was electrocuted.

“This...this...this...this is outrageous!”

Such books did not exist in the ancient era.

“Senior Lianyi, what’s wrong?”

Hearing the commotion, Lu Yang hurried over. The second floor was quiet; if one raised their voice slightly, anyone else could hear it.

“Who is the author of this book?”

“Which book?”

Lu Yang closed the book and saw the title on its cover. He fell silent for a long time.

Why is this book everywhere?

The first time I came to the scripture library, I stumbled upon this book, thinking it was my fortuitous encounter and that the manual might contain some mysterious cultivation technique. Then, the senior brother in the scripture library told me that this thing is a dirty book.

Just before I left for the Demon Region, I learned from Grandpa Ba that Shifu wrote this thing and that the copy in the scripture library might be the original.

The copies of Dragon Phoenix Transformation in the outside world had been destroyed. And wasn’t the copy on the first floor confiscated by the scripture library senior brother? Why is there another one on the second floor?

Shifu, exactly how many copies did you hide in the scripture library? Is it appropriate to use the idiom “a crafty rabbit has three burrows” here?

“Who wrote this book?” Jiang Lianyi fumed, determined to make the author regret it.

Lu Yang felt his scalp tingle at the question. This concerns Shifu’s life. Since joining the sect, Shifu has treated me well—though he was often absent from the sect, never guided me in my cultivation, frequently made enemies everywhere, causing me to be afraid of announcing which sect I’m from, and often spent time in jail, leaving me forbidden from taking the imperial examinations to become an official.

No matter what, despite all his faults, he’s still my shifu!

“It was written by my shifu, the Taciturn Daoist Priest.”

This tribulation is written in Shifu’s destiny; it is a calamity but also an opportunity. Shifu often taught Big Senior Sister that with pressure comes motivation. Surely, Shifu has already mentally prepared for this.

Jiang Lianyi nodded slightly, the corners of her mouth curling into a frightening smile. “Our Dao-Seeking Sect’s leader, the Taciturn Daoist Priest?”

“That’s right.”

“Where is he now?”

“Roaming the world, his whereabouts unknown; even the sect elders can’t locate him.”

“Got it. I’ll search for him after I go out then.” Jiang Lianyi kept the Dragon Phoenix Transformation book. The contents must not be seen by outsiders.

Just then, a stooped old man with an ordinary appearance and scrawny face approached.

“Fellow Daoist, this book belongs to our scripture library. Little Yun’s note only permits you to enter and read freely; it didn’t mention anything about taking books away, right?” The voice was weathered and full of stories. He spoke slowly but with undeniable authority.

“Elder Tao.” Lu Yang bowed with cupped fists. This is a figure from Grand-Shifu’s generation who came here to guard the scripture library after retiring. His cultivation is unfathomable.

Jiang Lianyi sneered and revealed her true appearance, not paying any heed to the old man.

“Phoenix Ancient Ancestor?!” Elder Tao’s eyes widened abruptly, his eyelids twitching. As a cultivator from the older generation, his knowledge surpassed even the eight elders’. He had seen Jiang Lianyi’s statue in the Demon Region.

“Heh, so what if I want to take it away?” Jiang Lianyi challenged.

Elder Tao was also tough. “Then take it! It’s not like I’m stopping you!”

Lu Yang, “...”

~~~

While things remained calm within the Dao-Seeking Sect, the outside world was thrown into turmoil as news spread of the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor, a legendary ancient great demon, awakening.

The Demon Region, the East Sea, the Buddhist Kingdom, the imperial court, the jianghu, the Three Great Diabolic Creeds, and the underground black markets—wherever cultivators were present, all were astonished by the news.

“The Phoenix Ancestor, who was missing for three hundred thousand years, is actually alive? And her combat power is no less than in those years, defeating Supreme Lord Zhu Tian, who is hailed as the number one below immortals?”

“Besides, the Phoenix Ancestor claims to be one of the Heavenly Court’s Four Regents! The young creed leader of the Heavenly Court Creed also appeared with her at the Demon Kingdom’s founding ceremony!”

“The Heavenly Court Creed has such terrifying depth?”

“Moreover, the Qilin immortal and the Phoenix Ancestor are actually married! The Phoenix Tribe’s depth likely far exceeds the world’s imagination. No wonder it was rumored in ancient times that no half-immortals dared to provoke the Phoenix Ancestor. With the Qilin Immortal as her backer, none would dare indeed.”

In a small tavern, drunk patrons discussed the events in the Demon Region animatedly, as if they had witnessed the astounding half-immortal battle themselves.

“Wait, Supreme Lord Zhu Tian and the Phoenix Ancestor—does that mean the Demon Region has two half-immortals?”

On the surface, no major factions had half-immortals; the peak was the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. This implied that the Demon Region had suddenly become the strongest faction.

“Half-immortals, huh...”

Be it Foundation Establishment great cultivators or Nascent Soul old monsters, their hearts were filled with awe and reverence at the mention of half-immortals, a realm they could never hope to reach in this lifetime. Most Foundation Establishment great cultivators didn’t even know the “half-immortal” realm existed. Now that they have learned about it, they could boast about this knowledge after returning.

Divine Transfiguration cultivators were considered the pillars of the cultivation world. Their sense of smell was sharper, and they detected an unusual scent from this matter.

“Two half-immortals awakening in succession is likely no coincidence. This is the prelude to the Battle of the Great Era...” An old man in a dirty Daoist robe listened to the news intermittently, sighing more deeply than the others.

“How did Little Yang establish a connection with the Phoenix Ancestor and trick her into our Heavenly Court Creed? Even I couldn’t have achieved that.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest was puzzled.

Every time I hear about my youngest disciple, it refreshes my understanding.

“Little Yang is bold enough to dupe even the Phoenix Ancestor. Next time I see him, I must tell him not to deceive people he can’t afford to offend, for it’ll easily lead to disaster.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest had plenty of experience in deception. His survival wasn’t due to sheer luck but a single principle he adhered to—never provoke those you couldn’t afford to offend. For example, for big shots like the Phoenix Ancestor, he would definitely run as far as he could, avoiding them entirely.

“Hmm? Someone’s coming?” The Taciturn Daoist Priest acutely sensed a Fusion expert drawing near, with a wild aura unlike a human’s.

A burly middle-aged man walked into the small tavern and sat beside the Taciturn Daoist Priest. His deep voice held a respect for knowledge. “I heard you compiled the latest hit, Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect. Are you still accepting disciples?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest saw the man’s face and paused slightly. “Chieftain Jin?”

Chapter 631: Manifold Nascent Soul Cultivation Techniques

Chieftain Jin was equally stunned. He glanced left and right but failed to recognize the disguised Taciturn Daoist Priest. “You know me?”

I had journeyed all the way to Great Xia in search of its top storyteller. Why does this man recognize me?

Am I that famous?

Chieftain Jin grew wary. His aura circulated, murderous energy slicing through his collar. He suspected the other party was a creditor, but then recalled his only creditor was now the Meng Family.

“It’s me, the Taciturn Daoist Priest,” the Taciturn Daoist Priest said in a low voice, unafraid of exposing his identity. He had no grudges with the Qiongqi Tribe.

I’m someone with principles; I choose who I deceive carefully—I don’t scam the poor. The Qiongqi Tribe is poor enough; no need to torment them further.

As for Chieftain Jin accidentally stumbling into the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, that’s Eighth Elder’s doing. What does that have to do with me?

I’m not afraid of Chieftain Jin having ill intentions and evil schemes.

Could someone with ill intentions and evil schemes be this poor?

“Taciturn Daoist Priest?” Chieftain Jin’s eyes widened. No wonder the pingshu performance is called Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect. Their own sect leader is doing the storytelling. Makes perfect sense.

“Wait, how did you find me?”

“Oh, that’s simple. In my earlier years, I didn’t repay my debts and hid everywhere. As my experience in hiding built up, my experience in finding people increased too.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest, “...”

“You want to become my apprentice and learn storytelling?” The Taciturn Daoist Priest was somewhat hesitant. This is my first time encountering a disciple actively seeking me out.

Chieftain Jin was also somewhat hesitant. The Taciturn Daoist Priest has a bad reputation. Would becoming his apprentice affect my reputation?

But on second thought, the Taciturn Daoist Priest is truly a good teacher with his gift of the gab and excellent deception skills—exactly what I lack. As the saying goes, ‘use others’ strengths to make up for your weaknesses.’ This is how it should be.

He gritted his teeth. As the saying goes, ‘fortune favors the bold.’ If I want to acquire real abilities, I must take risks.

I’ll gamble!

“Yes, I’m here to ask you to become my shifu!”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest felt Chieftain Jin’s firm resolve and was deeply moved. Although the Qiongqi Tribe’s fate profile is strange and prone to attracting calamity, where even the Luodi Merchant Guild doesn’t dare to take them in, I have always been cautious; I probably won’t run into trouble.

“Formally becoming my apprentice is not necessary. You’re almost a thousand years old. Our Dao-Seeking Sect doesn’t accept disciples that old. But you can follow me and learn.”

~~~

Despite betraying his shifu, Lu Yang continued studying cultivation techniques in the scripture library with a clear conscience.

Jiang Lianyi was also not in a hurry to search for the Taciturn Daoist Priest. In any case, he can’t leave Great Xia. My foremost priority is to learn about the changes in the cultivation world over the past three hundred thousand years.

If she encountered anything she didn’t understand, she could ask Elder Tao directly. Faced with the Phoenix Ancestor’s questions, Elder Tao naturally shared everything he knew. He had no intention of probing how Jiang Lianyi came to the sect.

Since Little Yun sent her, she’s naturally trusted. As a retiree, managing the small scripture library is enough. The sect’s affairs are for the younger generation. Moreover, when I answer the Phoenix Ancestor’s questions, she can also talk about ancient secrets—a mutually beneficial exchange.

The repository had a comprehensive collection of cultivation techniques. The last time Lu Yang came, he was still at the Basic Golden Core Stage. He browsed a few Nascent Soul cultivation manuals and found them obscure. Now, with a higher cultivation and a broader perspective, he no longer had difficulties grasping them.

“Pure Yang Cultivation Technique... Oh, it’s an ancestral cultivation technique for those with a Single Spirit Root. No need to read it.” Based on my understanding, this manual either contains inspirational messages and quotes from Single Spirit Root seniors, essentially chicken soup for the soul[1] without actual substance or gentle cultivation methods, like cooling down with ice when feeling hot, or radical cultivation methods, like taking aphrodisiacs to boost yang energy and pushing through by risking breakdown.

The last method can boost the cultivation speed of those with a Single Spirit Root, but it also carries huge risks. I heard several seniors couldn’t withstand the effects of the aphrodisiacs.

With Old Meng’s Nirvana True Fire, even those seniors who consumed aphrodisiacs would call his approach too radical.

“Mountain-Moving Art: a body-refining cultivation technique. Major mastery allows Nascent Soul cultivators to reach the pinnacle of strength, moving mountains and filling seas effortlessly.” Lu Yang sucked in a cold breath. This Mountain-Moving Art is really impressive. Old Meng can practice this. As for me, I’m not a body refiner, so I can’t cultivate it.

“If you want to refine your body, there’s a shortcut,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy kindly suggested upon seeing Lu Yang’s interest.

“What shortcut?”

“Getting struck by lightning. If you can survive the lightning tribulation, it can temper the body considerably. The Heaven Mandate Immortal often did this before immortal ascension. If not for great luck and ample pills, he would have been struck dead.

“But it was really effective. During that time, the Heaven Mandate Immortal could overpower the Qilin Immortal and give him a beating. Later, the Qilin Immortal got desperate and also endured lightning tribulations, resulting in a draw between the two. They mutually improved through competition, and it became a celebrated tale, inspiring various prodigies to emulate them—though many got struck dead.”

Lightning tribulations weren’t only for breakthroughs of cultivation realms. One could deliberately attract them over.

“I’m only at the Nascent Soul Stage. Wouldn’t getting struck by lightning be dangerous?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hand dismissively. My plans are foolproof, and I calculate everything beforehand. “What’s there to be scared of? Have you forgotten about the Unbeatable Nascent Soul? If you really can’t survive the lightning tribulation, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul will flee as a warning. It’s very safe.”

“...The Unbeatable Nascent Soul will be safe, but what about me?”

This question is a bit tricky. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy couldn’t think of a good solution for the time being. “Uh, I could show myself and tell the lightning tribulation to go back?”

“Are you sure the lightning tribulation will give you face?”

“Hard to say. Powerful lightning tribulations like the Nine Heavens Dark Lightning will give me face. But you’re only at the Nascent Soul Stage; it’ll definitely be insignificant lightning tribulations that probably haven’t seen me before.”

Lu Yang shook his head. He tossed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s proposal to the back of his mind and continued researching the cultivation techniques.

“Myriad Tribulations Imperishable Art: a cultivation technique specialized in tempering the Nascent Soul. Major mastery makes the nascent soul undying, imperishable, and eternal, unharmed even by falling stars or myriad tribulations.”

Lu Yang sucked in another cold breath. I didn’t expect such a formidable, top-tier cultivation manual to be casually sitting on the bookshelf like this! If I can master this, I may become even stronger than the Unbeatable Nascent Soul.

He looked up to confirm this wasn’t the “Yun Zhi Section” before continuing flipping through the pages to find out how this technique was cultivated.

“To achieve a Myriad Tribulations Imperishable Nascent Soul, one must first have the nascent soul survive myriad tribulations.

“...Damn it, so it’s a theoretical cultivation technique,” Lu Yang grumbled. I forgot that such a category of cultivation techniques exists. They are called theoretical cultivation techniques, feasible in theory and limited to theory—no one has ever succeeded in practice.

This type of cultivation technique is either for scamming laymen or whimsical ideas from mighty cultivation experts.

“Who wrote this... Tao Ran? Never heard of the name.”

Lu Yang seemed to recall something and turned to look at Elder Tao, who was explaining modern cultivation concepts to Jiang Lianyi nearby.

I think I’ve found the author.

1. This is the Chinese translation of the title of the 1993 self-help bestseller, Chicken Soup for the Soul. The book is a collection of feel-good, motivational, and inspirational stories. However, when used in Chinese, the term “chicken soup” sometimes has the sarcastic undertone of lacking actual substance. It depends on the context. ☜

Chapter 632: Second Senior Brother Defeated His Own Nascent Soul

“...Looks like Elder Tao really does have a lot of free time.”

Lu Yang silently placed the cultivation manual back and continued studying others.

Nascent Soul cultivation techniques were diverse. Rather than cultivation techniques, one could say they were more like collisions of philosophies.

For example, some seniors advocated seeking life through death, believing that one could only improve and sublimate their nascent soul by facing desperate situations.

On the other hand, others felt that cultivation should progress gradually, not to be rushed.

Lu Yang leaned toward the latter. With the Everlasting Immortal Fairy in my mental space, it is already a desperate situation of death. If I face another desperate situation, it’ll be ten deaths. No sublimation will be useful.

“This cultivation technique looks good—Nascent Soul Sword-Nurturing Technique. Seems suitable for me; I can use it as a reference.

“This cultivation technique uses the nascent soul as a scabbard to nurture a heart-sword. Once the heart-sword is formed, it can wield a sword. Based on a conservative estimate, the nascent soul’s combat power increases by thirty percent!”

The nascent soul is transformed from one’s golden core and controlled by one’s primordial spirit. Since it lacks a tangible body, it doesn’t have a proper weapon. The addition of a weapon will naturally increase its combat power.

“This cultivation technique is useless to you,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy reminded him.

“Why’s that?”

“Because the Unbeatable Nascent Soul can already wield a sword. The goal of this technique is already met.”

“The Unbeatable Nascent Soul can perform sword techniques? Why haven’t I seen it?” Lu Yang recalled his painful exchange with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, but didn’t remember it using sword techniques.

“Because you didn’t use sword techniques during the duel. Haven’t I told you? The Unbeatable Nascent Soul knows what you know and does it better. If you don’t believe me, just test it out.”

Lu Yang couldn’t suppress his curiosity. He entered his mental space and conjured a sword for himself. Then, he severed the link with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul and battled with it.

A miracle occurred.

This time, the more Lu Yang fought, the more valiant he became. Sword techniques came to him effortlessly, as if he was born with them. Clearly, he had broken through again in Sword Dao, reaching a level far beyond ordinary cultivators, one that would earn even applause from elders.

Then, he was defeated by the Unbeatable Nascent Soul.

“Ahem, why is this Unbeatable Nascent Soul so hard to beat? Immortal Fairy, how did you defeat it back then?” Lu Yang was pinned to the ground by the Unbeatable Nascent Soul and was being pummeled.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eyes darted evasively. “Tried...tried a few more times, and it could be defeated.”

Lu Yang stared at her suspiciously. “So how many times did you try?”

“I’m bad at math! I didn’t keep count!”

Lu Yang, “...”

He broke free from his mental space and comforted himself repeatedly. The Unbeatable Nascent Soul’s strength is a good thing...the Unbeatable Nascent Soul’s strength is a good thing...

Browsing as he walked, Lu Yang finally reached the “Yun Zhi Section” that he had yearned for, and he was thrilled by the first book he saw. freewebnovel.com

“This is Big Senior Sister’s cultivation insights at the Nascent Soul Stage? Let’s see how she cultivated her nascent soul.

“Step One: Shatter the golden core to form the nascent soul. Step Two: Pass the heavenly tribulation...”

Hmm? Why is step two already different from the others?

“Now that I think about it, I seem to have heard someone mention that Big Senior Sister already faced a heavenly tribulation when she was breaking through to the Nascent Soul Stage, while other cultivators face it when breaking through to the Divine Transfiguration Stage.

“Second Senior Brother emulated her and also faced a heavenly tribulation at the Nascent Soul Stage. Then, his nascent soul gained sentience and beat him up.”

Lu Yang felt a connection with Ye Zijin. Although we’ve never met, we’re already senior and junior brothers whose fates are joined.

“Elder Tao, how did Big Senior Sister manage to attract a heavenly tribulation at the Nascent Soul Stage?” Lu Yang asked Elder Tao.

“Oh, that? Back then, Little Yun was at the Apex Golden Core Stage. She accidentally stumbled into an ancient trial ground. There, she fought the phantom of the previous record holder and defeated it, clinching first place.”

“Who was the previous record holder?” Jiang Lianyi was curious. If it was an ancient figure, I should have heard of them.

“The Heaven Mandate Immortal.”

Lu Yang, “...”

So Heaven Mandate Immortal, you lost your temper over your defeat and zapped Big Senior Sister with lightning, huh?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded. “Sounds like something the Heaven Mandate Immortal would do. He often withdrew his moves when playing Five in a Row.

“And you let him withdraw his moves?”

“Of course. Why wouldn’t we let him? Chess is about fairness. If he withdrew his moves, we would hit him. After the beating, we would regret it and say we shouldn’t have hit him, pretending it never happened.”

Lu Yang, “...”

“I remember the ancient trial ground Lass Yun went to. It existed before ancient times. The Heaven Mandate Immortal went there at the Golden Core Stage and broke the record, becoming number one. He caused quite a stir then.
