“After becoming an immortal, he probably left a spell there, something like ‘if anyone breaks his record, they’ll get struck by lightning.’ It can’t exactly be considered revenge—well, not entirely. At least, being struck by lightning does strengthen the nascent soul.”

Lu Yang continued to ask Elder Tao. “Then what about Second Senior Brother? Did he also enter the ancient trial ground and break the record?” It seems Second Senior Brother is even more impressive than I thought.

“You’re talking about Little Ye? He wanted to go, but it wasn’t possible. After Little Yun left the ancient trial ground, it closed and could never be reopened. Even now, no one knows why.”

Jiang Lianyi could roughly guess the reason. The Heaven Mandate Immortal was someone with principles. “He was probably afraid someone else would surpass his record. His principle was that he couldn’t lose face twice.”

“...Quite principled,” Lu Yang remarked weakly. “Then where did Second Senior Brother’s lightning tribulation come from?”

“He cursed the Heaven Mandate Immortal for a full day.”

Lu Yang inhaled sharply. As expected of Second Senior Brother, he’s got guts. Even if I have the Everlasting Immortal Fairy protecting me, I wouldn’t dare treat the Heaven Mandate Immortal that way.

Elder Tao continued, “You know the rest. When this kid shattered his golden core to form a nascent soul, he drew a massive heavenly tribulation over—two lightning strikes right at the start.

“The lightning bolts opened up Little Ye’s nascent soul into enlightenment. His nascent soul was eye-opening. It could fly to the sky and shatter the lightning tribulation, then return to the body to beat up its master.” Elder Tao clicked his tongue in amazement. I have never seen something so absurd in my five thousand years of living.

Lu Yang was envious as he listened. My nascent soul will only flee when I face a lightning tribulation. “I heard that Second Senior Brother destroyed his nascent soul and refined a new one?”

“That’s just a lie to outsiders. The truth is a bit complicated and is inconvenient to share publicly. But you’re not outsiders, so it’s fine to tell you. In reality, Little Ye defeated his own nascent soul.”

Lu Yang was moved. This is the breakthrough I want most! “How did he defeat it?”

Elder Tao replied, “He said that no matter how strong the nascent soul was, it was still a part of him. Since it was a part of him, the whole must be stronger than a part, so he could definitely defeat his nascent soul!

“He also said that a spiritual victory is still a victory.”

Chapter 633: There Are No Shortcuts in Cultivation

Lu Yang was astounded by his Second Senior Brother’s wisdom. What a genius method! Why didn’t I think of it?!

“Immortal Fairy, does this method work?” He turned to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy with hopeful eyes.

“You can lie to yourself. Your Second Senior Brother’s nascent soul has spirit intelligence, so you can fool it with a few words. But your nascent soul isn’t sentient. How are you going to hoodwink it?”

Lu Yang hung his head dispiritedly. It seems this method won’t work. I can only defeat the nascent soul through honest effort.

He returned to the “Yun Zhi Section” and studied Yun Zhi’s writings word by word. He found them to be rich with profound meaning and gained much from reading them. “As expected of Big Senior Sister. Her insights are very reasonable, and upon careful contemplation, deeper layers of truth can be gleaned.”

This is far more useful than the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s guidance. The more Lu Yang read, the more the articles resonated with him. It’s as if I have written them myself!

Two months passed in a flash. During this time, Lu Yang remained stationed in the scripture library and never left the second floor. He studied Nascent Soul cultivation techniques tirelessly until he forgot to eat and sleep, reaping significant gains.

Sitting cross-legged on a straw mat, he breathed evenly, as though he was asleep, yet seemingly in a deeper layer of comprehension. Various cultivation philosophies and methods swirled in his mind in a tangled mess. What he needed to do was to disentangle the chaos, extract the usable parts, and adapt them to his own situation, thereby creating a cultivation technique unique to himself.

Studying multiple cultivation techniques posed a heavy burden on a cultivator’s mind. Only Lu Yang, whose mental power was unbeatable among his peers, could handle it. Any other Nascent Soul cultivator would have been overwhelmed and passed out.

Lu Yang opened his eyes, his pupils sparkling, and a confident smile playing on his lips. He swiftly moved his brush across the paper and wrote a new chapter.

“This must be the cultivation technique Big Senior Sister wanted me to write.”

~~~

“Better than last time. I only need to revise eighty percent of it,” Yun Zhi declared after earnestly reviewing Lu Yang’s Nascent Soul Chapter of the Clear Heart True Nature Mantra.

Last time, when Lu Yang wrote the Golden Core chapter, eighty percent of it also required revision. However, the remaining twenty percent needed no revision because it was directly copied from Yun Zhi.

This time, at least the remaining twenty percent was original content Yun Zhi approved of.

“What does your nascent soul look like? What are its special features? Release it for me to take a look.” Before modifying the cultivation technique, Yun Zhi wanted to see Lu Yang’s nascent soul and make targeted revisions.

“Uh...that’s a bit difficult.” Lu Yang revealed a troubled expression. Until he could defeat the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, he couldn’t let it out.

Yun Zhi raised an eyebrow. “Where can I see it?”

“In my mental space.”

Without another word, Yun Zhi’s soul left her body and flew into Lu Yang’s mental space.

Jiang Lianyi was also curious about Lu Yang’s nascent soul. According to what he said, his golden core is the same as Everlasting-jiejie’s, so it should also be the case for his nascent soul. But I’ve forgotten what Everlasting-jiejie’s golden core and nascent soul were like.

During the two months in the scripture library, she had roughly grasped the situation of the current cultivation world; staying longer was unnecessary.

Lu Yang’s mental space instantly became lively with the indigenous resident Everlasting Immortal Fairy, visitor Yun Zhi, visitor Jiang Lianyi, and tenant Lu Yang.

Lu Yang severed the link with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul with familiarity, was brutally thrashed by it with familiarity, and reconnected the link with it with familiarity.

Performance over.

Yun Zhi’s and Jiang Lianyi’s expressions were also spectacular. Yun Zhi recalled her Second Junior Brother, whom she hadn’t seen in a long while, while Jiang Lianyi hated her amnesia, which caused her to forget that her Everlasting-jiejie also used to have such exciting experiences.

However, Yun Zhi was the Big Senior Sister after all. She discerned that Lu Yang’s nascent soul differed from Ye Zijin’s.

Lu Yang explained, “The Everlasting Immortal Fairy told me that in theory, so long as I defeat the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, I’ll be able to use it.”

Yun Zhi cast a meaningful look at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “In theory, huh...”

As if her little schemes had been seen through by Yun Zhi, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s gaze drifted away, avoiding Yun Zhi’s eyes.

Yun Zhi turned around, her countenance serious. “If you wish to defeat your nascent soul, you cannot pull any tricks. Just as there are no shortcuts in cultivation, you must cultivate steadily and surpass your nascent soul in every aspect!”

Lu Yang humbly consulted, “Big Senior Sister, then how did you reach such a realm in less than a thousand years?”

“Through talent.”

Lu Yang, “...”

“Alright, I already know how to revise your cultivation technique. It’ll be done in two hours.”

Yun Zhi exited the mental space and waved for Lu Yang and Jiang Lianyi to leave. She preferred writing cultivation techniques alone. In reality, her main goal was to make the Everlasting Immortal Fairy leave.

Too noisy.

As her Little Junior Brother, Lu Yang obeyed Yun Zhi’s words.

As an evenly matched rival, Jiang Lianyi respected the creed leader.

The two descended the mountain.

“By the way, I haven’t introduced you yet, Senior. There’s one more person in the Everlasting Lineage you haven’t met.” Lu Yang remembered the third-in-command.

In private, Lu Yang had asked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy whether Jiang Lianyi counted as a member of the Everlasting Lineage, and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy firmly said no.

“Although Lianyi and Little Ling studied under me, they achieved nothing in the Dao of Everlasting. Moreover, their Dao Fruits are destined for the Survival of the Fittest Lineage.”

The Everlasting Lineage had strict criteria.

It was afternoon but not yet mealtime. The barbeque stall wasn’t open, its staff deftly using arrays to skewer the ingredients.

After many improvements, from only skewering meat, the array could now skewer enoki mushrooms, green beans, and more. It had become a versatile professional skewering array!

With the Everlasting Immortal’s strategy of “attack far, befriend nearby,” the barbeque shop’s influence grew underground, secretly controlling numerous restaurants. It had become a bona fide industry giant!

Lu Yang was surprised to run into someone in front of the shop.

“Junior Brother Man, what brings you here?”

“Senior Brother Lu, it’s been a long while since we last met. Over half a year, right?” Man Gu grinned, rubbing the back of his head. “I just broke through to the Nascent Soul Stage, so I’m here for barbeque skewers to celebrate.”

“Congratulations, Junior Brother Man! Your cultivation progress is pretty fast, eh?” Lu Yang smiled. “Shall we eat together?”

Man Gu naturally agreed.

Noticing Man Gu’s identity, Jiang Lianyi exclaimed softly, “Hmm? This little fellow is the last Ancient Barbarian?”

“Speaking of which, Senior, since the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s existence was erased, how did the Ancient Barbarian Tribe come to be in your memory?”

According to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, the Barbarian Tribe lived on the North Star. She planted a Tame Head Curse on their bloodline, creating the Ancient Barbarians, whose bloodline traits included countering demons. Since the mastermind behind the scenes erased the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s existence, the Ancient Barbarian Tribe’s origin should have also changed.

Jiang Lianyi’s expression turned peculiar. “It’s said that the Heaven Mandate Immortal was fond of women, regardless of whether they were beautiful or ugly. One of them was the Ancient Barbarian Tribe’s female ancestor, and from this union, the first generation of Ancient Barbarians was born.”

Chapter 634: Man Gu’s Nascent Soul

Lu Yang was not surprised that the mastermind behind the scenes attributed the origin of the Ancient Barbarian Tribe to the Heaven Mandate Immortal instead of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

Given that the authorship of the Demon Beast Cookbook had been altered from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to the Heaven Mandate Immortal, and that the bloodline suppression the Ancient Barbarian Tribe exerted over demon beasts couldn’t be erased, the only plausible course of action was to make the Heaven Mandate Immortal the progenitor of the Ancient Barbarian Tribe. That way, the bloodline suppression issue could be explained.

Man Gu’s features embodied a masculine handsomeness among men, but they would be terrifying if he were a woman. One could only infer that the Heaven Mandate Immortal was lascivious and possessed unique aesthetic tastes.

This was the most reasonable explanation.

After listening to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy recount her various misdeeds in the Ancient Barbarian Tribe, Jiang Lianyi realized her own memories had been tampered with. What terrifying methods.

“Brother Lu, who is this...” Man Gu looked at Jiang Lianyi in puzzlement. I don’t think I’ve seen this person in the Dao-Seeking Sect before.

“She’s Jiang Lianyi, a new member of our Heavenly Court Creed. Her identity is one of the Four Regents and the Phoenix Tribe’s Ancient Ancestor.”

Since we’re all members of the Heavenly Court Creed, there’s no need to hide things from each other. Moreover, Man Gu had witnessed my misfortune in accidentally resurrecting the Everlasting Immortal Fairy; he knows more than even the sect elders.

Man Gu stumbled several steps backward. His pupils contracted sharply, his face distorted in shock, to the point that his newly broken-through Nascent Soul Stage showed signs of instability. He had been in seclusion for the past two months for a breakthrough, unaware of the heaven-shaking and earth-shattering changes that had occurred in the outside world.

“Ph-Ph-Ph-Ph-Phoenix Tribe...” Man Gu stammered as if he had seen a ghost.

Lu Yang patted Man Gu’s shoulder, signaling him to calm down. He guided Man Gu into the barbeque shop and pressed him onto a stool. Only after Man Gu gulped down two large pots of tea did he regain his composure slightly.

Seeing Lu Yang here, Chef Liu attended to him as if he was serving his own ancestor while secretly transmitting an auditory message to his creed leader and the Everlasting Immortal, urging them to come quickly.

“Junior Brother Man, it seems you have been cultivating very diligently lately, being in seclusion and cut off from the outside world. Quite a lot has happened recently...” Lu Yang smiled as he slowly recounted his experiences in the Demon Region.

Man Gu gazed at Lu Yang in admiration. This is my true role model. When will I ever reach such a level? The sages speak of maintaining composure in the face of major events—they’re practically describing Brother Lu!

In contrast, I had lost my composure merely upon meeting the living Phoenix Ancient Ancestor. This is truly unacceptable! I must reflect upon myself!

“Second-in-Command, you’ve arrived?” The Everlasting Immortal and the Everlasting Creed Leader hurried over from the breeding farm, covered in dust.

“Might the lady beside you be the legendary Ancient Ancestor Jiang of the Phoenix Tribe?” the creed leader inquired cautiously after noticing the woman sitting quietly next to Lu Yang.

Although he had been working long-term at the breeding farm and the barbeque shop, he had not forgotten his original identity as a creed leader. Gathering and consolidating intelligence was his forte when he served as creed leader.

For instance, he had recently collected information such as the impending price hikes from the Food Stall Federation, plans by the Great Hotpot Alliance to launch new dishes, the opening of a new fried skewer shop on the commercial street, and the establishment of the Demon Kingdom.

Putting the information together, it’s not difficult to deduce that the person beside Lu Yang is the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor, who has altered her appearance.

Jiang Lianyi’s gaze swept past the creed leader and landed on the Everlasting Immortal. Her eyes narrowed slightly, her tone unfriendly. “You’re the one who nearly condensed the Everlasting Dao Fruit and prevented Everlasting-jiejie from resurrecting?”

Cold sweat broke out on the Everlasting Immortal’s forehead. He frantically said he didn’t dare to and almost fell onto his knees. When facing the Great Yu Imperial Preceptor, he still had some confidence to put up a fight. But against Jiang Lianyi, he could distinctly feel the gap between them. This isn’t an opponent I can contend with by relying on my self-detonation tactics alone. A direct confrontation will end in certain defeat!

Jiang Lianyi withdrew her gaze, letting the Everlasting Immortal off. “Forget it. You were merely a pawn pushed to the front by others. What purpose is there in finding trouble with you?”

The Everlasting Immortal felt as if he had been granted a great pardon.

Sensing the tense atmosphere, the creed leader quickly stepped in to smooth things over and presented a plate of grilled lamb skewers. “These are our improved lamb skewers. Everyone, please try them.”

With just the first bite, Lu Yang was slightly surprised. This improved formula is remarkable; it’s tastier than before!

Man Gu was somewhat dejected. Our Barbeque Barbarian Tribe lost...

“How did you achieve this?”

The creed leader brought out another plate of lamb skewers; this time, they were raw.

Lu Yang hadn’t paid close attention when he first entered the shop, but with the hint from the creed leader, he soon spotted the difference in these lamb skewers. “There’s no bloody smell, and just looking at the meat gives a sense of tranquility. Have these lamb skewers been blessed?”

The creed leader smiled modestly. “Something like that. Following the guidance of Master Shi Chan from the Hanging Monastery, we chant the Rebirth Requiem while slaughtering livestock. This dispels the lingering resentment of the livestock and elevates the quality of the meat to a whole new level.”

Lu Yang nodded in approval. This was something he hadn’t considered. It seems this Fellow Daoist Shi Chan, whom I have yet to meet, is truly brilliant; his intellect is on par with Meng Jingzhou and second only to mine.

“There’s certainly potential for promotion.” Lu Yang thought of the thriving “One More Time” barbeque chain outside. If we add these meat skewers cleansed with the Rebirth Requiem and enhance the flavor, business will likely soar to new heights.

Jiang Lianyi also found the skewers’ flavor decent. “The barbeque skewers are not bad, though not as good as what I can grill.”

Lu Yang broke into a cold sweat. Jiang Lianyi’s culinary skills could make even the Epoch Immortal see his life flash before his eyes. If one’s cultivation isn’t sufficient, who would dare to eat her barbeque skewers?

Fortunately, Jiang Lianyi had no intention of showing off her skills, which allowed Lu Yang to exhale a sigh of relief.

Chefs Liu and Gao worked deftly, serving plate after plate of fresh barbeque skewers.

“Come, let’s celebrate Junior Brother Man Gu’s breakthrough to the Nascent Soul Stage!” Lu Yang announced, raising a cup of tea.

“Wait a moment,” Man Gu said apologetically.

Just as Lu Yang and Jiang Lianyi wondered why, Man Gu released his nascent soul. His nascent soul was especially mature-looking. It had the body of an infant but the face of a man in his fifties or sixties.

Man Gu planted three lamb skewers in front of the nascent soul and bowed toward it respectfully. “Ancestor above, please partake of this meal.”

Ritual completed.

“Junior Brother Man, this nascent soul of yours looks rather mature...” Lu Yang’s eyelid twitched. What kind of strange nascent soul is this?

He looked toward Jiang Lianyi, who also shook her head, expressing that she had never seen such a situation.

Man Gu smiled sheepishly. “You know my golden core was the Ancestor Assembly Golden Core, right? It allowed me to invoke my ancestors to possess me and aid in battle. After shattering the golden core to form the nascent soul, the nascent soul took on the appearance of an ancestor. However, the appearance is random; the face changes frequently, and it’s uncertain which ancestor it will manifest as.

“Regardless of who it turns into, it’s still an ancestor, so I thought perhaps I should pay respects before eating?”

Lu Yang, “...”

“Does your nascent soul have any special features?”

“Yes. Whichever ancestor’s appearance the nascent soul takes on, I’ll gain some of that ancestor’s characteristics. If the ancestor was renowned for spatial spells during their life, I’ll be able to cast spatial spells. If the ancestor was renowned for speed during their life, my speed will increase.”

“That’s impressive! So this particular ancestor you just paid respects to, what was he renowned for in his life?”

“This ancestor was incredible. He followed an immortal in the ancient era and was renowned for his simple mind.”

Chapter 635: Meng Jingzhou’s New Move

A simple mind was not without its advantages. Simple-minded individuals could withstand mental attacks effectively.

Lu Yang seriously doubted whether his own mental attacks could harm Man Gu when the latter was bolstered by his ancestor.

The average person resisted mental attacks through direct confrontation, contesting whose mental power was stronger and who could utilize it better. However, those with simple minds were different. They were like a piece of cotton, able to absorb and cushion the impact of a mental assault.

While Man Gu’s nascent soul sounded impressive based on his description, its practical application had a major flaw—Man Gu could not recognize all his ancestors. This wasn’t Man Gu’s fault. Given the cultural level of the Ancient Barbarian Tribe, extremely few portraits had been passed down. The existing portraits were usually the work of painting cultivators who had passed by.

Hence, Man Gu could remember the characteristics of all his ancestors, but he couldn’t match them to their specific appearances. This made using his nascent soul highly unpredictable.

“The true name of this ancestor has been lost to time, but the stories of his deeds were passed down. It is said that although this ancestor had a simple mind, he also had great luck. Even if his actions took him in the complete opposite direction of his goal, he would still manage to reach it. Furthermore, this ancestor once touched upon the Dao of Life. It was a pity that he was interrupted just as he was about to achieve enlightenment.” Man Gu’s eyes shone with reverence. This was one of the most ancient of the Ancient Barbarians, one who had followed an ancient immortal; his status within the tribe spoke for itself.

“Immortal Fairy, do you recognize the ancestor Man Gu is worshipping?” Lu Yang eyed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy skeptically, suspecting that this prematurely aged nascent soul ancestor was one of her first victims.

“Man Ergou,[1] right? I know him well. This kid was very earnest about my lectures, always asking questions after class, like why demons need to wear clothes after taking human form if they don’t do so in their true forms. His attitude toward learning was far better than the other Barbarians.

“It’s just that his innate intellectual talent was lacking; he could never reach heights like mine.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head regretfully. He had been a highly promising student, but his natural aptitude was insufficient, and not even diligence could fully compensate for it.

Lu Yang thought, Just as I suspected, another victim.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued, “This kid was always getting lost. Once, he wanted to return to the Barbarian Tribe, but he ended up going in the opposite direction. He flew a complete circle around the North Star before finally making it back, and he was even late for class.

“He remembered me mentioning in class that cultivators should have a pioneering spirit and a drive for exploration. Thus, he was bent on drinking a few mouthfuls of water from the Mother-Child River to see if he could get pregnant. Qing He was beside him and stopped him, escorting him back to the tribe.

“Another time, he stumbled into a pond where a female cultivator was bathing and inadvertently saw her. The female cultivator screamed and insisted that Ergou compensate her, refusing to let it go. Then, two male cultivators jumped out, saying something like, ‘If you don’t give us a proper explanation today, this matter won’t be over.’

“How could Ergou have encountered a situation like that before? He was at a loss for what to do. Fortunately, he remembered my teachings: act with fairness, an eye for an eye, a tooth for a tooth, and correcting one’s mistakes is a great virtue.”

“What happened after that?”

“After that, he said, ‘I saw your body, so it’s only fair if you see mine. This way, it’ll be fair. Then, he started taking his clothes off.

“Those three people also didn’t know what was good for them. Seeing that Er Gou wasn’t offering spirit stones, they charged toward him at once to rob him. In the end, they still couldn’t beat Ergou.”

Lu Yang, “...”

This Ancient Barbarian ancestor is truly fearless and reckless like a tiger.

“Why is everyone here? Having a meal gathering without inviting me?” Meng Jingzhou swaggered into the barbeque shop as casually as if he was returning home.

He was passing by the barbeque shop and had a serious craving. As soon as he entered, he spotted Lu Yang and the others as well as Man Gu’s nascent soul, which shocked him. “Oh man! Junior Brother Man, this nascent soul of yours is very mature-looking, eh?”

And it also doesn’t look like you. Meng Jingzhou struggled to swallow the last few words, keeping them to himself.

Man Gu retracted his nascent soul and ate the tribute skewers on behalf of his ancestor before explaining the origin of his nascent soul.

Meng Jingzhou clicked his tongue in amazement as he listened. “Borrowing your ancestors’ power—as expected of the last Ancient Barbarian. Blessed by your bloodline, you have a very distinctive nascent soul. Junior Brother Man, I reckon you’ll surpass Lu Yang in no time and become the world’s number two Nascent Soul cultivator.”

Lu Yang shot a glance at Meng Jingzhou. “And who is the world’s number one Nascent Soul cultivator?”

Meng Jingzhou pointed at himself, speaking matter-of-factly. “Me, of course.”

“Aren’t you at the Two Infants Stage? Why are you pretending to be a Nascent Soul cultivator?”

Meng Jingzhou flared with anger. Lu Yang, you brat really don’t know how to speak properly. If the Phoenix Ancestor weren’t here, I’d definitely challenge you to show who’s better.

Although Lu Yang was also at the Two Infants Stage, no one knew about it, allowing him to masquerade as a Nascent Soul cultivator as he pleased.

“Two Infants Stage?” Man Gu rummaged through his memory of cultivation knowledge but couldn’t find a corresponding cultivation realm.

“Old Meng is a trailblazer. He has two nascent souls.”

“Two nascent souls?!” This time, it was Man Gu’s turn to be shocked. He had never heard of it, and neither had he read about any cultivator in history possessing dual nascent souls.

Becoming a trailblazer and creating a precedent... This is Brother Meng’s power!

Man Gu had been learning from Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou for two years, but until now, he still felt that the sea of knowledge was boundless. The depths and ideas of my two senior brothers are realms I can never dream of reaching in my entire life.

One should learn for as long as they live.

Just as Meng Jingzhou was about to flare up again and assert his position, Lu Yang seized the chance to cut off that line of thought. “Two months have passed; your cultivation realm should be stable now. What’s different about having two nascent souls?”

Sure enough, the moment the topic shifted to cultivation, Meng Jingzhou’s attention was diverted, and he grinned. “A huge gain. Let me demonstrate for you.” He chuckled smugly and activated his two nascent souls.

Two plump and fair-skinned babies, looking exactly like a younger version of Meng Jingzhou, sat on his shoulders.

“Merge!” Meng Jingzhou commanded softly.

The boundaries between the two nascent souls and himself blurred, and they gradually fused into one entity. Large bumps swelled on Meng Jingzhou’s neck, and two more appeared under each of his armpits.

“Ha!” Meng Jingzhou exerted force, and the bumps on his neck transformed into two additional heads, while four extra arms sprouted from under his armpits. “I just learned it, so I’m still not very proficient. Hehe, what do you think?”

“Dang, Three Heads Six Arms?!” Lu Yang was genuinely astonished. This is a move all physique cultivators dream of mastering. Based on what I know, among the Fusion cultivators, only a few like Third Elder know this move. Aside from them, only Transcendent Tribulation cultivators can perform this move. And they had guidance from predecessors.

On the other hand, Meng Jingzhou had learned it through self-study, equivalent to being the creator. His talent and comprehension are so high, second only to mine.

Isn’t this much more remarkable than my Unbeatable Nascent Soul?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy patted her chest reassuringly. “If you can defeat the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, I guarantee it will prove more powerful in a fight than his Three Heads Six Arms.”

Jiang Lianyi was also slightly stunned. Is this the talent exchanged from lifelong singlehood?

The human race is indeed formidable. No wonder only one of the ancient immortals was a demon. None of the demon prodigies at the kingdom-founding ceremony possessed this kind of talent.

Meng Jingzhou noticed Lu Yang’s expression and secretly brimmed with smug satisfaction.

Man Gu felt that Meng Jingzhou was truly amazing and praised him sincerely from the bottom of his heart. “Twins really are built different.”

1. “Er Gou” translates to something like “second dog.” ☜

Chapter 636: Nascent Soul Power-Borrowing

Noticing the varying degrees of astonishment on the three’s visages, Meng Jingzhou knew that his arduous training over the past two months had not been in vain.

How could a mere puny Lu Yang compare to me, the number one figure of the almighty Two Infants Stage?

There are advantages to being alone in a unique cultivation realm—I’m both the first and last in this cultivation realm.

Meng Jingzhou sat down. He picked up a couple of skewers and immediately realized something different upon sniffing them. “They smell more fragrant than before.”

After a couple of bites, he was sure his senses weren’t mistaken. “They taste better than before too.”

“They have been blessed,” Lu Yang told him.

“What do you mean by blessed?”

Lu Yang repeated the creed leader’s explanation verbatim, to which Meng Jingzhou also highly praised. It seems this Fellow Daoist Shi Chan, whom I have yet to meet, has some outstanding qualities. His intellect is on par with Lu Yang’s and second only to this young master’s.

With the flavor of the barbeque skewers elevated to a new level, Meng Jingzhou’s appetite improved. Holding a skewer in one hand and a cup of tea in the other, he clinked cups with Lu Yang and thoroughly enjoyed the meal. As for the grilled kidney skewers, roasted oysters, and whatnot, he accepted all that was available, which surprised Man Gu.

Noticing Man Gu’s bewilderment, Meng Jingzhou casually explained, “There’s another benefit after forming the nascent soul. My blood is the best yang-boosting tonic. Now, any yang-boosting tonic, aphrodisiacs, or similar substances have no effect on me.”

One could say that the Meng Jingzhou was a legendary potent tonic. A single drop of his blood released into the outside world would incite a frenzy and fetch an astronomical price.

If Meng Jingzhou were willing, he could live in a brothel, reveling night after night.

Was he willing? Of course, he was willing.

“Brother Meng, you’re amazing,” Man Gu complimented, giving a thumbs-up.

“Your constitution reminds me of Yang Kongtong,” Jiang Lianyi suddenly said.

“Who is Yang Kongtong?” Lu Yang searched his memory but couldn’t recall hearing the name.

“He’s the one who formed the Harem Golden Core. Didn’t Everlasting-jiejie tell you about him?” Jiang Lianyi was slightly stunned; Yang Kongtong had been very famous in the ancient era.

“...Oh, it’s him.” Lu Yang realized the Everlasting Immortal Fairy genuinely hadn’t mentioned this person’s name.

Jiang Lianyi continued, “Yang Kongtong’s Harem Golden Core allowed him to simultaneously obtain power from all members of his harem, causing his combat power to skyrocket. He was hailed as the number one Golden Core cultivator of ancient times.

“After he and his harem reached the Nascent Soul Stage, it became the Harem Nascent Soul. In battle, he could summon the nascent souls of his harem to fight alongside him.”

Lu Yang pictured the scene: Yang Kongtong goes into battle, followed by eight or nine babbling kids. It feels rather bizarre.

“Yang Kongtong’s constitution was called the Dual Cultivation Body. He was born with great romantic peach blossom luck and practiced Blissful Union methods. The more he engaged in dual cultivation with female cultivators, the faster his cultivation advanced.

“His constitution also made him exceptionally enduring in bedroom affairs. His blood also had yang-boosting properties. At its peak, his harem numbered over a hundred.”

Meng Jingzhou’s eyes turned red with envy. We both have yang-boosting constitutions, so why is the gap between us so vast?

Is there no justice in this world?

Jiang Lianyi comforted, “You needn’t envy him too much. Yang Kongtong had both peach blossom luck and peach blossom calamity. He failed to manage the conflicts within his harem and was ultimately killed by them. He died rather gruesomely and tragically, with his corpse dismembered.

Meng Jingzhou shuddered, feeling that his Single’s Spirit Root wasn’t so bad after all. “Wait a moment, Senior Lianyi, are you saying that Yang Kongtong could use his harem’s nascent souls to fight when he was at the Nascent Soul Stage?” he suddenly asked.

“Yes, is there a problem?”

Meng Jingzhou stroked his chin, a bold idea forming. “Since Yang Kongtong could use others’ nascent souls to fight, can’t I do the same?”

A question mark popped out of Jiang Lianyi’s head.

Meng Jingzhou elaborated with sincerity and patience. “Think about it. Yang Kongtong had a harem of nearly a hundred. Was that a harem? That was lust. If lust could allow him to borrow others’ nascent souls to fight, shouldn’t friendship allow me to borrow nascent souls to fight as well?”

Besides, I already have two nascent souls. What harm could a few more do?

Jiang Lianyi widened her eyes slightly, startled by Meng Jingzhou’s idea. More importantly, this is feasible in theory!

“Maybe it could work. I happen to have the cultivation manual Yang Kongtong used on hand. We can use it for reference.”

With this new idea, the four of them couldn’t sit still. They only ate half of their barbeque skewers before hurrying back to Heaven’s Gate Peak to discuss this method’s feasibility with Yun Zhi.

~~~

At the moment, Yun Zhi had just finished revising Lu Yang’s cultivation manual when she saw four people searching for her to explain their purpose in coming.

“Yang Kongtong? Dual Cultivation Body? Harem Golden Core?” Yun Zhi had not heard of this, as not every tale from antiquity had been passed down.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy emerged, confirming that Yang Kongtong did exist.

Man Gu was extremely excited to see the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. According to Lu Yang, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was the great immortal who had created our Ancient Barbarian lineage!

She’s the creator of the Ancient Barbarian Tribe!

Jiang Lianyi took out Yang Kongtong’s cultivation manual, titled Multiple Cultivation Techniques.

With four peerless experts—Yun Zhi, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Jiang Lianyi, and Lu Yang—present, they quickly deciphered the Multiple Cultivation Techniques.

“This manual mostly describes how to cultivate together with a harem, which is useless for Junior Brother Meng,” Yun Zhi said, pointing to two specific chapters. “However, the concept of ‘borrowing power’ during the Golden Core and Nascent Soul stages is applicable.”

This was a method she hadn’t considered before. Moreover, she had plenty of golden cores and didn’t need this method.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy suggested, “Let the Meng boy try first. His constitution is closest to Yang Kongtong’s, so he’s the most likely to succeed in Nascent Soul Power-Borrowing.” She casually decided the fate of a Nascent old monster.

The four peerless experts examined Meng Jingzhou while revising the cultivation technique.

The Nascent Soul old monster Man Gu could only wait quietly on the sidelines for the result. “Why wasn’t there an ancestor renowned for wisdom?” He ran through the characteristics of every ancestor and felt somewhat rueful.

Soon, half a day passed. They had researched from dusk until the wee hours and finally attained some results.

“Junior Brother Meng, try the method on this paper.” Yun Zhi had condensed the method onto a single piece of paper.

Meng Jingzhou treated it like a supreme treasure and began studying it earnestly. His cultivation comprehension was no weaker than Lu Yang’s. It didn’t take long for him to understand the method on paper, which essentially involved changing the ‘lust’ aspects of the Multiple Cultivation Techniques to ‘friendship.’

“Old Lu, cooperate with me for a try,” Meng Jingzhou asked. When it comes to the strongest steel-like bond, it has to be Lu Yang.

“Alright.”

The two circulated their cultivation techniques simultaneously, achieving synchronization. They discovered the method indeed worked. Lu Yang’s Unbeatable Nascent Soul floated out from the top of his head and flew toward Meng Jingzhou’s dantian.

Meng Jingzhou stood up in excitement. “Haha, it really works! Now I have three nascent souls!” Bolstered by three nascent souls, he felt imbued with power from head to toe.

Lu Yang hesitated for a moment before saying, “My nascent soul isn’t very easy to control. It’s rather...irascible. Be careful, Old Meng.”

Meng Jingzhou laughed heartily, not taking it to heart. “What are you talking about? I have two nascent souls inside me. So what if your nascent soul is irascible...”

Suddenly, Meng Jingzhou’s expression shifted dramatically. A sharp pain erupted in his dantian, where a fierce battle was taking place.

Lu Yang’s nascent soul is beating up my nascent souls!

Chapter 637: The Unbeatable Nascent Soul’s Usage Method

Lu Yang’s nascent soul lived up to its “Unbeatable” name. It could fight one against two and still overpower Meng Jingzhou’s two nascent souls! Moreover, the two nascent souls were utterly powerless to fight back—it was a completely one-sided battle!

Caught off guard by this sudden assault, Meng Jingzhou was sent reeling, writhing on the ground in agony. The Unbeatable Nascent Soul was incompatible with Meng Jingzhou, causing his abdomen to swell grotesquely.

“Old Meng, hang in there! I’ll get a doctor! We must save your nascent souls!” Lu Yang yelled with urgency, appearing extremely concerned.

“Old Lu...you bastard...bullying me because my nascent souls can’t fight on their own!” Enduring the acute pain, Meng Jingzhou concentrated his attention on his dantian, preparing for a decisive battle against the nascent soul of that scoundrel Lu Yang.

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul possessed autonomous combat capabilities, while Meng Jingzhou’s twin infants required conscious control, leading to the lopsided situation now.

Alarmed, Lu Yang hastily retracted his nascent soul, after which Meng Jingzhou felt considerably better.

Lu Yang shrugged. “Don’t look at me. It was my nascent soul that hit you, not me. Once my nascent soul enters your body, it’s beyond my control.”

“Get lost!” Meng Jingzhou waved his hand impatiently. I can’t even complain about getting beaten; just seeing this grandson makes me angry.

At the same time, he was secretly astonished. This grandson Lu Yang’s nascent soul is terrifying. Even if I had controlled both my nascent souls to fight just now, I probably would have lost more often than won. It would take three against one to guarantee victory.

However, judging from the attempt to borrow power from Lu Yang’s nascent soul, the method is generally successful. The problem lies with Lu Yang himself.

Lu Yang quietly asked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, “Immortal Fairy, if Old Meng and I join forces to defeat the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, does that count as me defeating it?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shot Lu Yang a sidelong glance. “Why don’t you suggest that you and I join forces to defeat the Unbeatable Nascent Soul?”

Lu Yang, “...”

“Junior Brother Man, you try with Junior Brother Meng,” Yun Zhi directed.

There was another Nascent Soul cultivator present.

Man Gu had wanted to attempt this for a while. He studied the method Yun Zhi had just written and imitated Lu Yang’s posture, sitting cross-legged beside Meng Jingzhou.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Jiang Lianyi observed with keen interest. This was a novel method that hadn’t existed in ancient times.

Meng Jingzhou’s and Man Gu’s auras resonated. The mature-looking nascent soul flew out from the top of Man Gu’s head and darted into Meng Jingzhou’s dantian.

Seeing Man Gu’s nascent soul, Yun Zhi’s eyelid twitched slightly. I’ve never seen such a nascent soul either.

Once again, Meng Jingzhou possessed the power of three nascent souls and felt a significant boost in strength. “Haha, it’s finally a success this time!”

With a thought, he summoned three nascent souls: two resembled Meng Jingzhou, and one looked older than Meng Jingzhou’s father.

“Merge!” Meng Jingzhou shouted, merging with the three nascent souls and transforming into a divine figure with four faces and eight arms, majestic and near-immortal in its sacredness.

This was the limit of nascent soul fusion—there was only so much room on the neck; it couldn’t accommodate a fifth head.

After transforming into the four-faced, eight-armed deity, Meng Jingzhou felt reborn, and his thoughts became vastly different, turning exceedingly sluggish.

“Wait, sluggish?” Fortunately, Meng Jingzhou’s foundation was intact, and he quickly realized something was amiss. It was as if a thin veil had been draped over his mental space, making everything hazy and his thinking very slow.

Evidently, Meng Jingzhou was not present when Man Gu introduced this particular ancestor who had followed an immortal. Man Gu hurriedly explained the ancestor’s traits, after which Meng Jingzhu dissolved the fusion and returned the nascent souls with a dark face.

Is there not a single normal nascent soul available for my experiments?

Then it occurred to him that this was the Dao-Seeking Sect, and he let it go.

Yun Zhi suggested, “Little Junior Brother, Junior Brother Man, you two should also attempt once to see whether you can integrate another’s nascent soul into your own body.” The first two experiments can be considered marginally successful, even though the results were unsatisfactory. Still, they serve to confirm the feasibility of this method.

Now it just depends on how Little Junior Brother and Junior Brother Man Gu will fare.

Unexpectedly, Lu Yang and Man Gu failed one after the other. They could only send their nascent souls into the other’s dantian, but the recipient couldn’t harness the nascent soul’s power. Furthermore, Man Gu’s ancestor got beaten up by the Unbeatable Nascent Soul.

“So it seems that it’s Junior Brother Meng’s unique constitution that produces this effect?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded. “Yang Kongtong and the Meng boy share similarities in their constitutions; perhaps it’s not a coincidence.” One should know that the concept of a Single’s Spirit Root didn’t exist in ancient times; it is a constitution that appeared after the ancient era.

Jiang Lianyi recalled Yang Kongtong’s end and found it somewhat regrettable. “It’s a pity. The Dual Cultivation Body is extremely rare. It only appeared in our era because various constitutions were constantly emerging.

“Yang Kongtong was dismembered by his harem. By then, there was no longer any chance to study his constitution in detail.” If we could have studied it properly, the theoretical field of cultivation might have advanced a small step.

An idea suddenly struck Lu Yang. “By the way, Junior Brother Man, don’t circulate your energy. Let me see if I can send my nascent soul into your dantian.”

“Alright.” Although Man Gu wasn’t entirely sure about Lu Yang’s intention, he always did whatever the latter said.

Lu Yang activated the cultivation technique and released his Unbeatable Nascent Soul, sending it into Man Gu’s dantian.

“It worked!” Lu Yang was overjoyed. As I thought, it’s plausible.

Before the Unbeatable Nascent Soul could unleash its mighty power and beat up Man Gu’s nascent soul, Lu Yang hastily withdrew it. Although I can’t subdue the Unbeatable Nascent Soul for my own use, sending it into an enemy’s body to defeat them from within is a viable strategy!

Even the Everlasting Immortal Fairy praised Lu Yang’s cleverness. Why didn’t I think of this method?

Oh right, no one had analyzed Yang Kongtong’s cultivation technique back then.

Lu Yang gained plenty from this night and was quite fortunate—his nascent soul was the only one among the three that didn’t suffer a beating.

Dawn arrived. As Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu had no other business, they departed one after another.

“Here, I revised the cultivation technique.” Yun Zhi handed Lu Yang a brand-new version of the Clear Heart True Nature Mantra. After Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu left, Lu Yang had free time.

Its presentation and content had undergone a dramatic transformation. Lu Yang could tell the difference in this cultivation manual after flipping through just a couple of pages.

In terms of content, it’s far more structured and clear than what I’d written. In terms of power, it undoubtedly far surpasses my own work. And in terms of authorship, my name is actually listed before Big Senior Sister’s.

Lu Yang was deeply moved. After circulating his energy for just a Microcosmic Loop according to the cultivation technique, he felt it was tailor-made for him, an impeccable fit.

Jiang Lianyi swept her eyes across it briefly and couldn’t help but marvel, admiring her creed leader’s skill. If it were me, I certainly couldn’t have written a cultivation manual that could simplify profound ideas and make them easy to understand.

Lu Yang remembered something and reported his achievement to Yun Zhi, hoping for some acknowledgement and rewards. “By the way, Big Senior Sister, I tested it earlier. I can send the Unbeatable Nascent Soul into the enemy’s body to defeat them from within.”

“Oh, this is indeed a pretty good method. Use it on me; let me see the effect.”

“Alright.” Lu Yang performed the cultivation technique. He released his Unbeatable Nascent Soul and hurled it toward Yun Zhi’s dantian.

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul’s eyes were ice-cold, devoid of emotion, and free from desire. It cast a frigid glance at Yun Zhi, then took to his heels.

Chapter 638: Sword-Cleansing Pond

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul bolted at lightning speed. Lu Yang admitted to himself that if it were him, there was no way he could fly that fast.

Nevertheless, no matter how fast the nascent soul was, it couldn’t escape Yun Zhi’s grasp. With a mere gesture of reaching into the air, Yun Zhi caught the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, which had almost fled beyond the sect’s boundaries, and pulled it back.

Even though it was captured, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul didn’t give up. It exhausted every possible method to break free—Shrinking Earth, Draw Underground Prison, Close Horizon From Cliff, Lu-Style Arhat Fist... If its opponent had been a Nascent Soul cultivator, they would have long been beaten to death.

Unfortunately, its opponent was not a Nascent Soul cultivator, so all these efforts were futile. Be it escaping or attacking, despite the Unbeatable Nascent Soul employing the entirety of its arsenal of methods, it was no match for Yun Zhi. freewebnovel.com

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul brandished its claws and teeth, still dreaming of attacking Yun Zhi, but it was immediately subdued when she flicked its forehead with her finger, leaving it dazed and quiet.

Holding the Unbeatable Nascent Soul by its tiny foot and swinging it gently, Yun Zhi wore a pensive expression. “This level of offensive power is quite remarkable. It’s a decent offensive method.”

She tossed the Unbeatable Nascent Soul back to Lu Yang. “However, this is not the proper path. You still need to hone your skills and strive to defeat your own nascent soul.”

“Yes.”

Having learned the cultivation technique for this phase, Lu Yang settled down to prepare for cultivating the sword array.

The Seven Star Sword Set obtained from the Creation Ancient Domain had been lying around in his identity jade tablet. He had only taken out one sword when acting as Young Creed Leader Lu at the heavenly altar. However, this was not Lu Yang’s original intention. His plan had been to form a sword array with the complete Seven Star Sword Set.

Sword cultivators generally followed two cultivation paths: one was ‘One Sword Breaks All Spells,’ focusing wholeheartedly on tempering a single sword to achieve ‘Person and Sword as One’; the other was sword arrays, which could enable swords to unleash power beyond their original capabilities—a truly wondrous route.

Unfortunately, Lu Yang’s shifu had died early, and neither Yun Zhi nor Jiang Lianyi was adept at sword arrays, so he had no one to guide him.

If Jiang Lianyi had understood swords, she wouldn’t have been deceived by the sword array the Qilin Immortal knelt on.

However, there was good news. After being intimidated by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, the unyielding Seven Star Swords now obediently submitted to Lu Yang, not daring to show the slightest resistance, saving him the time needed to refine and tame them.

“Little Junior Brother, if you wish to practice swordsmanship, you may try the Sword-Cleansing Pond. Once you’ve gained something from it, I have a sword array here that you can cultivate.” Yun Zhi recalled some spoils of war she had acquired, which would be perfect for Lu Yang.

“Sword-Cleansing Pond?” Lu Yang didn’t know there was such a place within the sect.

“That was where Shifu practiced his sword in his early years. After Shifu achieved major success in the Sword Dao and no longer needed to cleanse his sword, the place was forsaken.”

Many among the Dao-Seeking Sect disciples used swords as weapons, but only Lu Yang could truly be called a sword cultivator. The Sword Spirit Root was rare. Lu Yang was the second cultivator after the Taciturn Daoist Priest to possess one in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“After descending the mountain, head east for about eight hundred li. That is where the Sword-Cleansing Pond is located.” Yun Zhi pointed out the direction for Lu Yang. “Currently, your control over the Seven Star Sword Set is passive; you haven’t established a connection with them. The Sword-Cleansing Pond can enhance the communication between you and them, allowing you to control them fully. This is the foundation for cultivating sword arrays.

“The Sword-Cleansing Pond can wash away the baleful energy from both the cultivator and the swords, improving their integration and coordination. Not only Shifu, but also Grand-Shifu used to cultivate there frequently.”

“Ah? Is Grand-Shifu a sword cultivator too?” Lu Yang thought of the little fellow guarding Incarceration Peak and found it hard to associate him with sword cultivators.

“No. He went there to wash away his baleful energy toward Shifu, lest he doesn’t hold back and accidentally beat Shifu to death.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Sometimes, Lu Yang felt it was a miracle his shifu had survived this long.

Jiang Lianyi was not interested in the Sword-Cleansing Pond and instead voiced her desire to visit Incarceration Peak. Yun Zhi gladly agreed, offering to take her there.

~~~

Following Yun Zhi’s directions, Lu Yang descended the mountain, passed through the core area of the Dao-Seeking Sect, and arrived at the vast grassland on the periphery.

These grasslands used to be extremely dangerous for Lu Yang. They were home to various demon beasts, and the breeding farm established by the Everlasting Creed Leader and the Everlasting Immortal was situated right at the edge of this grassland.

Now, Lu Yang was a far cry from his former self. These terrifying demon beasts are not worth mentioning. As long as I want to run, they can’t even catch up to me!

On the grassland, Lu Yang flew on his sword and sped along, hovering just over three feet above the ground. Behind him was a horde of demon beasts emitting Nascent Soul auras, occasionally interspersed with a few Divine Transfiguration demon beasts. They howled and caused the earth to tremble, creating a terrifying sight.

“What’s there to fear about Divine Transfiguration demon beasts? There are also Void Refinement and Fusion demon beasts here,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy kindly reminded him. Lu Yang, you’re getting scared too early. “That said, you don’t need to be too afraid. Those Void Refinement and Fusion demon beasts can’t be bothered to chase you. These demon beasts are likely tamed. They mainly attack disciples who make them feel threatened.” As for whether this is for training purposes or mere mischief, I wouldn’t know.

Finally, at the critical moment, Lu Yang successfully flew out of the grassland’s boundaries. The demon beasts’ pursuit ceased abruptly, and they did not advance a step further.

“Little Junior Brother, are you practicing flying?” To his surprise, Gan Tian was right at the edge of the grassland. Although she was still blindfolded, she could perceive the life-and-death chase scene her little junior brother had just been through by sensing others’ auras and the wind sounds.

“Third Senior Sister, don’t those demon beasts chase you when you pass through the grassland?”

“You didn’t know? As long as you display your identity jade tablet, those demon beasts won’t attack you. Didn’t Big Senior Sister tell you?” Gan Tian waved her own identity jade tablet.

“No.”

“Then she probably thought those demon beasts wouldn’t pose a threat to you.”

“Senior Sister, what are you doing here?” Lu Yang asked.

Gan Tian pointed toward a dark mountain range further away. “That’s Tangting Mountain. I was missing a material for refining a magical treasure, so I went there to dig some up. I was just about to head back. And you? Are you here to participate in the cave domain trial?”

“I’m going to the Sword-Cleansing Pond.”

“Sword-Cleansing Pond... Oh right, you’re a sword cultivator. That place is perfect for you. Do you know the way? Do you want me to take you there?”

“Many thanks, Senior Sister.” Big Senior Sister had only given a general direction; having someone guide me there would be best.

“We’re fellow senior sister and junior brother. There’s no need for thanks.”

With Gan Tian leading the way, Lu Yang soon arrived at the Sword-Cleansing Pond.

The Sword-Cleansing Pond lay in a small valley, nestled between two millennia-old ancient trees. Leaves from these trees floated quietly on the pond’s surface, the scene appearing almost frozen in time. No cultivator had visited the Sword-Cleansing Pond for two hundred years. Now, a trace of life had finally returned to this place.

“This is the Sword-Cleansing Pond.”

Lu Yang scooped the leaves out of the pond, revealing the clear, bottomless water. The water possessed a magical quality, where simply looking at it seemed to cleanse the spirit.

“Good place!” Lu Yang’s eyes shone. Just by looking at the pond, I can imagine how Shifu had cultivated here over a hundred years ago.

“According to Shifu, to use the Sword-Cleansing Pond, one needs to place the sword in the water, washing away the ostentation and adornment to reveal the true, original essence.

Lu Yang took out the Seven Star Sword Set. Once the seven divine swords appeared, they clung affectionately to Lu Yang, startling him into quickly pressing them all down into the pond.

As the swords soaked in the pond, they were indeed no longer restless. Lu Yang could even sense the feelings they transmitted to him—comfort and coolness. If things continued like this, Lu Yang was confident he could truly master the Seven Star Sword Set at the Sword-Cleansing Pond.

He sat cross-legged beside the pond in a proper posture and calmed his mind, attempting to communicate and interact with the swords, empathizing with them.

Three days passed in a flash. Lu Yang sat motionless the entire time, with Gan Tian guarding his cultivation.

She observed the changes in Lu Yang and was secretly amazed by his talent in Sword Dao. She felt as though Lu Yang had disappeared. This is the state of maintaining communication with the swords, entering the realm of Person and Sword as One. To think he has achieved so much in just three days!

Lu Yang had entered an indescribable, profound, and wondrous state. Throughout these three days, he had engaged in a vague and specious communication with the Seven Star Sword Set, effectively enhancing his connection with them.

He slowly opened his eyes, his gaze calm and unperturbed like an ancient well.

Success! I’ve completely grasped the Seven Star Sword Set!

Lu Yang raised his right hand and curled two fingers upward. The Sword-Cleansing Pond followed his will and danced in the air, splashing water and scattering the Seven Star Sword Set across the ground.

“Hmm?”

Didn’t I grasp the Seven Star Sword Set? How did it become the Sword-Cleansing Pond?

Chapter 639: Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array

“Oh no, I grasped the wrong thing.” Lu Yang finally figured out the reason. During these three days, I wasn’t communicating with the Seven Star Sword Set but with the Sword-Cleansing Pond!

“Little Junior Brother, you...” As Gan Tian was blindfolded, she perceived the external commotion through her other senses and took a moment to process what her Little Junior Brother had done.

He has made off with the Sword-Cleansing Pond!

“Wait, this is an accident! I can explain!” Lu Yang hastily shouted while secretly trying to sever the connection with the pond.

But the bond he had formed with the Sword-Cleansing Pond over three days couldn’t be broken so easily. After several unsuccessful attempts, he had no choice but to admit one thing—the Sword-Cleansing Pond had latched onto him.

Brother, is this really necessary? Can’t you follow someone else? I’m insignificant and weak; I don’t dare to keep you. Boldly appropriating sect property is unjustifiable no matter how you look at it.

Gan Tian wore an expression that said no further explanation was needed. “Little Junior Brother, Big Senior Sister has long mentioned you had extraordinary talent, just that it’s a bit unorthodox. Seeing it today confirms that.” I didn’t get the chance to witness it in the Demon Region, but now I finally have.

Lu Yang, “...”

Big Senior Sister, can’t you say something nice about me for once?

“An accident simply happened during the communication process—I didn’t cultivate it off-kilter,” Lu Yang clarified earnestly, correcting Gan Tian’s mistaken view.

“Immortal Fairy, why didn’t you remind me that I was communicating with the Sword-Cleansing Pond all this time?” Third Senior Sister might not have noticed something amiss, but how could you not have?

“Ah? I thought you planned to control the Sword-Cleansing Pond first, and then borrow its power to control the Seven Star Sword Set.”

“...That does seem like it could work.”

Following the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s line of thinking, Lu Yang realized it was indeed possible to control the Seven Star Sword Set by first controlling the Sword-Cleansing Pond.

The comfort the Seven Star Sword Set felt in the pond couldn’t have been fake. Since they have experienced it once, they would surely want it a second time.

And if they want to experience it a second time, they will have to behave and listen to me!

“Never mind. Let’s just inform Big Senior Sister.” Now that things have come to this, I can’t just forcibly separate myself from the Sword-Cleansing Pond.

Lu Yang collected the spilled water back into the Sword-Cleansing Pond, then stored both the Sword-Cleansing Pond and the Seven Star Sword Set into his identity jade token with movements so practiced they resembled cleaning up a crime scene.

The two returned the way they came. When they passed through the vast grassland, Lu Yang whipped out his identity jade tablet, and sure enough, the demon beasts no longer attacked.

~~~

Meanwhile, Yun Zhi and Jiang Lianyi had finished their tour of Incarceration Peak. The archaic cultivators imprisoned there were trembling with fear.

What is the background of the Dao-Seeking Sect? How did they manage to unearth the Phoenix Ancestor, who has been missing for several hundred thousand years?

If they had previously looked down on the Dao-Seeking Sect due to their own archaic status, even that last shred of pride was now gone.

In terms of antiquity, who could surpass the Phoenix Ancestor? Even if the Four Ancient Immortals were here, they were from the same era as the Phoenix Ancestor, so there’d be no distinction in seniority.

As for the Grand-Shifu, his reaction was no better than Old Tao’s, especially when he heard from Yun Zhi that the Phoenix Ancestor was unearthed by Lu Yang, his expression becoming much more spectacular.

The student surpasses the master—this kid Lu Yang is far more capable than his shifu in stirring things up.

The Grand-Shifu was thankful he had retired. If I were still in the position of sect leader, I wouldn’t be able to handle the mess Lu Yang is causing.

~~~

“You’re saying you refined the sect’s Sword-Cleansing Pond?” Yun Zhi was momentarily stunned by Lu Yang’s report.

If I remember correctly, I told you to go to the Sword-Cleansing Pond to refine the Seven Star Sword Set, not to refine the pond itself.

“It was an accident,” Lu Yang repeatedly stressed that there were extenuating circumstances.

However, even if there were mitigating circumstances, Lu Yang still didn’t hold the high ground. Appropriating sect property still warranted some form of punishment.

“Creed Leader, I remember you promised me that I could take anything from this sect?” Jiang Lianyi stepped forward to extricate her senior brother from trouble. “In that case, can I take the Sword-Cleansing Pond?”

“Of course, you can.”

Just like that, the rationale of this matter was settled.

Yun Zhi’s original intention had been to find a legitimate reason to justify giving the Sword-Cleansing Pond to Lu Yang. The Sword-Cleansing Pond was dispensable to the Dao-Seeking Sect. In two thousand years, they had only produced two sword cultivators, and the number of times the pond had been used was pitifully small. However, she couldn’t give it to Lu Yang directly, for that would be disregarding sect rules and regulations, which wouldn’t be conducive to sect unity.

“Very well. Since you’ve already acquired the Sword-Cleansing Pond, you should be able to grasp the Seven Star Sword Set within a few days, achieving the foundation for practicing sword arrays.” Yun Zhi took out a small booklet from the front of her robe. “This is a spoil of war I obtained after encountering an enemy. It happens to contain a sword array manual. This is the first layer; take it and study it for now.”

Lu Yang accepted the booklet. Upon seeing the name of the sword array, his hand trembled, nearly dropping it.

Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array.

“Can this sword array truly exterminate immortals?” Lu Yang’s voice quivered as he asked the question.

I’m asking the obvious. If it can’t exterminate immortals, why would it have such a name?

“It can’t. It was probably just given an impressive name to boost one’s courage.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Which lunatic came up with this name?

“I don’t know who he was either.” Yun Zhi recalled the incident. “I ran into him by chance. He was secretly plotting a major scheme, and if it had been successful, it would have turned Great Xia upside down. The situation was urgent then, and there was no time to seek help. I was forced to act, and then I got rid of him.

“He was undoubtedly an archaic cultivator, but I can’t be certain whether he’s from Great Yu or Great Qian. This sword array and your Qingfeng Sword belonged to that person.

“I’ve tested the sword array’s power. It can’t exterminate immortals, but its power is still impressive. What you have is the first layer. I’ll give you the subsequent ones once your cultivation realm rises.”

Lu Yang asked, “Was he a sword cultivator?”

“No, he just knew how to use a sword. It felt like he knew a bit about talismans, spells, and the like, but wasn’t very proficient. He could bully half-immortals with his cultivation realm, but he would struggle against someone of the same level.”

“...Wait a moment, he was an immortal?!”

Yun Zhi didn’t understand why Lu Yang’s reaction was so dramatic. “Of course, he was an immortal. A half-immortal wouldn’t dare to give their sword array a name like this. He could be considered the weakest immortal I’ve encountered, even weaker than the one we met at the Everlasting Creed.”

Big Senior Sister, you spoke of it so lightly, saying he was the ‘weakest immortal,’ but even the weakest immortal is still an immortal! Yet you killed him just like that!

Even Jiang Lianyi couldn’t keep her cool, much less Lu Yang.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy remembered the aura of the Dao Fruit she had sensed deep within the Dao-Seeking Sect’s treasury. It likely belonged to this person. “Tch, it’s just killing an immortal. You make it sound as if no one else can do it. It’s just because I haven’t had the opportunity; otherwise, I could do it too.”

Just as Lu Yang was about to thank Yun Zhi and start building rapport with the Seven Star Sword Set to begin cultivating the sword array and become a qualified sword cultivator, he sensed movement from the Nine-Netherworlds Token—someone from the Nine-Netherworlds Creed was contacting him.

After reading the message on the token, a strange expression appeared on his face.

“What is it? Did the Nine-Netherworlds Creed contact you?” Yun Zhi asked.

“The Nine-Netherworlds Creed informed me that the creed leader of the Radiant Sun Creed wants to meet me.”

Chapter 640: The Heavenly Court Creed’s Sincerity

At the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s headquarters, a massive map of Great Xia occupied the entire main wall. All seventeen provinces and tens of thousands of cities of Great Xia were displayed on the map in detail. One-fifth of the cities were marked with red dots, signifying that the Nine-Netherworlds Creed had extended its influence to these cities. Even the largest city, the imperial capital, had been penetrated by the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

Mu Baiyi stood with his hands clasped behind his back, gazing quietly at the map. He mumbled to himself, his eyes overflowing with unconcealable greed and desire.

“Soon, very soon...

“The imperial court is nothing special. They hadn’t even detected such a large-scale operation from our creed...

“Soon, this Great Xia will be filled with our Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s barbeque shops...”

Mu Baiyi couldn’t resist touching one of the red dots on the map. Each dot represented a barbeque shop, symbolizing the vast amounts of money that would soon flow into the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, helping him repay his loans.

Although we’re still in the investment and store-opening phase, with profits being thin due to reinvestment to open more shops, the prospects are promising. With this fortune, I’ll no longer have to worry about anyone uncovering my scheme of taking out loans using my followers’ identities to distribute monthly payments.

This is lifesaving money.

“It’s all thanks to the Heavenly Court Creed.” Having witnessed the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor defeat Supreme Lord Zhu Tian, Mu Baiyi’s reverence and awe toward the Heavenly Court Creed further increased. “According to Young Creed Leader Lu, several key figures from the ancient Heavenly Court have yet to awaken. Even so, this Heavenly Court Creed is far beyond what our Nine-Netherworlds Creed can compare to.”

“Creed Leader, Creed Leader Chi of the Radiant Sun Creed wishes to meet with you,” Vice Creed Leader Xiang reported, presenting the Radiant Sun Creed’s visiting card.[1]

Mu Baiyi raised an eyebrow, somewhat puzzled. The Nine-Netherworlds Creed believed in reincarnation, and its cultivation techniques generally leaned toward a yin attribute. As the Radiant Sun Creed’s name suggested, their cultivation techniques were of a yang attribute. The two creeds hardly interacted with each other.

“What does he want?”

A meeting was inevitable. As they were from fellow diabolic creeds, a certain level of courtesy had to be maintained.

~~~

Since the location of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed headquarters couldn’t be revealed, the two creed leaders met at a teahouse one day later, with the Radiant Sun Creed paying to reserve an entire floor. freewebnovel.com

Creed Leader Shi arrived on time, accompanied by two protectors.

Creed Leader Shi was a man who appeared to be in his thirties or forties. His face was fleshy and fierce-looking. He was bald and only had one eye. A frightening scar ran from his forehead down to his cheek under his right eye, making him look quite intimidating.

“Hahaha, Fellow Daoist Mu, it’s been a long time since we last met!” Creed Leader Shi greeted, his attitude as amicable as though Mu Baiyi was his biological brother.

“If you have business, state it. If there’s none, goodbye to you,” Mu Baiyi replied coldly, unwilling to engage with Creed Leader Chi more than was necessary. He found the other party’s enthusiasm overwhelming.

“Aiya, come now, with the relationship between us, would I seek you out for no reason?” Creed Leader Shi sat down, chuckling as he rubbed his bald head.

“What is it?”

“I’ve noticed that your Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s barbeque shops are pretty popular lately. I’ve even tried them, and they indeed offer great value. Eating spirit food of this quality at such a price—no wonder the business is so good.”

“What do you want?” Mu Baiyi stared at Creed Leader Shi warily. Anyone who has designs on my money will have to fight me with their life on the line.

“Don’t be nervous. We’re not here to snatch your business. I heard that the One More Time Barbeque shops don’t just belong to your Nine-Netherworlds Creed but also people from the Heavenly Court Creed?”

Mu Baiyi’s expression tightened. “You planted a spy in our creed?” The matter of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s collaboration with the Heavenly Court Creed is privy only to the creed’s higher-ups.

“The feeling is mutual.” Creed Leader Chi also knew there were Nine-Netherworlds Creed members in his own creed, though he didn’t know their specific identities.

Creed Leader Chi looked at Mu Baiyi fervently and rubbed his hands together. “So, I was thinking, since your Nine-Netherworlds Creed has such a close relationship with the Heavenly Court Creed, you must have a way to contact them. I was wondering if you could help us get in touch. I’d like to meet the Heavenly Court Creed and get to know them.”

He had personally gone to the Demon City and witnessed the scene of the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor presiding over the Demon Kingdom like a monarch. Along with previous events like Dou Heavenly Sovereign defeating a Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivator and Young Creed Leader Lu wreaking havoc in the Dao-Seeking Sect, all these deeds indicated that the Heavenly Court Creed’s power was profound and unfathomable.

Although their Radiant Sun Creed was strong, they weren’t arrogant enough to oppose the Heavenly Court Creed. That would be akin to an egg striking a rock. Perhaps the Radiant Sun Creed might need to rely on the Heavenly Court Creed in the future, so forging friendly relationships early and getting acquainted wouldn’t hurt.

Mu Baiyi’s initial inclination was to refuse the Radiant Sun Creed a meeting with the Heavenly Court Creed, worried that the benefits that could have fallen to the Nine-Netherworlds Creed would end up with the Radiant Sun Creed instead. Didn’t Young Creed Leader Lu get the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s economy moving just by casually setting up a barbeque shop?

However, one of the strategies Young Creed Leader Lu proposed was “establish connections internally with the Heartless and Radiant Sun creeds.” If he finds out that I had refused the Radiant Sun Creed’s request to establish contact, the consequences for us would be unpleasant.

“Helping you contact the Heavenly Court Creed is possible. However, we are not a charity. May I ask what price your esteemed creed intends to pay?”

Creed Leader Chi had anticipated this. He gave a glance to one of the protectors behind him, who whipped out a yellow piece of paper from his robe and placed it before Mu Baiyi. “I’ve heard your barbeque shops offer delivery service. But because it involves cross-city delivery, the barbeque skewers turn cold over time, causing the taste and texture to suffer.

“This is a paper unique to our creed. It has heating and insulation properties. Moreover, it’s easy to produce at a low cost. Fellow Daoist Mu, if you’re interested, I can provide you with the method to create such a paper.”

This paper was chicken ribs and of little use to the Radiant Sun Creed. Keeping it was pointless, and discarding it was a waste. They might as well use it as a stepping stone to express goodwill to the Nine-Netherworlds Creed and befriend them.

Mu Baiyi’s and Vice Creed Leader Shi’s eyes lit up. This is truly good stuff! It can significantly increase the delivery orders!

“Alright, I’ll contact them for you right away.” Seeing the other party’s immense sincerity, Mu Baiyi immediately took out his Nine-Netherworlds Token. “But let me state clearly in advance—I can only contact Young Creed Leader Lu; I don’t have any way to contact anyone else in the Heavenly Court Creed.”

“Young Creed Leader Lu is fine,” Creed Leader Shi hurriedly said. In terms of status, Young Creed Leader Lu is fully qualified to be on par with the creed leader of a diabolic creed.

Mu Baiyi wrote Creed Leader Shi’s desire for a meeting on the Nine-Netherworlds Token. Soon, a response came from the other side.

“What does it say?”

“The usual place. Yanjiang Commandery. Meet at the headquarters of One More Time Barbeque Shop.”

Hearing this, Creed Leader Chi was overjoyed and immediately imparted to Mu Baiyi the refinement method for the heating paper. Mu Baiyi mentally reviewed it and confirmed it was genuine. Besides, the Radiant Sun Creed wouldn’t dare to deceive me about this.

“Fellow Daoist Mu, I’ll have to trouble you to put in a good word for me with Young Creed Leader Lu!”

“No problem, that’s easy!”

~~~

In Yanjiang Commandery, at the headquarters of One More Time Barbeque Shop, the three parties met.

Mu Baiyi and Creed Leader Chi sat upright and still, not daring to breathe heavily, their backs drenched in sweat from nervousness.

“Fellow Daoist Mu, didn’t you say you’d put in a good word for me? Say something!” Creed Leader Chi transmitted an auditory message to Mu Baiyi.

Mu Baiyi was sweating profusely, having lost his previous composure.

Sitting across from them were the Great Emperor of Southern Extreme Nirvana, Jiang Lianyi, and the Heavenly Court Creed Leader, Yun Zhi.

Upon learning that it was a meeting between figures at the level of a creed leader, Lu Yang wished to show respect to the Nine-Netherworlds Creed and the Radiant Sun Creed and demonstrate the Heavenly Court Creed’s sincerity, so he specially invited his own creed leader.

1. In the past, the aristocrats didn’t visit other aristocrats as they pleased. To visit someone, one had to send a baitie or a visiting card/greeting card to express one’s desire to visit a particular person in the household. It would contain information such as one’s name and reason for visit. This card was typically handed to servants to pass on to the servants of the receiving household, which could allow room for manipulation. This is the reason you might have seen people using this for their schemes in Chinese dramas. ☜

Chapter 641: The Heavenly Court Creed’s Holy Son

The One More Time Barbeque Shop headquarters was closed for the night. Unbeknownst to everyone else, beneath the calm exterior of the shop were surging undercurrents.

Tonight, the leaders of three creeds were meeting here.

The Nine-Netherworlds Creed and the Radiant Sun Creed treated the meeting with the Heavenly Court Creed with utmost importance. The leaders of both creeds had come in person to receive them, followed by several Fusion experts, fully displaying the diabolic creeds’ profound foundations.

The Heavenly Court Creed also regarded the two creeds with utmost importance. Their Creed Leader and the Great Emperor of Southern Extreme Nirvana were both present and seated, while four Heavenly King protectors stood behind them. On such an occasion, even Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had to stand in the back row. If the Everlasting Immortal Fairy residing within Lu Yang could be counted, it could also be said that Dou Heavenly Sovereign was present.

Mu Baiyi and Creed Leader Chi were extremely nervous. Who would have thought that all the major figures of the Heavenly Court Creed would come to a simple meeting? What use is there in us bringing so many people? Even if we combine them all, they’re still no match for the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor alone.

The scene of the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor battling the ancient Dijiang had been captured by recording orbs and spread like wildfire among the upper echelons of the cultivation world. Anyone who saw it broke out in a cold sweat and felt ashamed about their inferiority. It was all the more so for the seated Heavenly Court Creed Leader, who had only been mentioned in conversations, yet had never been seen before.

The strength of this Heavenly Court Creed Leader is a mystery. According to Young Creed Leader Lu, the Heavenly Court Creed Leader had fought to a draw with Yun Zhi, who is suspected to be at the Advanced Transcendent Tribulation Stage. This means she’s also at the Advanced Transcendent Tribulation Stage!

“H-hello, on behalf of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, I welcome the esteemed members of the Heavenly Court Creed.” Mu Baiyi forced himself to keep his composure as he stammered with his opening remarks. After all, this is the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s territory; I have to play host.

He continued, “I’m not sure if Young Creed Leader Lu has introduced me to you both. My name is Mu Baiyi, and I am the creed leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

“This is Chi Dongfang, the Radiant Sun Creed Leader.”

“H-hello.” Creed Leader Chi was also overwhelmed by the two’s presence, his eyelids twitching as he tried to calm himself.

“I’m Jiang Lianyi. You both should have seen me before,” Jiang Lianyi said lazily in greeting.

“Greetings, Senior Jiang,” the two creed leaders chorused in unison.

“I’m Yun Mengmeng. You may address me as Creed Leader Yun.”

“Greetings, Creed Leader Yun.” freewebnovel.com

Yun Zhi’s disguise technique was far superior to the Dao-Seeking Nine’s; no one could see through it. Chapter 644: Li Haoran’s Nascent Soul

Initially, Mu Baiyi didn’t care about who the reincarnation of Qin Haoran was. After all, given Qin Haoran’s impoverished state, how could there be any money left in his inheritance? Anything valuable would have been sold off long ago; how could it remain until now?

However, he couldn’t simply tell the three vice creed leaders about this. If they learn that the Nine-Netherworlds Creed has no money, it would be a disaster.

But things are different now. The Heavenly Court Creed’s power is evident. Qin Yanyan must be the reincarnation, regardless of whether she is or not!

Gender isn’t an issue. Besides, no one stipulated that reincarnation must preserve the same gender.

If they can truly find the reincarnation of Creed Leader Qin, that would be perfect! It will be the first confirmed case proving that reincarnation does exist!

There’s no better news than this for the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. Haven’t we worked hard to build the Fengdu Ghost City for this exact purpose?

Creed Leader Yun’s presence is too overpowering. Even sitting opposite her made my legs feel weak, much less the protectors standing behind me.
