Did Junior Brother Li finally succumb to the pain of being a kept man and commit suicide out of depression?

“That said, recovering the head consumes too much energy, so I decided on this.”

The limbs and torso formed a new whole and performed various skills, while Li Haoran’s head stayed at a distance, wearing a smug expression.

“This way, my head won’t get injured.”

Chapter 645: Experiences From Six Lifetimes

“If I want to increase the intimidation factor, I can also do this!”

The Fire Infant demonstrated its mighty power once more. Li Haoran’s torso and head were shrouded in a layer of flames. If he suddenly appeared like this at night, he could frighten a crowd to tears.

Lu Yang seriously contemplated the uses of Li Haoran’s nascent soul. “If the body is completely disassembled, there will be six body parts attacking. If they are manipulated skillfully, the enemy will face assaults from six directions, making it hard to defend against. If only the head flies out, and the remaining body forms a headless corpse to attack, it would be highly effective for life preservation.”

“Senior Brother Lu, this is not my only life-preserving method!” Li Haoran laughed heartily upon hearing Lu Yang’s analysis.

“Merge!”

His head reattached to his neck seamlessly, without the slightest flaw. No one could tell that he had been a headless corpse just a second ago.

“Come, Senior Brother Lu, attack me!”

Lu Yang didn’t stand on ceremony. Bringing two fingers together, he shot a formless sword qi at Li Haoran.

Li Haoran’s body swayed slightly, and his right arm detached, causing the formless qi to pass between his torso and the detached arm.

“How’s that?” Li Haoran reattached his right arm and spun around, his body unharmed and intact.

“Interesting. What about this?” Lu Yang didn’t give Li Haoran time to react, slashing out over a dozen sword qi in succession. This was a rain of sword qi that Li Haoran couldn’t dodge by dismembering himself!

Li Haoran’s expression shifted. Given my reaction speed, it’s true that I can’t dodge so many sword qi.

Then, a smile appeared at the corner of his mouth.

But it’s not like there’s no other way.

He removed his head and held it by the hair. Swinging his arm in a wide arc, he hurled his head far away with a whoosh.

Li Haoran’s body withstood the brunt of all the sword qi head-on, while his head transformed into a streak of light and fled into the distance. If the sword qi strikes had been fatal, he could have saved his life using this method.

Lu Yang couldn’t help but applaud. This Red Kid Nascent Soul is indeed useful, with various applications based on one’s imagination.

Before long, Li Haoran’s head flew back and reconnected with his body, restoring him to his original state.

“Hiss, Senior Brother Lu, you were quite ruthless.” Once his body fused back, Li Haoran felt the pain from the sword qi wounds.

Meng Jingzhou looked at Li Haoran’s Fire Infant, lost in thought. My nascent soul can transform into three heads and six arms, while Junior Brother Li’s nascent soul is about making his own three heads and six arms fly around?

Unlike Li Haoran, who used spells as his primary attack method, Meng Jingzhou was a physique cultivator with high demands on the coherence of the body. Dismembering my body to crash into enemies will be far less powerful than assuming a fist technique stance and throwing a couple of punches...

“Wait, it might actually work...” Meng Jingzhou suddenly had an idea and moved closer to Li Haoran. “Junior Brother Li, let’s discuss something. Your senior brother has some insights about Nascent Soul cultivation and needs your cooperation.”

“What insights?”

“My physique is a bit special; I can borrow others’ nascent souls. Take this cultivation manual and learn this technique. It will allow you to lend me your nascent soul.”

Li Haoran’s expression turned peculiar. This was his first time hearing that nascent souls could be borrowed.

Could it be that the Meng Family doesn’t only lend money but also nascent souls?”

“I’ll learn it.”

Li Haoran quickly mastered the cultivation technique Meng Jingzhou handed him; it was just a single thin sheet of paper and very simple. His learning speed was even faster than Man Gu’s.

The two sat cross-legged and triggered resonance. The Fire Infant flew out from Li Haoran’s body and entered Meng Jingzhou’s dantian.

Meng Jingzhou felt the power of the Fire Infant. This is the power of the Three Nascent Souls Stage—truly extraordinary.

Shouting loudly, he performed nascent soul fusion and once again transformed into the adept with four heads and eight arms. Next, he cut off four arms and had the other four arms hold them, thus becoming an adept with four heads, four arms, and four weapons!

With a heave-ho, Meng Jingzhou swung the severed arms effortlessly, whipping up gusts of wind. These are excellent weapons, perfectly suited for me!

“Success!”

Li Haoran’s eyelid twitched. Senior Brother Meng doesn’t seem like a righteous cultivator; he’s more like a diabolic path leader.

After remaining quiet all this time, Yun Zhi finally spoke. Her voice wasn’t loud, but it held the power to silence the entire place. “Junior Brother Li, we just returned from meeting with the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, where we heard about their origins. Do you have any memories related to this?”

Hearing that serious business was about to be discussed, Meng Jingzhou hurriedly returned the nascent soul to Li Haoran.

Lu Yang was momentarily stunned to hear it involved the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s origins. He nodded earnestly. “I actually do have memories, but they’re not complete. Qin Haoran told Senior Yiren that he was the eighth reincarnation and that I am the ninth. He could confirm he was the eighth incarnation because of the memories he had of the previous seven lifetimes. But I haven’t fully inherited Qin Haoran’s memories yet. The memories of the earlier lifetimes are fragmented.”

“Feel free to speak.”

Li Haoran nodded and began sifting through the vast ocean of Qin Haoran’s memories for relevant information.

Qin Haoran possessed nearly two thousand years of memories. Such a massive amount was more than Li Haoran could handle. To avoid losing himself in the sea of memories, Li Haoran had asked his shifu to seal the memories, only removing portions of the seal as needed.

“My memories of the first three lifetimes are quite blurry. I can’t recall what happened.

“Eighty thousand years ago, in the fourth lifetime, the ‘me’ then awakened by chance, gaining a part of my memories from past lifetimes. From these memories, ‘I’ acquired knowledge about cultivation and embarked on the path of cultivation.

“As ‘my’ cultivation increased, other parts of the first three lifetimes’ memories surfaced, such as the ‘Nine Netherworlds’ and ‘reincarnation.’ Mu Baiyi has probably told you about this.

“Relying on the fragmented past life memories, my fourth incarnation established the Nine-Netherworlds Creed to explore the true meaning of reincarnation.

“Of course, there were hardly any gains. The hideout was even raided by two constables. He was upright and loyal to his friends, letting his subordinates escape first while he covered the rear. As a result, he didn’t manage to reincarnate and was captured, sentenced to life imprisonment.

“My fifth incarnation reincarnated in the Buddhist Kingdom, saw through the mundane world and renounced secular life, becoming a nun. Later, she fell in love with the abbot of a neighboring temple. They both returned to secular life and married under the witness of Buddha. freewebnovel.com

“My sixth incarnation joined the Nine-Netherworlds Creed and used his past life memories to ascend to the position of creed leader. He embezzled creed funds for personal use and delayed payments month after month until he was assassinated.

“My seventh incarnation was female. She became a palace maid, spending her days in elaborate schemes and intrigue within the imperial harem.” Li Haoran’s expression turned somewhat uncomfortable as he recalled some unpleasant events.

“As for my eighth incarnation, all of you know him. It’s that scoundrel Qin Haoran who deserves a thousand cuts. He also had the highest cultivation. He tried to undergo a lightning tribulation to advance to the Transcendent Tribulation and evade his creditors, but was struck dead by lightning.

“And the ninth incarnation is me.”

Several tumultuous and magnificent lives indeed.

After listening to the full account, Yun Zhi asked calmly, “The fourth incarnation was born eighty thousand years ago, while the eighth incarnation, Qin Haoran, immediately reincarnated and became you after his death. That is to say that the fourth incarnation didn’t immediately reincarnate into the fifth incarnation after death—there was a time gap, right?”

Li Haoran. “Yes. The closer to the present, the shorter the interval between the lifetimes. By my lifetime, there is no longer a time gap.”

Yun Zhi verified, “According to this temporal rule, your first three incarnations were not from Great Xia but from Great Yu or even Great Qian, right?”

“You could say that.”

Yun Zhi continued, “The interval between reincarnations has been growing shorter and shorter until now, where there is no more time gap. It could be a form of countdown or an accumulation method. Your current lifetime might be the last one, or something might happen after you die and enter your tenth lifetime.”

“Indeed.”

Yun Zhi mulled over it, then turned to Jiang Lianyi. “I have no further questions. Senior, do you have any?”

Jiang Lianyi nodded. “Can you elaborate on the experiences of the elaborate schemes and intrigue in the imperial harem?”

“...No.”

“Then I also have no further questions.”

Chapter 646: The Origin of the Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array

“What are you thinking about?” Lu Yang asked upon seeing Meng Jingzhou squatting on the ground in deep contemplation, as if he was pondering some recondite question.

Meng Jingzhou craned his neck to look up at Lu Yang. “I’m thinking about which imperial consort Junior Brother Li was in his sixth lifetime. Did she later become the empress? If she became the empress, she would be the ancestor of the current emperor.”

Lu Yang, “...”

The Xia Emperor’s lifespan is almost exhausted, and you’re finding him an ancestor, huh?

“Junior Brother Li, you have just broken through and need to consolidate your cultivation. We shall not disturb you further.” freewebnovel.com

Li Haoran had already shared all he knew, and Yun Zhi had also obtained the answers she wanted. There was no need for them to linger and delay Li Haoran’s cultivation any longer.

~~~

Three days later, at Heaven’s Gate Peak, Lu Yang sat on the sword stone in the lotus position. Beside him was a naturally formed stone pool—the Sword-Cleansing Pond that had latched onto him.

Inside the pond, seven swords swam about like seven lively and cheerful fish.

Sensing the increasingly clear connection with the Seven Star Sword Set, Lu Yang opened his eyes instantly. As he raised two fingers, the seven swords leaped out of the pond, gleaming under the sunlight, readily accepting Lu Yang’s control.

Lu Yang let out a long breath. Finally, I have established a connection with the Seven Star Sword Set.

He carefully took out the first layer of the Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array. This was a bona fide item of an immortal; it could stir up storms of bloodshed anywhere it appeared and was extremely precious.

“This immortal’s items are also very precious. Why don’t I see you handling them so carefully?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt this was discrimination. An immortal that even Lass Yun could get rid of is obviously of a low caliber. Such stuff does not warrant this level of care and attention.

“So, Immortal Fairy, what have you given me?”

“The Unbeatable Golden Core and the Unbeatable Nascent Soul! Those are great things that make you unbeatable among your peers of the same level! My initial reputation for storming through the ancient era was built upon the Unbeatable Golden Core!

“Go ask around. Which prodigy back then didn’t quail in terror at the sight of this immortal and flee in panic? How many prodigies had their Dao hearts crushed by me...”

Having cultivated to this point, Lu Yang had long achieved the art of multitasking. He listened to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy recount her glorious ancient battle achievements while focusing on cultivating the sword array.

The Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array was an immortal-tier great array. Even the first layer was quite abstruse. Fortunately, Lu Yang possessed a Sword Spirit Root and exceptional talent in Sword Dao; he understood it within an hour. If it were Meng Jingzhou, he wouldn’t grasp anything even after half a month.

The preface of the manual described the creator’s thought process when devising the sword array. Lu Yang read it softly.

“This sword array is a remnant I obtained by chance while traveling the world to seek traces of ancient immortals, desiring to compete with them. The sword array bore stains of immortal blood. Based on the clues, it can be inferred that this is a sword array left behind by an ancient immortal.

“The ancient immortals were truly brilliant, capable of producing such an array. Magnificent! That said, my own talent can rival the ancient immortals’. If an ancient immortal could create such an array, it’s equivalent to me being able to create it. If I were born in the ancient era, I would have been the one to create this sword array.

“As such, this sword array is essentially my creation—only the timing is off.”

Lu Yang, “...”

He really wanted to know which ancient immortal created this sword array. Where is their sense of shame?

At the same time, he found it strange. None of the Four Ancient Immortals seemed to have used a sword; otherwise, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wouldn’t be completely ignorant about the Sword Dao.

Setting his doubts aside for now, Lu Yang continued studying the sword array. Although the sword array’s origin is dubious, its power is genuinely formidable.

“The Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array has requirements for the number of swords—a minimum of two and a maximum of nine. The more swords, the greater the array’s power.”

Before Lu Yang lay nine swords—the Seven Star Sword Set he had just bonded with, the Qingfeng Sword, and the Mingyue Sword.

“Rise!”

With a thought, the swords moved according to his heart. Like stunning swans, the nine swords shot straight up, piercing through the clouds and soaring toward the firmament at extreme speeds. In the blink of an eye, they exceeded Lu Yang’s range of control, and his connection with them was lost.

Lu Yang waited with his head tilted back for a long time. Under gravity’s pull, the nine swords eventually retraced their original path and returned to his control range. The nine swords were aligned in a row, resembling a nine-toothed rake. They descended from the sky and sank into the ground like they were cutting tofu, leaving only the hilts exposed.

Logically, a Nascent Soul sword cultivator shouldn’t be capable of controlling nine swords simultaneously, let alone with such effortless ease. However, Lu Yang’s mental power far surpassed the norm. Along with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s threats to the Seven Star Sword Set and their wish to soak in the Sword-Cleansing Pond again, they allowed Lu Yang and the seven swords to share the same intent. Thus, the Seven Star Sword Set could make the most correct decisions without him exerting effort.

As for the Qingfeng and Mingyue swords, it was needless to say that Lu Yang treasured them immensely. He would rather forget he was a sword cultivator and use spells in battle than employ these two swords.

Such treatment of swords was one of its kind among sword cultivators. The link between Lu Yang and the nine swords enabled his current achievement.

“Array, rise!” Lu Yang uttered softly.

The nine swords resonated, causing the grass beneath his feet to tremble slightly, subdued by the sword qi released. The swords formed a sword array that sealed heaven and earth, and the resulting sword qi was so dense that not even spirit energy could penetrate it.

“Array, move!”

With the Qingfeng Sword as the lead, the nine swords chimed continuously, suspended high in the sky like inverted heavenly sabers ready to cleave all foes. With a single gesture from Lu Yang, the first layer of the Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array was activated, crushing downward with a pressure not inferior to that of an inverted mountain covered with sword tips.

Boom!

Everything beneath the nine swords was annihilated. Even the array’s master, Lu Yang, was awed by its power despite observing from the side.

“Whew, as expected of the Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array!”

Not far away, Gan Tian was consulting Jiang Lianyi about ancient history. Jiang Lianyi had been keeping an eye on Lu Yang’s actions. When she saw him execute the Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array, a peculiar expression crossed her face.

Puzzled, she asked Gan Tian to pause and walked straight over.

After the sword array dissipated, subtle sword qi still lingered in the air. Any Golden Core cultivator present would have been cut.

Lu Yang slumped on the ground, panting heavily. Executing the sword array had drained his mental power and spirit energy. However, the sword array’s power was impressive, far stronger than what he could achieve with only the Qingfeng Sword.

“Senior Lianyi, what brings you here?”

“I couldn’t help but feel that the sword array you performed looked familiar, Senior Brother.”

“Familiar?”

Jiang Lianyi didn’t answer. As she replayed the scene of Lu Yang performing the sword array, realization dawned upon her.

“Isn’t this the sword array my husband knelt on?!”

The Qilin Immortal had often knelt on a sword array. She had become so accustomed to it that she had forgotten that the thing her husband knelt on after misbehaving was a sword array.

Lu Yang asked gingerly, “And that sword array Senior Qilin knelt on, where is it now?”

Jiang Lianyi waved her hand nonchalantly. “I broke it long ago and have no idea where I threw it.”

Chapter 647: Battle of Evenly Matched Opponents

Lu Yang felt conflicted. Should I or should I not continue learning this Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array?

He had just grasped the fundamentals when he heard the terrible news about the sword array’s true origin, which dealt a heavy blow to his enthusiasm to learn.

If I don’t learn it, I have no other sword array to study.

If I learn it, this is the sword array Qilin Immortal used to deceive his wives, and its true power is uncertain.

What if the array’s ultimate function is just to soften the sword tips?

“That won’t happen,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy refuted after hearing Lu Yang’s concerns. “You don’t have to worry about this sword array’s power; it’s very strong. The Qilin Immortal and the Heaven Mandate Immortal only tampered with the immortal swords.”

“Immortal Fairy, you understand sword arrays?”

“By intuition.”

“...Is your intuition reliable?”

“My intuition tells me that my intuition is very reliable.”

Lu Yang fell speechless for a moment before sighing with a sense of resignation. I should just learn it. Regardless of its actual power, in terms of grade, this is undoubtedly the highest-level sword array the Dao-Seeking Sect possesses.

Jiang Lianyi shared the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s view, also believing the sword array’s power was considerable and worth learning.

Lu Yang found Jiang Lianyi’s opinion utterly unconvincing—he had never seen Jiang Lianyi disagree with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Senior Brother, there’s one more thing I need to tell you,” Jiang Lianyi said with a solemn expression.

“What is it?”

“I have stayed in the Dao-Seeking Sect for over two months now and have grasped the basic situation of the current cultivation world. It’s time for me to travel around and search for the Taciturn Daoist Priest and the Phoenix Tribe’s talented junior while I’m at it. I did say I would guide her, and promises must be honored.”

Lu Yang didn’t find it surprising. Jiang Lianyi couldn’t stay in the Dao-Seeking Sect forever and remain by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s side. She had another purpose for leaving, which Lu Yang could guess even if she didn’t state it.

The whereabouts of the Qilin Immortal and Ao Ling.

Jiang Lianyi’s feelings for those two were no less than her feelings for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Senior Lianyi, then I shall wish you a smooth journey. May your wishes come true, and I hope you achieve your goals soon.” Lu Yang cupped his fists and smiled.

Although I exposed Shifu as the author of Dragon Phoenix Transformation, I didn’t tell Senior Lianyi that Big Senior Sister can find Shifu, giving him a longer lease on life.

As a disciple, I’ve shown extreme benevolence and done my utmost.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy also darted out to bid Jiang Lianyi farewell, saying fiercely, “Achieve your goals quickly and come back soon! If anyone bullies you out there, tell this immortal! I’ll have Lass Yun teach them a lesson!”

“Certainly.”

Jiang Lianyi didn’t leave immediately. She waited until Lu Yang’s fifth day of comprehending the sword array and then departed quietly one afternoon.

~~~

Another two days passed. Lu Yang’s mastery of the sword array became more proficient, and his energy consumption decreased significantly.

“I just lack a target to test the sword array’s power on.”

After practicing for so many days, the lawn had been shaved down several layers by the sword array. He found the power formidable, but without an actual test subject for reference, he kept feeling like something was missing.

There are only so many potential targets on Heaven’s Gate Peak. Big Senior Sister is out of the question, and Third Senior Sister is not an option...that leaves that damned puppet...

Recalling that puppet that had been overpowering him since the very beginning of his cultivation, Lu Yang felt he should have no problem with it now.

The most suitable test subject!

No sooner said than done.

Heaven’s Gate Peak wasn’t that large. Lu Yang soon found the puppet digging a hole to plant a tree under a pine tree.

“Hehe, I’ve finally found you. Let’s settle our old and new scores together!”

~~~

A battle of evenly matched opponents began.

Ten breaths into the battle, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul fled in haste.

Twenty-five breaths into the battle, Lu Yang was pummeled black and blue, howling as the iron shovel struck him.

One minute into the battle, Lu Yang was buried in the soil, becoming brothers with the pine tree planted beside him.

The battle ended with a narrow victory by the puppet.

Only after the puppet carried its shovel on its shoulder and staggered out of the pine grove did Lu Yang dare to emerge, his heart still pounding with fear.

“As expected of the puppet that’s been beating me up since I was young. It has some skill. Looks like I’m still not its match at this stage.”

During the fight with the puppet, Lu Yang didn’t even have time to deploy the Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array before the battle concluded. Given Lu Yang’s position at the bottom of the cultivation ladder on Heaven’s Gate Peak, it was truly difficult to find a target to test his sword array on as he pleased.

“Old Lu, are you around?”

Meng Jingzhou’s voice echoed through the pine grove. He had come looking for Lu Yang. The commotion from the earlier battle had caught his attention, and he figured Lu Yang could be here.

Hearing his voice, Lu Yang hurriedly brushed the dirt off his clothes. I can’t give Meng Jingzhou a chance to mock me!

He plucked out the pine twigs stuck to his hair and tidied himself up before replying irritably, pretending as though he had just heard Meng Jingzhou. “Stop shouting! I’m here!”

“The injuries on your face...”

The puppet had shown restraint; the swelling on the face would subside naturally.

Lu Yang remained composed. “It’s nothing. I just ingested a pill, but the medical potency was too strong and hard to digest. Big Senior Sister helped by striking the acupoints on my face to accelerate the absorption.”

Meng Jingzhou eyed Lu Yang suspiciously. I keep feeling like this grandson is spouting nonsense.

“By the way, I’ve just mastered a sword array. Come and give it a try.” Lu Yang hastily diverted Meng Jingzhou’s attention to prevent him from noticing anything amiss.

Besides, isn’t this brat the most suitable target?

“Oh, you’ve started to learn sword arrays? I’d like to see just how powerful your sword array is!”

Sword arrays were a sword cultivator’s trump card. Meng Jingzhou could gauge Lu Yang’s capabilities through it.

“Then you’d better be careful!” Lu Yang knew Meng Jingzhou would agree.

Without standing on ceremony, he flicked his wrists, and nine gleaming swords materialized above Meng Jingzhou’s head, their sharp sword qi causing one’s heart to palpitate.

Meng Jingzhou uttered a command softly and activated Three Heads Six Arms, raising all six arms skyward to block the attack head-on.

“Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array!”

“Holy crap, hold on, what did you say your sword array is called...”

The moment Meng Jingzhou heard the sword array’s name, he had a sense of foreboding. This thing sounds ridiculously powerful!

Before the sword array even descended, Meng Jingzhou, whose six arms were raised to the sky, dropped to his knees with a thud, his posture extremely precise.

Startled, Lu Yang immediately withdrew the sword array and helped Meng Jingzhou up, a delighted expression spreading across his face. “Old Meng, if you wanted me to stop, you didn’t need to perform such a grand bow.”

Meng Jingzhou flared with rage. “Bullshit! Who’s performing a grand bow to you? It was clearly your sword array that forced me to my knees!”

Lu Yang was flummoxed.

Seeing Lu Yang was still playing dumb, Meng Jingzhou cursed furiously, “Don’t play dumb with me! You brat must have done this on purpose! Your sword array has a kneeling effect! When I was standing beneath it, my legs wouldn’t listen to me!”

Lu Yang had never stood beneath the sword array himself and didn’t know it had this effect. He scratched his head. This experiment is really effective, and there is an unexpected gain too.

But why does the Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array have such an effect?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pondered for a moment and figured it out. “I get it!” She explained, “The Qilin Immortal was probably worried his kneeling posture wouldn’t be precise enough to earn Lianyi and Little Ling’s forgiveness, so he added an ‘Automatic Kneeling Array’ to the sword array!

“See, I always said the Qilin Immortal was meticulous. He couldn’t have simply set up an ordinary sword array.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Good thing Senior Lianyi left early. If she had found out about this, it would have spelled disaster.

Chapter 648: Sword Flight

Although making Meng Jingzhou kneel was an immensely satisfying experience, that was not where Lu Yang’s focus lay.

Setting aside the sword array’s offensive power, its forced-kneeling effect was first-rate in utility.

With Meng Jingzhou’s earlier example, even if Meng Jingzhou had assumed a defensive stance, the sudden kneeling would forcefully change his posture and shift his center of gravity, rendering his defense unsustainable and catching him completely off guard.

The upper limit of this move went without saying; the Qilin Immortal had personally tested it. If this move is mastered, it could work even on immortals.

I just don’t know which cultivation levels the first layer of the sword array is effective against. It definitely works on Nascent Soul cultivators, but what about Divine Transfiguration cultivators?

That’s hard to say.

Moreover, the Divine Transfiguration senior brothers and sisters in the sect can’t be treated as ordinary Divine Transfiguration cultivators; they have no reference value.

“Forget it. I’ll find some unlucky Divine Transfiguration cultivator to test it on when I have the time.”

Lu Yang was genuinely grateful to the Qilin Immortal for leaving behind such a peerless sword array. If I get the chance, I must share this good news with Senior Lianyi as a way to repay the Qilin Immortal’s favor of making me eat dirt.

“Come come come, let’s continue!” Lu Yang pulled at Meng Jingzhou, insisting on resuming the unfinished experiment, but Meng Jingzhou adamantly refused.

You must be kidding. I’m not a fool. Kneeling once isn’t enough? You expect me to kneel twice?

Lu Yang conceded. “Alright then, why did you come looking for me?” Based on Meng Jingzhou’s personality, he definitely wouldn’t have sought me out for no reason.

“You know I ran away from home. But I’ve been using the spirit stones my younger sister gave me before she left. If word of this gets out, it will damage this young master’s reputation. I have found a good way to be self-reliant and earn money—making money myself and spending it myself.

“Coincidentally, I learned about a black market in the outside world that regularly holds gatherings for Nascent Soul old monsters. They exchange information, barter goods, and buy treasures there. I plan to go there and make a hefty profit!”

Going alone will be boring—better to drag someone along.

Lu Yang stroked his chin. It sounds like a pretty good place. Although both Meng Jingzhou and I are at the Double Infants Stage, we could be considered Nascent Soul cultivators—we can go.

“Alright.”

Meng Jingzhou smiled and patted Lu Yang’s shoulder. “I knew you’d agree. I’ll go get the old horse.”

Lu Yang grabbed Meng Jingzhou before he could leave. “No need to get the old horse. I’ll take you there.”

Meng Jingzhou was puzzled. “How will you take me there? By flying on a sword?”

Lu Yang revealed a mysterious smile. “Something like that.”

~~~

With the popularization of the flying carriage invented by Lu Yang, more and more cultivators grew fond of this novel transportation artifact. It was safe and reliable; even if a collision happened mid-air, the airbags inside the carriage ensured survival, making it far superior to sword flight in the past.

In the skies, aside from the common flying vessels, the proportion of flying carriages rose year after year. Nevertheless, flying carriages were a novelty and still relatively rare to most cultivators. Occasionally, cultivators would turn their heads, attracted by a flying carriage elegantly gliding past.

But today, a transportation artifact even more eye-catching than a flying carriage flew in the air, causing passengers on flying vessels to glance sideways frequently.

It was a magical treasure about 2.5 meters long, 1.5 meters wide, and 1.5 meters high. With its open-top design and spacious interior, cultivators could stand, squat, or lie down. The grayish-brown exterior appeared subdued yet noble, while the uneven marks on its surface revealed the erosion of time and testified to the artifact’s long history, standing firm despite the wear of passing time.

The Sword-Cleansing Pond carried Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou toward their destination, with the two lying on opposite sides of the pool.

“This is what you call sword flight?”

“Isn’t the scabbard a part of the sword?”

“Yes.”

“Isn’t the scabbard’s function to hold the sword, making it count as a type of vessel?”

“Yes.”

“Isn’t the Sword-Cleansing Pond’s function to hold swords, also making it count as a type of vessel?”

“Yes.”

“Then isn’t the Sword-Cleansing Pond equivalent to a scabbard?”

“Yes.”

“Then isn’t the Sword-Cleansing Pond a part of the sword?”

“Yes.”

“Then isn’t me flying on the Sword-Cleansing Pond essentially sword flight?”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Your logic is impeccable.

“You know what, this really is more comfortable than ordinary sword flight.” Meng Jingzhou conceded Lu Yang’s point. He stretched lazily, feeling so comfortable he wanted to doze off.

Considering public decency, Lu Yang hadn’t filled the pond with water. Bathing in public isn’t very seemly.

A flying vessel passed by. On board, a child holding a female cultivator’s hand pointed at the two older brothers lying in the pool and asked in a childish voice, “Mommy, what kind of magical treasure is that?”

The female cultivator quickly pulled the child into the passenger cabin.

Just as Lu Yang was enjoying the unique mode of sword flight, an official in uniform stopped them. His expression was stern as he raised his right hand, halting the Sword-Cleansing Pond.

“Cease flight.”

“Official, what’s the matter?” Lu Yang stood up from the pond, his face full of bafflement.

Judging by the official’s uniform, he was likely a bureaucrat in the department managing aerial order.

But Lu Yang didn’t understand why he had been stopped.

Are novel magical treasures not allowed in the air?

I don’t think there’s such a rule.

Drunk flying?

But we haven’t been drinking.

“You have exceeded the load capacity.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

“Who is piloting this magical treasure?”

“Me,” Lu Yang said.

“What is your cultivation level?”

“Nascent Soul Stage.”

The official lowered his head to write a violation ticket. “The law stipulates that sword flight may carry only one person. Violators are subject to a base fine of fifty to one hundred spirit stones. For those with higher cultivation levels, the fine increases proportionally. Exceptions apply to special circumstances such as emergencies, danger, or rescues.

“You are at the Nascent Soul Stage, so the fine ranges from five thousand to ten thousand spirit stones. Considering that your attitude is good, according to regulations, the fine is five thousand spirit stones. Any objections?”

“Wait a moment, does this count as sword flight?”

The official nodded, his expression normal. “Isn’t the scabbard a part of the sword?”

“Yes.” freewebnovel.com

“Isn’t the scabbard’s function to hold the sword, making it count as a type of vessel?”

“Yes.”

“This is a Sword-Cleansing Pond, right?”

“Yes.”

“Isn’t the Sword-Cleansing Pond’s function to hold swords, also making it count as a type of vessel?”

“Yes.

“...Alright, Official, no need to continue. I accept the fine.” Lu Yang resigned himself to his bad luck.

I can guess with my butt what the official is going to say next.

“Then sign here.” The official tore off the fine notice to Lu Yang.

“Wait.” Meng Jingzhou stopped Lu Yang.

Five thousand spirit stones wasn’t a huge sum, but Meng Jingzhou felt that since they were out to make money, paying a fine before earning anything was inauspicious. He voluntarily stepped forward to plead for leniency on Lu Yang’s behalf.

“Look, Official, my brother here is flying a sword for the first time and doesn’t know the rules. We’re also disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect. Could you possibly show some leniency?”

Hearing they were Dao-Seeking Sect disciples, the official’s eyes showed surprise, and his attitude noticeably changed. “You’re really from the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

“Why would we lie?” Meng Jingzhou took out his identity jade tablet to prove his identity.

The official took back the ticket, and the two exhaled in relief.

Then, the official wrote a new ticket and handed it to Lu Yang.

“The higher-ups have instructed that fines for Dao-Seeking Sect disciples are to be doubled. The fine is ten thousand spirit stones.”

Chapter 649: Black Market

“But the flying carriage doesn’t count as sword flight?” A flying carriage could carry up to five people, far more than the Sword-Cleansing Pond.

The official shot a glance at Lu Yang and explained, “Flying carriages are specialized flight artifacts. Each one undergoes quality inspection, and the law has special provisions for them. If your Sword-Cleansing Pond also has special provisions, that would be acceptable too.”

Lu Yang admitted defeat.

The two met their end before starting the campaign and lost money before earning any.

Fortunately, no other incidents occurred afterward.

During the several days of flight, the two landed at an inn to avoid camping outdoors. In passing, they helped the lady boss deal with her younger brother-in-law, who brought relatives to claim her husband’s inheritance after his death. The two politely declined the family heirloom the lady boss offered to express her gratitude. Based on clues, they even deduced that the lady boss was her husband’s murderer.

At the second inn, the two ran into two Qi Training cultivators quarreling over the best room. They even obtained information about a nearby treasure site from them and dug up a highly valuable treasure for Foundation Establishment cultivators along the way. After handing it over to the local authorities, a lost-and-found notice was pasted on the announcement board. This attracted two Foundation Establishment clans, unveiling a century-old feud. The family heads of both clans committed suicide in a torrential downpour, drawing the curtain on the hundred-year vendetta.

At the third inn, the two met a young miss from a wealthy family being hunted over a thousand li. They escorted her home, where they discovered and dealt with a malevolent ghost hiding in her house for ten years, forcing the ghost’s master to reveal himself. After a single round of battle, they captured him. The young miss offered herself in marriage out of gratitude, but the two declined. Following clues left by the ghost’s master, they dismantled a diabolic rogue cultivator’s hideout.

Finally, the Sword-Cleansing Pond successfully carried the two to You Province.

~~~

“At last, we’re here.” The two let out a long sigh. Although the journey had only taken a few days, it felt like they had been flying for over a month, their bodies aching all over.

“This pond of yours isn’t very comfortable to lie in.”

“It’s because there’s no water. Bathing in it is actually quite comfortable.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy thought to herself, Isn’t it because you two encountered too many incidents on this journey?

The black market that Meng Jingzhou mentioned was located at the foot of a certain mountain in You Province. It was usually hidden within a secret domain and would undergo spatial displacement during the transition between yin and yang, emerging from the secret domain to provide a venue for trading.

At that time, cultivators from nearby cities would come for secret transactions, along with others like Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou who traveled from farther away.

“We’re just in time. On the fifteenth of every month, Nascent Soul old monsters gather here.”

The two wore black robes with their collars turned up, revealing only their eyes. This was protocol in the black market; it made it easier to flee if authorities came to arrest people.

When they arrived, the black market had been open for over two hours. The cultivators waiting outside had already entered, so the entrance appeared deserted. A cultivator guarded the entrance to prevent mortals from accidentally entering the black market and causing unnecessary trouble.

The guard didn’t stop the two. He had witnessed the two flying on the Sword-Cleansing Pond, storing it away, and changing into black robes. With such practiced and fluid movements, they must be old hands. Anyone capable of piloting such a large pond must at least be a Golden Core cultivator.

Entering the black market, the two found it extremely quiet compared to a normal market, with only the occasional sounds of cultivators speaking. Inside, cultivators here for trade employed methods like concentrating sound into a thread or transmitting auditory messages through spiritual consciousness to ensure the secrecy of transactions.

Without supervision from the authorities, many items never seen in daily life could be found here.

Such as the cultivation manual Lu Yang was holding.

“Boss, are you sure this is the Qi Training chapter of the cultivation technique used by the Dao-Seeking Sect’s prodigy, Lu Yang?”

The vendor assured him with conviction. “How could it be fake? I have a distant relative in the Dao-Seeking Sect. He was the one who brought this cultivation technique out! Young brother, you’re at the Qi Training Stage, right? Why not buy one and try it? I guarantee you’ll soar to great heights and become a genius like Prodigy Lu after cultivating this!”

Without supervision from the authorities, many counterfeits could be found in the black market.

Lu Yang silently put it back. This is too obviously fake.

There were also less blatant fakes, like the one next to it, which was claimed to be the latest edition of the Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Upon taking a closer inspection, one would notice the title was actually Saga of the Doo-Seeking Sect.[1]

Pondering about it, the reason such a book appeared here became clear. Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect was sold everywhere on the streets outside; there was no need to sell it here in the black market. This was meant to scam the unlucky fellows with poor eyesight or those thin-skinned cultivators who were too embarrassed to put something back once they picked it up.

Lu Yang also saw a Purple-Gold Gourd purported to suck in anyone who responded when their name was called. A real Purple-Gold Gourd was worth more than the entire black market combined; even a replica would be a treasure cherished by Divine Transfiguration cultivators. Neither the real thing nor a decent replica would appear here.

Storage rings of various shapes and sizes were correspondingly much cheaper than those outside due to their unknown artifact-refiners and lack of quality assurance. Some storage rings matched their descriptions and were genuine products crafted by untalented artifact-refiners. Others appeared genuine but were actually fakes with limited uses due to errors during the refinement process. Only someone deeply knowledgeable about storage rings could distinguish them.

There were also many talismans for warding off ghosts and evil. These were hard to fake, and counterfeits could easily lead to serious trouble, so the ones sold were genuine. However, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou didn’t need them—a single drop of Meng Jingzhou’s blood was more effective than a stack of talismans. Against ghosts of the same level, Meng Jingzhou’s yang energy was so exuberant that merely emitting his aura could make them dissolve.

As for female cultivators with alluring figures soliciting patrons on the streets, the two completely ignored them.

“Why aren’t there things like souls, eyeballs soaked in potions, and soul-summoning banners?” Lu Yang had strolled halfway through the black market. The atmosphere was as expected—eerie and haunted—but the goods for sale differed significantly from his imagination.

Meng Jingzhou shot his good brother a disdainful look. “The purpose of this black market is tax evasion. What you’re thinking about is a black market of the diabolic path. If I knew the location of those black markets, I’d raid them immediately and claim the reward from the authorities. Why would I still attend some gathering of Nascent Soul cultivators? The moneymaking efficiency would be much higher.”

Lu Yang admitted Meng Jingzhou had a point.

“We’re here. This is the gathering place for us Nascent Soul old monsters.” Meng Jingzhou pointed to a luxurious palace fully coated in black, with statues of rare beasts at the four corners of its eaves. An array blocked spiritual consciousness, and two Golden Core cultivators stood at the entrance.

This was a place he had learned about from Dai Bufan. It’s absolutely reliable.

Lu Yang turned to Meng Jingzhou. “Speaking of which, I haven’t asked, but what is this self-reliant moneymaking method you mentioned?”

“Selling blood.”

Chapter 650: Selling Blood

Lu Yang thought to himself, No wonder you brat insisted on coming to this godforsaken little place where birds don’t even poop. So it’s because you’re here to sell blood.

Spineless.

Aren’t you afraid the Phoenix Tribe will find out and eliminate you as a competitor?

Lu Yang could already envision the scene. When the time comes, I’ll step in and use my status as the Phoenix Ancestor’s senior brother to persuade the Phoenix Tribe to leave him an intact corpse.

“Seniors, please hold on.” The two Golden Core cultivators guarding the palace entrance stopped them politely, wanting to verify their cultivation realms.

Most attendees would present their invitation cards. However, there were also foreign Nascent Soul cultivators without invitation cards, and their cultivation realms needed to be ascertained. Otherwise, if anyone wearing a mask could enter the Nascent Soul great hall, it would become a joke.

“Are you talking to me?” Meng Jingzhou halted, casting a cold glance their way. He let a wisp of his Double Infants Stage aura drift out, intimidating the two.

The two Golden Core guards hurriedly apologized, cold sweat breaking out. They’re definitely Nascent Soul cultivators, at least at the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage!

“We wouldn’t dare. Please enter, seniors.”

As the two entered the main hall, the atmosphere changed abruptly. It was brightly lit, and upon closer inspection, the light was emitted by Mermaid Oil Lamps that burned for a thousand years without extinguishing. These were priceless, originating from the mermaids of the East Sea, a major tribe qualified to attend the Demon Kingdom’s founding ceremony.

The Mermaid Oil Lamps were difficult to refine, and the method was kept a secret, with few privy to it. Given Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s extraordinary statuses, they were aware of the refinement process.

The most challenging part was the material. It required a paunchy mermaid at the Fusion Stage. The fatty flesh from their belly had to be cut off, then a limb regeneration technique had to be applied to heal the wound and regrow the fat. The sliced fat was the raw material for crafting the Mermaid Oil Lamps.

As for why the refinement method was a secret, Lu Yang figured it was probably similar to the Phoenix Tribe’s reasons for selling blood. He didn’t need to dwell on it further.

The center of the main hall displayed over a dozen magical treasures and dozens of medicinal herbs. They were all useful for Nascent Soul cultivators, but they were of no use to Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

There were also many side halls. Judging by their names, some sold information, some provided private meeting spaces for Nascent Soul old monsters, some offered custom pill refinement, and others offered custom artifact refinement...

“That area seems quite crowded. Shall we go take a look?”

In the main hall were several dozen figures in black robes, signifying they were Nascent Soul cultivators. These cultivators were rushing toward one particular side hall—the bartering venue. It seemed to be the customary hour now, and interested Nascent Soul old monsters gathered there to trade.

In the side hall, the Nascent Soul old monsters formed their small cliques.

“Old Monster Pei, I didn’t expect you old fellow to be still alive. When you die, be sure to tell this old woman in advance so that I can head over to offer congratulations,” said an old woman leaning on a cane with a wolf head.

“What a pity then. I’ll definitely outlive you, Granny Xie!” Old Monster Pei’s eyes were weathered and cold, giving others the feeling of being watched by a venomous creature.

Those present here were Nascent Soul old monsters from nearby cities. Even if they deliberately concealed their identities, everyone could roughly guess who they were. As for Old Monster Pei and Granny Xie, their disguises were perfunctory; anyone familiar with them would recognize them at a glance.

The two were famous Advanced Nascent Soul cultivators in the area. They were considered unbeatable here and feared no danger. The Nascent Soul families they founded were also major clans, dominating many industries like metal smelting, textiles, and armed escort services, amassing great wealth. Some even speculated these two were the black market’s true owners, though no one could confirm it.

But Meng Jingzhou could confirm it. The intelligence he received from Dai Bufan was that these two were indeed the black market’s owners, and that their conflict was a facade for outsiders to obscure the truth.

Dai Bufan’s intelligence was always comprehensive and reliable, as long as it didn’t involve Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

“Does anyone have marrow-cleansing and tendon-washing pills or natural treasures? Generous rewards will be given,” a Nascent Soul old monster shouted, seeking treasures to improve a junior’s aptitude.

“Which fellow Daoist has a disciple admission slot for a first-class sect? I’m willing to trade a Nascent Transformation Pill for it.”

“You’d really trade a Nascent Transformation Pill for it?” Another Nascent Soul old monster with the resources was clearly tempted.

The Nascent Soul old monster requesting the trade took out a wooden box sealed with talismans. Wisps of pill fragrance wafted from the box.

“This scent... It’s indeed a Nascent Transformation Pill. I don’t have a first-class sect admission slot, but I have something better.”

“Something better? Could it be an S-class sect?” The old monster holding the pill was astonished.

“No, even higher.”

“The Five Great Immortal Sects?” The old monster with the pill couldn’t remain calm. Since when could admission to the Five Great Immortal Sects be sold? Even if it could be sold, how could a mere Nascent Transformation Pill be sufficient for the trade?

Once you’re admitted to one of the Five Great Immortal Sects, it’s like a carp leaping over the dragon gate. From then on, a bright future will open up, and the vast horizon and sky will stretch before you. Regardless of whether they’re at the Qi Training or Foundation Establishment stage, any disciple from one of the Five Great Immortal Sects will be treated as an equal by us Nascent Soul cultivators here!

“Fellow Daoist, your ambition isn’t bold enough. It’s even higher. This slot I have grants admission to the number one faction under heaven.”

The Nascent Soul old monster with the pill was perplexed. Is there a sect above that?

The nearby Nascent Soul old monsters secretly pricked up their ears. If these two didn’t make a deal, they could step in for the trade instead.

The other party nodded profoundly and said slowly, “The Great Xia imperial palace is recruiting eunuchs. You can enter just by signing up.”

The Nascent Soul old monster with the pill flew into a rage and nearly attacked. Fortunately, he calmed down at the last moment. The black market prohibited violence. Offenders would, at best, be barred from entering the black market forever, or at worst, lose their lives here.

The other party is clearly provoking me on purpose.

Meng Jingzhou mysteriously sidled up to the Nascent Soul old monster, who had just suppressed his wrath, and whispered, “Fellow Daoist, the Dao-Seeking Sect will recruit disciples in six months. The exam questions are already set, and I happen to have the real entrance exam questions. Are you interested?”

“Get lost!”

This obviously sounds like a scam.

“Fellow Daoist, don’t be angry. If you don’t want that, I also have yang-boosting blood that’s more effective than Phoenix blood. Are you interested?”

That Nascent Soul old monster was about to yell “get lost” again, but just as he opened his mouth, he realized he did need something like that. “Is it really more effective than Phoenix blood?”

Currently, only Phoenix Blood Stones soaked in Phoenix blood have yang-boosting properties, but the effects are average, and there is the risk of the Phoenix Tribe finding out. If there is blood more potent than Phoenix blood, that would be perfect.

But which race’s blood could be more effective than Phoenix blood?

Lu Yang snorted coldly, playing the straight man for Meng Jingzhou. “This is the blood of a mighty expert who preserved his virgin boy body. He once entered and exited brothels seven times without faltering, remaining unmoved and free of lust even when women sat on his lap! Even palace eunuchs would praise his willpower and self-restraint! All his yang energy is locked within his blood. How could Phoenix blood, poisonous sacs of lascivious jiao-dragons, or Yin-Yang Blissful Union Flowers compare?!” freewebnovel.com

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Damn it, you might as well not have played the straight man. Why does that make me sound so pitiful?

Chapter 651: Transaction

To be frank, the owner of the Nascent Transformation Pill was tempted. He was already in his twilight years, and coupled with excessive indulgence in his youth, his vitality was depleted; even Phoenix blood couldn’t help. That was why he wanted to carve out a future path for his descendants, hoping they could secure the backing of a major sect.

At the moment, it doesn’t seem like there’s hope to join a major sect. If I could get something to boost my yang and indulge myself in some pleasure instead, that seems fine too.

If my descendants are disappointing, can’t I just make more descendants?

My identity is well concealed; no one should be able to recognize me.

“How much per drop?”

“Ten thousand spirit stones per drop.”

“Words alone can’t be proof. How can I verify the blood’s authenticity?”

Meng Jingzhou chuckled lightly and took out a small porcelain bottle. “What’s difficult about that? This bottle contains one drop of blood. Consume and refine it, and you’ll know its effect.”

Methods in the cultivation world were mysterious and unfathomable. Cultivators of the Curse Lineage could cast curses from afar using blood, hair, and other items, making them nearly impossible to guard against.

This had long crossed Meng Jingzhou’s mind. The blood he brought today had been pre-treated, with all traces of the owner’s identity thoroughly erased.

The Nascent Transformation Pill’s owner took the small porcelain bottle skeptically and poured the blood onto his palm.

The drop of blood resembled a blood-red jade, lustrous and smooth, its origin clearly extraordinary. The yang energy it emitted was nothing to scoff at, evidently much higher than that of Phoenix blood.

This is good stuff.

The surrounding Nascent Soul old monsters watched the drop of blood without blinking, secretly revealing expressions of desire. If it was genuine, they needed to buy a bottle.

After ensuring the blood hadn’t been tampered with, the pill owner swallowed the drop and quietly refined it. freewebnovel.com

There’s a reaction!

The pill owner’s face flushed. The blood’s effect was far stronger than he expected. His body reacted instinctively, and even activating his cultivation technique couldn’t eliminate the desire that coursed through him.

Meng Jingzhou was also somewhat surprised. I didn’t expect my blood’s effect to be so good.

As for being happy...it doesn’t seem like something worth being happy about.

“I’ll buy it!”

“Fifty thousand per drop.”

“You!”

“You can choose not to buy it,” Meng Jingzhou said sagely. The initiative is in my hands; I can sell it for however many spirit stones I wish.

“Fifty thousand it is then! Give me three drops!” the pill owner acquiesced through gritted teeth. This thing can’t be bought even with money; fifty thousand isn’t a loss!

Grinning widely, Meng Jingzhou accepted the storage ring containing 150,000 spirit stones. The money came so fast; it’s enough to pay fifteen fines.

If we hadn’t exposed our Dao-Seeking Sect identity, it could have paid thirty fines!

Lu Yang clicked his tongue in amazement. I’ve seen people borrowing “essence” to pray for children, but this is my first time seeing someone borrowing “blood” to pray for children.

Unfortunately, perhaps the Nascent Soul old monsters were on the cautious side. When they saw the pill owner agree to the trade so readily and the exorbitant price of the yang-boosting blood, they hesitated, and no one else decided to trade.

The two circled the side hall once more. Confirming they couldn’t find other customers, they had to give up.

“Let’s change locations. I know another black market.” Meng Jingzhou transmitted an auditory message. He was meticulous and had inquired about several black markets.

All the information had come from Dai Bufan. The latter’s intelligence wasn’t easily divulged. Thus, Meng Jingzhou had to pay a hefty price for this—he promised Dai Bufan he wouldn’t cause any trouble for the next six months.

The two retraced their steps and left the black market.

Just as Lu Yang was about to take out the Sword-Cleansing Pond for sword flight, an eerie voice came from behind.

“Fellow Daoists, are you leaving already?”

“Who’s there?!” Lu Yang whirled around.

Four Nascent Soul old monsters in black robes emerged from the dense forest, their eyes cold and expressions hostile.

“What are you trying to do?!”

“What we are trying to do?” The leader sneered sinisterly. “Fellow Daoist, you brought out such a precious treasure in the side hall—yang-boosting blood that surpasses Phoenix blood. It made our eyes burn with envy.

“Some things were inconvenient to say in the side hall with so many people around. Now that we have appeared here, you should understand our intentions, fellow Daoists.”

Meng Jingzhou slowly clenched his fists, growing wary. “We are born slow-witted and don’t understand your intentions.”

The leader was unrelenting. “Can you really not make it cheaper? Even Phoenix blood is only twenty or thirty thousand per drop!”

Meng Jingzhou snorted coldly, his attitude firm. “No. I’ve faced countless dangers to obtain this yang-boosting blood. Fifty thousand spirit stones per drop, not a single spirit stone less! If it were you, fellow Daoist, would you lower the price?”

“Is that so? What a pity then. I thought if you were more tactful, we could become friends. Since you’re so heartless...” The leader dragged out his words, seizing the opportunity to signal the other three with his eyes.

The other three individuals reached into their sleeves, and a cold glint flashed before they suddenly threw something at Lu Yang.

Lu Yang had anticipated this. With his large hand, he caught three storage rings.

The leader shook his head regretfully. “Never mind if there’s no discount then. Here is a total of five hundred thousand spirit stones. Please tally the numbers, fellow Daoist.”

Lu Yang scanned them with his spiritual consciousness and accepted the storage rings before giving Meng Jingzhou a meaningful look. “It’s indeed five hundred thousand spirit stones. Deliver the goods.”

Meng Jingzhou took ten bottles of blood from his identity jade tablet and tossed them to the other party.

The leader’s eyes shifted, noticing Meng Jingzhou’s subtle movements in the dark, even spotting his identity jade tablet. “Fellow Daoist, you’re a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

“So what if I am?” Meng Jingzhou cursed inwardly, Oh no, I exposed my identity as a Dao-Seeking Sect disciple.

The leader stared fixedly at Meng Jingzhou and slowly said, “If you are Dao-Seeking Sect disciples, we cannot let you leave so easily. I am also a reputable figure. If word gets out, I’m afraid it would be hard for me to continue mingling in these circles.” A smile spread across his lips. With his back to the moonlight, his expression was cloaked in shadows; only his gleaming, cold teeth were visible.

“What are you trying to do?” Lu Yang sensed the four’s attitudes had changed drastically upon learning their identities.

“Please visit my estate and allow me to show my hospitality as a host!”

Now that we’re aware of their identities, if I don’t entertain them, how would my brothers in the trade view me?

Lu Yang eyed the four vigilantly and shook his head gently. “I think that won’t be necessary.”

Their attitude is strange—they definitely have ulterior motives!

The leader pressed forward step by step. “Fellow Daoist, it’s just taking a seat at my estate. Why be so wary?!”

Lu Yang snickered repeatedly, having already seen through their pretense. He warned them, “Fellow Daoist, Great Xia has ruled for a hundred thousand years. The righteous path is powerful, and the methods of the diabolic and heretical path is not to be pursued. Do you not know how many like you have been arrested by Great Xia and dragged into prison, regretting it for life?!

“As disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect and part of the righteous path, we absolutely will not collude with the diabolic and heretical path. If you’re thinking of pulling strings and going by the back door to get your descendants into the Dao-Seeking Sect, that’s wishful thinking!”

The leader’s eyes were icy. He stealthily reached into his sleeve and touched his storage ring. With a pinch of his fingers, he fanned out several lost cultivation manuals like a folding fan. “Is there really no chance? To be frank, I have substantial family assets and countless secret treasures and ancient texts. Perhaps there is something that might catch your eye, fellow Daoists?”

“No chance!”

Seeing Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s resolute stance, the leader looked up at the sky and heaved a long sigh.

“Never mind, never mind. Let’s go.”
